### [1] [The soft volume of ultra-high energy neutrinos experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13143)
*Stefano Palmisano,Diego Redigolo,Michele Tammaro,Andrea Tesi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个半解析框架，基于玻尔兹曼方程（Boltzmann equation）将超高能中微子通量映射为中微子望远镜中的径迹事件率，通过漂移-扩散方程（drift-diffusion equation）近似处理μ子输运问题，并应用于IceCube和KM3NeT数据，提供了连接中微子通量模型与径迹事件可观测量（track-event observables）的第一性原理桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的中微子望远镜数据分析依赖于完整的蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation），计算代价高且不易直接关联微观物理过程。本文旨在建立一个快速、可控的半解析框架，以第一性原理方式将中微子通量模型映射为径迹事件率，并保留与微观μ子能量损失过程的直接联系。

Method: 基于玻尔兹曼方程描述中微子相互作用产生的次级μ子在介质中的分布；利用软能量损失（soft energy losses）的主导地位，对碰撞算子（collision operator）进行二阶展开，将输运问题简化为能量空间中的漂移-扩散方程，稀有的硬散射（hard scatterings）则作为微扰处理。由此推导出主公式（master formula），并通过对输运系数的理论不确定性进行边缘化（marginalizing）来拟合数据。

Result: 该框架应用于IceCube的贯穿径迹（through-going tracks）数据，得到的弥散通量（diffuse-flux）拟合与实验观测结果兼容。同时，重新评估了KM3NeT报告的超高能径迹事件，检验了其与IceCube在同一能区未见事件的一致性。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个连接中微子通量模型与径迹事件可观测量的第一性原理框架，可快速替代完整蒙特卡洛模拟，对精确中微子天文学（precision neutrino astronomy）及标准模型外新物理的搜索具有直接应用价值。

Abstract: We develop a semi-analytical framework to map ultra-high-energy neutrino fluxes onto event rates at neutrino telescopes. The formulation is based on the Boltzmann equation for the distribution of secondary muons produced by neutrino interactions in matter, and naturally accounts for the effective target volume relevant for through-going tracks. This "soft volume" is controlled by muon propagation and stochastic energy losses, and can be significantly larger than the instrumented detector volume. Exploiting the dominance of soft energy losses, we derive a controlled second-order expansion of the collision operator, reducing the transport problem to a drift-diffusion equation in energy space, with rare hard scatterings treated perturbatively. The resulting master formula provides a fast alternative to full Monte Carlo simulations while retaining a direct connection to the microscopic muon energy-loss processes. We apply the formalism to IceCube through-going muon data, marginalizing over theoretical uncertainties in the transport coefficients, and obtain a diffuse-flux fit compatible with the experimental result. We also revisit the interpretation of the ultra-high-energy track event reported by KM3NeT, assessing its consistency with IceCube non-observation in the same energy range. Our results provide a first-principles bridge between neutrino-flux models and track-event observables, with direct applications to precision neutrino astronomy and searches for physics beyond the Standard Model.

</details>


### [2] [Weak charged current induced electron and positron scattering off proton at JLab and MAMI energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13523)
*A. Fatima,M. Sajjad Athar,S. K. Singh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对电子和正电子与自由质子之间的弱相互作用过程进行了全面的理论研究，涵盖准弹性散射、共振产生、介子产生等多个通道，分析了截面、极化可观测量和自旋不对称性，旨在检验弱相互作用动力学并约束轴矢量耦合参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着JLab和MAMI等高亮度、高精度带电轻子束流设施的发展，中间能区（数百MeV至数GeV）的弱相互作用过程成为研究电弱动力学、核子结构和强子响应函数的重要前沿，亟需系统的理论研究来指导实验探索。

Method: 本文采用理论综述的方法，系统研究了电子和正电子与自由质子间的弱带电-电流相互作用，涵盖奇异数守恒与奇异数改变通道的准弹性散射、$P_{33}$(1232)、$P_{11}$(1440)、$S_{11}$(1535)等共振的非弹性产生，以及$\eta$和$K$介子的产生和奇异粒子的伴随产生过程。

Result: 分析了微分和总截面、末态重子的极化可观测量和质子靶的自旋不对称性，展示了它们对弱相互作用动力学和可能的第二类流（second class currents）的敏感性，并讨论了在准弹性散射区域确定轴向偶极质量（axial dipole mass）的替代方法。

Conclusion: 该研究可实现对G不变性和T不变性的严格检验，为约束弱相互作用的轴矢量扇区（axial vector sector）提供独特且独立的机遇，并能够在不依赖(反)中微子诱导过程固有不确定性的情况下研究$P_{33}$(1232)共振激发的轴矢形状因子。

Abstract: The development of next-generation, high-luminosity, and high-precision charged lepton beam facilities at JLab and MAMI has opened, in recent years, a new frontier in the exploration of weak interaction processes induced by electrons and positrons in the neutral current sector, which can also be used to study weak interaction processes induced by charged currents. In particular, these processes in the intermediate energy regime, spanning from a few hundred MeV to a few GeV, play a crucial role in understanding electroweak dynamics, nucleon structure, and hadronic response functions. This review presents a comprehensive theoretical study of weak charged-current interactions of electrons and positrons with free protons, encompassing quasielastic scattering in both the strangeness conserving and strangeness changing channels, together with inelastic production of the $P_{33}$(1232), $P_{11}$(1440), $S_{11}$(1535) resonances, $η$ and $K$ mesons, and associated production of strange particles. We analyse differential and total cross sections, polarization observables of the final baryons, and spin asymmetries of the proton target, demonstrating their sensitivity to the underlying weak interaction dynamics and to possible second class currents, thereby enabling stringent tests of G- and T- invariance. The explored kinematic region also offers a unique and independent opportunity to constrain the axial vector sector of the weak interaction, and it provides a discussion of alternative ways to determine the axial dipole mass in the quasielastic scattering region, a fundamental parameter that is in debate for nearly two decades. It also focuses on the study of the axial-vector form factors associated with the excitation of the $P_{33}(1232)$ resonance in a manner that is free from the uncertainties inherent in their determination from studies of (anti)neutrino-induced weak processes.

</details>


### [3] [Polarized observables in $τ\to VV ν_τ$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13743)
*Vindhyawasini Prasad,Hiroyuki Umeeda*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用广义隐藏局域对称（generalized hidden local symmetry, GHLS）框架下的螺旋度形式（helicity formalism），系统研究了τ⁻ → V₁⁻ V₂⁰ ν_τ衰变（V₁⁻, V₂⁰为轻矢量介子）中的极化观测量。预言的分支比与有效手征模型（effective chiral model）结果相当，但小于角动量代数模型（angular momentum algebra model）。纵向极化分数f_L在τ质量尺度上对端点极限f_L=1/3（洛伦兹对称性（Lorentz symmetry）的推论）存在不可忽略的修正，未来Belle II实验的测量将为非轻子粲衰变中的极化模式提供关键信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究τ轻子衰变至两个矢量介子（two vector mesons）过程中的极化观测量，以检验不同理论模型（有效手征模型、角动量代数模型）的预言差异，并探索洛伦兹对称性在τ质量尺度上的修正效应。

Method: 采用广义隐藏局域对称（generalized hidden local symmetry, GHLS）框架，结合螺旋度形式（helicity formalism）计算极化观测量。研究涵盖(V₁⁻, V₂⁰) = (ρ⁻, ρ⁰), (ρ⁻, ω), (K^{*-}, ρ⁰), (K^{*-}, ω), (ρ⁻, \bar{K}^{*0})五种衰变道。

Result: 预言的分支比（branching fractions）与有效手征模型结果可比，但小于角动量代数模型。纵向极化分数f_L在τ质量尺度上对端点极限f_L=1/3存在不可忽略的修正。

Conclusion: 未来Belle II实验对τ⁻ → V₁⁻ V₂⁰ ν_τ衰变中f_L的测量，将为非轻子粲衰变（nonleptonic charm decays）中观测到的极化模式提供关键信息。

Abstract: We study polarization observables in $τ^- \to V_1^- V_2^0 ν_τ$ decays for $(V_1^-, V_2^0)=(ρ^-, ρ^0), (ρ^-, ω), (K^{*-}, ρ^0), (K^{*-}, ω), (ρ^-, \bar{K}^{*0})$ using the helicity formalism within the generalized hidden local symmetry framework. The predicted branching fractions are comparable with those from the effective chiral model, but smaller than those from the angular momentum algebra model. Our results for the longitudinal polarization fractions $f_L$ indicate that nonnegligible corrections to the endpoint limit ($f_L = 1/3$), a consequence of Lorentz symmetry, are present at the scale of tau mass. Future measurements of $f_L$ at Belle II for $τ^- \to V_1^- V_2^0 ν_τ$ decays will provide crucial information on polarization patterns observed in nonleptonic charm decays.

</details>


### [4] [High-Energy Neutrinos from Black Hole Evaporation in Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13755)
*Ioannis Dalianis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究中子星内部非对称暗物质引力坍缩形成的微观黑洞产生高能中微子的机制。通过分析暗物质俘获、黑洞形成与霍金蒸发的循环过程，预测了具有特定能谱和空间分布的中微子信号，为连接暗物质、致密天体、黑洞热力学与高能中微子天文学提供了新观测窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非对称暗物质（asymmetric dark matter）在中子星内累积并发生引力坍缩形成微观黑洞后，能否通过霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）产生可观测的高能中微子信号，从而建立暗物质与高能中微子天文学之间的物理联系。

Method: 建立暗物质俘获、黑洞形成与霍金蒸发的重复循环模型，区分由暗物质热化时间（thermalization time）与坍缩循环竞争决定的两种不同 regime（partially thermalized regime 和 fully thermalized regime），计算时间积分的霍金辐射、次级中微子能谱以及银河系和弥漫河外中微子通量。

Result: 预测的中微子信号具有两个特征：一是宽能谱，其谱峰自然高于约 10 TeV，由初始霍金温度（initial Hawking temperature）决定；二是银河系成分强烈集中于银心方向。在有利的微观和天体物理条件下，该信号可能贡献银河系高能中微子观测通量的百分之一水平。

Conclusion: 该机制为通过中子星内部持续产生的微观黑洞观测霍金蒸发提供了新的途径，将暗物质、致密天体、黑洞热力学与高能中微子天文学联系起来，尽管事件率普遍较低。

Abstract: We investigate the production of high-energy neutrinos from microscopic black holes formed through the gravitational collapse of asymmetric dark matter accumulated inside neutron stars. When Hawking evaporation dominates over accretion, long-lived, feebly interacting particles beyond the Standard Model escape the neutron star and subsequently decay into high-energy neutrinos. We analyze the repeated cycle of dark matter capture, black hole formation, and evaporation, identifying two distinct regimes determined by the competition between the dark matter thermalization time and the collapse cycle. In particular, we identify a partially thermalized regime in which the dark matter cloud evolves toward a quasi-stationary state with a temperature significantly exceeding that of the neutron star core. We derive the time-integrated Hawking emission, the resulting secondary neutrino spectra, and the expected Galactic and diffuse extragalactic neutrino fluxes. The predicted signal exhibits two distinctive signatures: a broad neutrino spectrum with a characteristic energy scale set by the initial Hawking temperature of the evaporating black hole, whose spectral peak naturally lies above $\mathcal{O}(10\,{\rm TeV})$, and an extended Galactic component strongly concentrated toward the Galactic Center. Although the predicted event rates are generally small, the resulting signal may contribute at the percent level to the observed Galactic high-energy neutrino flux under favorable microscopic and astrophysical conditions. The proposed mechanism provides a new observational window on Hawking evaporation through microscopic black holes continuously produced inside neutron stars, linking dark matter, compact objects, black hole thermodynamics and high-energy neutrino astronomy.

</details>


### [5] [S-matrix bootstrap bounds on self-interacting dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13141)
*Qing Chen,Zhuo-Hui Wang,Shuang-Yong Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 通过色散原始S矩阵自举方法，基于自相互作用暗物质对低能散射幅度的约束，得到了比分波幺正性更严格的弱耦合标量暗物质质量上限：通用情形约0.3 GeV，赝戈德斯通玻色子情形可降至MeV量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自相互作用暗物质（self-interacting dark matter）将星系暗晕（galactic halos）的结构直接转化为对低能散射幅度的约束，而仅靠分波幺正性（partial-wave unitarity）给出的暗物质质量上限不够强，需要更严格的约束条件。

Method: 利用解析性、交叉对称性、定域性和分波幺正性，在有效场论截断尺度Λ以下假设弱耦合有效场论（EFT），并允许Λ以上的任意紫外（UV）粒子内容，通过色散原始S矩阵自举方法计算允许的最大阈值散射幅度。

Result: 对于基准自相互作用截面σ_self=10^(-24)(M/GeV) cm^2，在受控EFT区域内，通用弱耦合标量暗物质的质量满足M≲0.3 GeV；若暗物质为导数主导的赝戈德斯通玻色子，质量上限取决于M/Λ的层级关系，可降至MeV量级或更低。

Conclusion: 本研究利用色散原始S矩阵自举（dispersive primal S-matrix bootstrap）方法，结合解析性（analyticity）、交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）、定域性（locality）和分波幺正性（partial-wave unitarity），对弱耦合标量暗物质（weakly coupled scalar dark matter）的自相互作用散射幅度施加了比单独分波幺正性更严格的质量约束。对于基准自相互作用截面，通用弱耦合标量暗物质的质量上限约为0.3 GeV；若为导数主导的赝戈德斯通玻色子（pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson），质量上限可降至MeV量级甚至更低。

Abstract: Self-interacting dark matter turns the structure of galactic halos into a direct requirement on a low-energy scattering amplitude. We show that, for weakly coupled scalar dark matter, this requirement implies a much stronger mass bound on the dark matter particle than partial-wave unitarity alone. Using analyticity, crossing symmetry, locality and partial-wave unitarity, we compute the maximal allowed threshold amplitude with a dispersive primal S-matrix bootstrap, assuming only a weakly coupled EFT below a scale $Λ$ and allowing arbitrary UV particle content above $Λ$. For the benchmark self-interaction cross section $σ_{\rm self}=10^{-24}(M/\mathrm{GeV})\mathrm{cm}^2$, the mass of a generic weakly coupled scalar satisfies $M\lesssim 0.3\,\mathrm{GeV}$ in the controlled EFT regime. If dark matter is a derivative-dominated pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson, the mass bound is lowered to the MeV scale or below, depending on the hierarchy $M/Λ$.

</details>


### [6] [$V/H$+Jet Production with the Cambridge/Aachen Algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13962)
*K. Khelifa-Kerfa*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文计算了强子对撞中非全局QCD可观测量（非全局对数，non-global logarithms）的固定阶微扰修正至四阶，重点研究了由Cambrige/Aachen喷注算法（jet algorithm）定义的最高横动量喷注的不变质量分布。结果表明，在固定阶下Cambrige/Aachen算法比anti-k_t和k_t算法更有效地抑制非全局对数，而全阶表现与k_t算法相当；有限N_c修正保持在百分之一水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验不同喷注算法（jet algorithm）对非全局QCD可观测量（non-global QCD observable）微扰结构的影响，特别是明确Cambrige/Aachen算法在固定阶和全阶下对非全局对数（non-global logarithms）的抑制效果。

Method: 采用固定阶微扰计算（fixed-order perturbative calculation）至四圈阶（four-loop order），针对强子-强子对撞（hadron-hadron collisions）中与矢量玻色子（vector boson）或希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）联合产生的最高横动量喷注的不变质量分布，喷注由Cambrige/Aachen顺序重组算法（sequential recombination algorithm）定义。

Result: 固定阶下，Cambrige/Aachen算法比anti-k_t和k_t算法更有效地抑制大非全局对数（large non-global logarithms）；全阶下其表现与k_t算法相当。全阶重求和形状因子（all-orders resummed form factors）的对比显示，有限N_c修正（finite-N_c corrections）保持在百分之一水平（percent level），与已有研究一致。

Conclusion: Cambrige/Aachen喷注算法在固定阶下对非全局对数的抑制具有优势，且全阶行为与k_t算法基本一致，有限N_c修正可忽略。相关工作构成了一个系列研究，系统考察不同喷注算法对非全局可观测量微扰结构的影响。

Abstract: We present fixed-order perturbative calculations up to four-loop order for a generic non-global QCD observable in hadron-hadron collisions. Specifically, we study the invariant-mass distribution of the highest-$p_t$ jet produced in association with a vector boson or a Higgs boson, where jets are defined using the Cambridge/Aachen sequential recombination algorithm. This work is part of a series of papers~\cite{Khelifa-Kerfa:2015mma, Khelifa-Kerfa:2024hwx, Khelifa-Kerfa:2024dut, Khelifa-Kerfa:2025cdn, Khelifa-Kerfa:2024udm, Khelifa-Kerfa:2025jev} examining the impact of various jet algorithms on the perturbative structure of non-global observables across different collision environments. We find that at fixed order the Cambridge/Aachen algorithm suppresses the large non-global logarithms more effectively than the anti-$k_t$ and $k_t$ algorithms, while at all orders it performs comparably to the $k_t$ algorithm. Furthermore, comparisons of all-orders resummed form factors reveal that finite-$N_c$ corrections remain at the percent level, consistent with previous findings.

</details>

# eess.IV [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Efficient Computing for Medical Image Acquisition and Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13204)
*Xiao Wang,Jayasai Rajagopal,Md Safaiat Hossain,Peng Chen,Mohamed Wahib,Enzhi Zhang,Emma J. Reid*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文从统一计算视角综述了CT、MRI、PET和SPECT四种医学成像模态的图像重建，涵盖成像物理、数学模型、解析/迭代/统计重建方法以及高效计算策略（如优化算法、物理感知前向算子、内存高效实现和并行计算），展示了通过融合成像物理、数学建模与高效计算实现精确且可扩展的医学图像重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学成像系统（如CT、MRI、PET、SPECT）不直接获取图像，而是通过测量物理信号并求解逆问题（inverse problem）来重建图像。随着数据集的维度与规模不断增大，图像重建已成为现代医学成像的主要计算瓶颈，亟需统一的计算框架来整合成像物理、数学建模与高效计算。

Method: 本文首先回顾每种模态的成像物理与数据采集过程，推导出统一的广义数学框架；在此基础上讨论解析重建（analytical reconstruction）、迭代优化（iterative optimization）和统计模型重建（statistical model-based reconstruction）方法及其计算特性；最后分析高效计算策略，包括优化算法、物理感知前向算子（physics-aware forward operator）、内存高效实现（memory-efficient implementation）和并行计算（parallel computing）。

Result: 先进的重建方法（解析、迭代与统计模型重建）能够显著提升图像质量，同时降低辐射剂量或扫描时间，但代价是计算成本大幅增加。高效计算因此成为实现临床可行重建时间的关键。

Conclusion: 成像物理、数学建模与高效计算的整合，可实现准确且可扩展的医学图像重建，为解决现代医学成像中的计算瓶颈提供了统一的理论与实践框架。

Abstract: Medical imaging systems such as CT, MRI, PET, and SPECT do not directly acquire images. Instead, they measure physical signals that encode anatomical or physiological information, and image reconstruction recovers the underlying image by solving an inverse problem. Although these imaging modalities are governed by different imaging physics, they share a common computational framework that naturally connects medical physics, linear algebra, probability, numerical optimization, and efficient computing. As medical imaging systems acquire increasingly large and higher-dimensional datasets, image reconstruction has become one of the primary computational bottlenecks in modern medical imaging. Advanced reconstruction methods, including analytical reconstruction, iterative optimization, and statistical model-based reconstruction, substantially improve image quality while reducing radiation dose or scan time, but at significantly increased computational cost. Efficient computing has therefore become essential for achieving clinically practical reconstruction times. This chapter presents a unified computational perspective on medical image acquisition and reconstruction across CT, MRI, PET, and SPECT. It first reviews the imaging physics and data acquisition process for each modality and derives a generalized mathematical framework for image reconstruction. Building on this framework, the chapter discusses analytical, iterative, and statistical reconstruction methods together with their computational characteristics. Finally, it examines efficient computing considerations, including optimization algorithms, physics-aware forward operators, memory-efficient implementations, and parallel computing strategies. Together, these topics demonstrate how the integration of imaging physics, mathematical modeling, and efficient computing enables accurate and scalable medical image reconstruction.

</details>

### [8] [SiMOS quantum-dot spin qubits enabled by extreme-ultraviolet lithography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13121)
*Thomas Van Caekenberghe,Paul Steinacker,Bart Raes,Sofie Beyne,Clement Godfrin,Jacques Van Damme,Sylvain Baudot,Arne Loenders,Gulzat Jaliel,Stefan Kubicek,Johan De Backer,Yannick Hermans,Sugandha Sharma,Shuchi Kaushik,Yuchao Jiang,Yosuke Shimura,Roger Loo,Vukan Levajac,Kristof Moors,George Simion,Florian K. Unseld,Ensar Vahapoglu,Ajit Dash,Tuomo Tanttu,Chris C. Escott,Chih Hwan Yang,Andre Saraiva,Arne Laucht,Wee Han Lim,Nard Dumoulin Stuyck,Massimo Mongillo,Danny Wan,Andrew S. Dzurak,Kristiaan De Greve*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文展示了在300毫米半导体试验线上使用极紫外（EUV）光刻技术制造的高性能硅金属氧化物半导体（SiMOS）自旋量子比特，实现了晶圆级均匀性、亚纳米级栅极尺寸控制，以及高达99.8%的SPAM保真度、99.9%的单量子比特门保真度和99.1%的两量子比特门保真度，验证了EUV光刻作为硅基量子处理器制造技术的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模硅量子处理器的实现需要自旋量子比特（spin qubits）与先进半导体制造技术兼容，并要求光刻工艺兼具纳米级精度和优异的均匀性。尽管目前性能最高的硅自旋量子比特依赖于电子束光刻（electron-beam lithography），但其串行曝光过程限制了可重复性研究和晶圆级（wafer-scale）制造。

Method: 采用极紫外光刻（extreme-ultraviolet lithography, EUV）在300毫米半导体试验线上制造硅金属氧化物半导体（SiMOS）自旋量子比特。通过室温栅极-栅极漏电流产率、临界栅极尺寸的亚纳米级控制以及交换开启特性（exchange turn-on characteristics）评估晶圆级量子点均匀性，并利用门层析成像（gate set tomography, GST）表征四个双量子点系统的保真度。

Result: 实现了100%的室温栅极-栅极漏电流产率和亚纳米级的临界栅极尺寸控制。四个双量子点系统在门层析成像中展现出高度一致的保真度：SPAM保真度高达99.8%，单量子比特门保真度达99.9%，两量子比特门保真度达99.1%。交换开启特性表现为10-13 dec/V，表明EUV图案化实现了优异的制造均匀性。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了EUV光刻（EUV lithography）作为基于高保真度SiMOS自旋量子比特的量子处理器的一种可行制造技术。

Abstract: The realization of large-scale silicon quantum processors requires spin qubits compatible with advanced semiconductor manufacturing technologies, demanding lithographic processes that combine nanometer-scale precision with exceptional uniformity. Although the highest-performing silicon spin qubits demonstrated to date have relied on electron-beam (e-beam) lithography, its serial exposure process limits reproducibility studies and wafer-scale fabrication. Here, we demonstrate high-performance silicon metal-oxide-semiconductor (SiMOS) spin qubits fabricated using extreme-ultraviolet (EUV) lithography in a 300 mm semiconductor pilot line. We report wafer-scale quantum-dot uniformity metrics, including 100 % room-temperature gate-to-gate leakage yield and sub-nanometer control of critical gate dimensions. We characterize four double-dot systems realized in two triple-quantum-dot devices. Gate set tomography (GST) reveals consistently high fidelities across all four systems, with values up to 99.8 % for SPAM, 99.9 % for single-qubit gates, and 99.1 % for two-qubit gates. The devices exhibit highly reproducible exchange turn-on characteristics of 10-13 dec/V, indicating high fabrication uniformity enabled by EUV patterning. These results establish EUV lithography as a viable manufacturing technology for quantum processors based on high-fidelity SiMOS spin qubits.

### [9] [Electronic properties and topological aspects of graphene nanohelicoids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13294)
*Xiaoqian Liu,Arsen Herasymchuk,Yaroslav Zhumagulov,Oleg V. Yazyev*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出石墨烯纳米螺旋体（graphene nanohelicoids），即蜂窝晶格（honeycomb lattice）嵌入螺旋面（helicoidal surface）的几何结构；通过紧束缚近似（tight-binding approximation）构建有效一维晶格模型，发现其能带具有反手征对称性（anti-chiral symmetry），且随宽度和边缘取向变化呈现半导体-金属交替转变、能带间隙周期性闭合与重开，以及Zak相位在平庸与非平庸之间的交替切换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将石墨烯纳米带（graphene nanoribbons）的几何概念推广至螺旋曲面，探索拓扑结构与电子性质之间的新关联。

Method: 从三维螺旋结构出发，构建有效一维晶格模型；采用紧束缚近似（tight-binding approximation）进行系统研究，并推导解析紧束缚模型，引入连续形变（continuous deformation）方法解释相关现象。

Result: 能带结构呈现动量平移的粒子-空穴关系（momentum-shifted particle-hole relation）$E_v(k)=-E_c(k+π)$，反映非对称性对称性（nonsymmorphic symmetry）导致的反手征对称性（anti-chiral symmetry）。随宽度变化，体系在半导体与金属之间交替转变，能带间隙周期性闭合与重开，Zak相位在平庸与非平庸之间交替切换。

Conclusion: 石墨烯纳米螺旋体的带宽依赖性能带反转（band inversion）和交替Zak相位可通过连续形变解析模型得到解释，揭示了该类新型碳纳米结构的拓扑电子性质。

Abstract: We introduce graphene nanohelicoids, geometric analogues of graphene nanoribbons, in which the honeycomb lattice is embedded on a helicoidal surface. Starting from the three-dimensional helical structure, we construct effective one-dimensional lattice models with band structures characterized by a momentum-shifted particle-hole relation $E_v(k)=-E_c(k+π)$ that reflects an anti-chiral symmetry arising from the nonsymmorphic symmetry. A systematic investigation of graphene nanohelicoids using the tight-binding approximation reveals a number of trends upon varying width and edge orientation, for instance, alternating transitions between semiconducting and metallic regimes. As the structure width varies, the band gap periodically closes and reopens, accompanied by an alternating Zak phase that switches between trivial and nontrivial. We derive an analytic tight-binding model and introduce a continuous deformation of the graphene nanohelicoids that explains the origin of width-dependent band inversion and alternating Zak phase.

</details>


### [10] [On-chip quantum sensing of Kondo spins in a high-mobility quasi-one-dimensional nanoconstriction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13397)
*Shun-Tsung Lo,Che-Cheng Wang,Sheng-Chin Ho,Jun-Hao Chang,Ming-Wei Chen,G. L. Creeth,L. W. Smith,Shih-Hsiang Chao,Yu-Chiang Hsieh,Pei-Tzu Wu,Yi-Cheng Wu,Chi-Te Liang,M. Pepper,J. P. Griffiths,I. Farrer,G. A. C. Jones,D. A. Ritchie,Tse-Ming Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 通过在全芯片集成的电子谐振器（ER）与量子点接触（QPC）结构中，实验区分了局域近藤（Kondo）屏蔽态与非局域自旋单态，并揭示了0.7反常（0.7 anomaly）与近藤自旋单态之间的竞争关系，为非侵入式探测开放纳米约束结构中自发磁杂质提供了量子方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近藤（Kondo）自旋在扩展到多个自旋杂质或当局域化自旋本身可能是由开放纳米约束结构（如量子点接触（quantum point contact, QPC））中多体相互作用产生时，其确切性质仍不清楚。实验中难以将近藤态与其他共存的多体自旋态区分开来。

Method: 在高质量GaAs/AlGaAs异质结构晶体管上，通过光刻定义全芯片集成的电子谐振器（electronic resonator, ER）和量子点接触（QPC）。通过调控ER的占据数奇偶性（occupancy parity），控制QPC自旋的局域近藤屏蔽以及ER-QPC集成结构中的非局域自旋单态。

Result: QPC自旋的局域近藤（Kondo）屏蔽与非局域自旋单态均可通过ER占据数奇偶性进行调控。0.7反常（0.7 anomaly）与近藤自旋单态具有不同的物理起源，并且两者之间存在相互抵消的竞争关系。

Conclusion: 这些结果展示了一种非侵入式量子方法，可用于探测开放纳米约束结构（open nanoconstriction）内自发产生的磁性杂质。

Abstract: The precise nature of Kondo spins has remained enigmatic when extended to multiple spin impurities or, more intriguingly, when the localized spin itself may already be the consequence of many-body interactions in a presumably-delocalized open nanoconstriction, such as a quantum point contact (QPC). It is experimentally challenging to distinguish the Kondo state from other coexisting many-body spin states in such a strongly correlated system. Here we lithographically define an all-on-chip electronic resonator (ER) and a QPC in a high-mobility GaAs/AlGaAs heterostructure transistor. Local Kondo screening of the QPC spin and nonlocal spin singlet across the ER-QPC integration are controllable in response to ER occupancy parity. We also show that the 0.7 anomaly, another strongly-correlated state in QPCs, not only has a different physical origin but furthermore counteracts the Kondo spin singlet. These results demonstrate a noninvasive quantum method for sensing spontaneous magnetic impurities within an open nanoconstriction.

### [11] [Emergent induction in magnetic Weyl semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13559)
*Takahiro Anan,Takahiro Morimoto*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上研究了磁性Weyl半金属中由磁动力学驱动的涌现电磁响应，推导了包含带内和带间贡献的磁电响应公式，并应用于极性Weyl铁磁体模型，揭示了环向量子动力学与涌现感应响应之间的密切关系，且发现电感在Weyl色散能量范围内增强，反映了拓扑性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Weyl半金属（Weyl semimetals）中，特别是磁性Weyl半金属中，涌现电磁响应（emergent electromagnetic responses）的理论理解尚不充分，需要建立更一般的理论框架。

Method: 采用磁性Weyl半金属的有效两带模型（effective two-band model），推导了磁电（magnetoelectric, ME）响应公式，该公式同时包含带内贡献（intraband contribution）和带间贡献（interband contribution）。

Result: 带内贡献与弛豫时间τ成正比，而带间贡献与Weyl节点（Weyl nodes）的分离相关。将公式应用于极性Weyl铁磁体（polar Weyl ferromagnets）模型后，发现环向量子（toroidal moment）动力学与涌现感应响应密切相关。电感（inductance）的化学势依赖性表明，涌现电磁响应在Weyl色散能量范围内增强，体现了Weyl半金属的拓扑性质（topological nature）。

Conclusion: Weyl半金属中的磁电响应会通过磁化动力学（magnetization dynamics）介导产生涌现感应，且该响应具有拓扑起源，在Weyl色散能量区间得到显著增强。

Abstract: We theoretically study emergent electromagnetic responses in Weyl semimetals. Focusing on magnetic Weyl semimetals, we develop a general theory of emergent induction driven by magnetic dynamics. We show that magnetoelectric (ME) responses in Weyl semimetals give rise to emergent induction mediated by magnetization dynamics. Using effective two-band models for magnetic Weyl semimetals, we derive a formula for the ME response that includes both intraband and interband contributions. The resulting formula shows that the intraband contribution is proportional to the relaxation time $τ$, whereas the interband contribution is associated with the separation of the Weyl nodes. Applying the general formula to a model of polar Weyl ferromagnets, we demonstrate that the dynamics of the toroidal moment is closely related to the emergent inductive response in polar Weyl ferromagnets, as recently discovered by Suzuki et al. [Y. Suzuki et al. arXiv:2607.12322]. The chemical-potential dependence of the inductance indicates that the emergent electromagnetic response is enhanced in the energy range of the Weyl dispersion, reflecting the topological nature of Weyl semimetals.

</details>


### [12] [Aharonov-Casher-induced electric quadrupole of charge-neutral particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13745)
*Hojun Lee,Youngjae Jeon,Suik Cheon,Hyun-Woo Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文揭示了携带磁矩的电中性粒子在晶体中通过Aharonov-Casher效应与电场梯度耦合，从而表现出电四极矩（AC-EQ），并以磁振子为例在两种磁性体系中计算了该效应的大小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电粒子的轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum, OAM）在固体中已表现为轨道磁化，但电中性粒子的OAM在固体中的物理表现尚不清楚。本文旨在阐明后者通过Aharonov-Casher效应如何产生可观测的电多极矩。

Method: 基于Aharonov-Casher（AC）效应，推导出携带磁矩的电中性粒子与电场梯度的耦合，并引入AC诱导的电四极矩（AC-induced electric quadrupole, AC-EQ）形式，将其分解为标量、环形偶极和约化四极分量。以铁磁烧绿石（Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction, DMI）和螺旋Fe langasite（无DMI）两种体系中的磁振子（magnons）为例，计算AC-EQ的大小。

Result: 在铁磁烧绿石中，DMI诱导出可观的AC-EQ；在螺旋Fe langasite中，即使没有DMI，螺旋自旋构型本身也能产生AC-EQ。两种体系中，单胞积分的AC-EQ分量大小均达到典型核电四极矩的量级。

Conclusion: 电中性粒子可通过AC效应在晶体中表现出电四极矩，这为理解中性粒子角动量的物理表现提供了新途径，并有望在磁性材料中观测到类似核电四极矩的效应。

Abstract: For charged particles, their orbital angular momentum (OAM) in solid have a direct magnetic manifestation as an orbital magnetization. For charge-neutral particles, however, the physical manifestation of the OAM in solid remains unclear. Here, we show that a charge-neutral particle carrying a magnetic moment couples to electric-field gradient through the Aharonov-Casher (AC) effect, thereby exhibiting the electric quadrupole in crystalline solids. This AC-induced electric quadrupole (AC-EQ) contains the scalar, toroidal dipole, and reduced quadrupole components, which are conjugate to the divergence, circulation, and shear of the electric field, respectively. As representative examples, we calculate the AC-EQ of magnons in two magnetic systems. In ferromagnetic pyrochlore, Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (DMI) induces a sizable AC-EQ, whereas in helical Fe langasite the AC-EQ emerges from the helical spin configuration even in the absence of DMI. In both systems, the unit-cell-integrated AC-EQ components reach magnitudes comparable to typical nuclear electric quadrupole moments.

</details>


### [13] [Phonon down-conversion by normal metals for superconducting devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13870)
*Guglielmo La Magna,Gianluigi Catelani*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过动力学方程模型研究超导器件中由对破缺声子（pair-breaking phonons）引起的准粒子中毒（quasiparticle poisoning）机制，并分析利用正常金属薄膜的下转换（down-conversion）过程来缓解该问题的效率。研究发现，在微米量级的金属膜厚度范围内，下转换效率可接近最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导器件（如探测器和量子计算实现）受准粒子中毒效应影响严重，其中对破缺声子是关键中毒机制之一。本文旨在研究通过正常金属薄膜进行声子下转换来缓解该中毒效应的效率及影响因素。

Method: 基于动力学方程（kinetic equations）建立模型，在稳态条件下分别采用解析近似和数值方法求解，从而评估定义的下转换效率（down-conversion efficiency）。

Result: 下转换效率在有限范围的金属膜厚度内接近最优（nearly optimal），最小近优厚度（minimum near-optimal thickness）通常在微米量级。效率依赖于材料参数（如电子-声子相互作用强度、界面声子透射系数）以及薄膜和基底厚度。

Conclusion: 正常金属薄膜的下转换过程能有效缓解超导器件中的对破缺声子中毒问题；通过合理选择膜厚（约微米量级）可在较宽范围内实现接近最优的缓解效率。

Abstract: Thanks to low dissipation, superconducting devices are promising for a number of applications, such as detectors and implementations of quantum computation. However, their working can be adversely impacted by quasiparticles, which is why so-called quasiparticle poisoning mechanisms and their mitigation are under intense investigation. Here we focus on one poisoning mechanism, namely pair-breaking phonons, and its mitigation through down-conversion by a normal-metal film - the process in which scattering of high-energy phonons by electrons lowers the energy of the former below the pair-breaking threshold. To study the down-conversion, we introduce a model based on kinetic equations, which we solve both analytically (approximately) and numerically in the steady state. We use the solution the estimate a properly-defined down-conversion efficiency which depends on material parameters (such as the strength of electron-phonon interaction and the phonon transmission coefficient at interfaces) and film and substrate thicknesses. Interestingly, we find that the efficiency is nearly optimal over a finite range of metal thicknesses, with the minimum near-optimal thickness being typically of the order of a micron.

</details>


### [14] [Realization and manipulation of spiral charge density waves in a two-dimensional metal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13878)
*Lili Zhou,Ruizi Zhang,Chen Si,Zhaoteng Dong,Mengya Ren,Keru Guo,Can Zhang,Jizheng Wu,Fudi Zhou,Huixia Yang,Yaxin Zhao,Guoyuan Yang,Xiaolong Xu,Yuanxiao Ma,Xiao Kong,Yu Zhang,Yeliang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文展示了通过应变（strain）可以解除电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）态的近简并性，并在NbSe₂中实现不同CDW态的空间分离。利用范德华（van der Waals, vdW）相互作用稳定微米级应变网络，使原始3×3 CDW在单轴压缩下转变为孤立单向4×1序，在双轴拉伸下转变为2×2序。其中4×1 CDW具有多带起源且热稳定性显著增强，并在应变网络节点处形成手性螺旋纹理，可通过电压脉冲熔化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近简并的电荷密度波态在集体现象的竞争中扮演核心角色，但在真实材料中这些态常被无序（disorder）所纠缠，阻碍了它们的解缠与控制。因此，需要一种能够解离、稳定并操控这些竞争电子序的方法。

Method: 利用范德华相互作用在NbSe₂中稳定一个微米级的应变网络（strain network），产生空间不均匀的应变场（spatially inhomogeneous strain fields），从而实现对不同CDW态的空间分离。

Result: 原始NbSe₂的本征3×3 CDW超晶格在一维受限压缩（1D-confined compression）下转变为孤立的单向4×1序，在双轴拉伸（biaxial tension）下转变为2×2序。4×1 CDW具有多带起源（multiband origin），热稳定性显著增强，可维持至70 K。在应变网络节点处，进一步形成手性螺旋纹理（chiral spiral textures），且可通过电压脉冲（voltage pulses）熔化。

Conclusion: 应变被确立为一种强有力的方法，可用于解缠、稳定和操控竞争电子序（competing electronic orders）。

Abstract: Nearly degenerate charge-density-wave (CDW) states play a central role in the competition among collective phenomena. In real materials, however, these states are often intertwined by disorder, hindering their disentanglement and control. Here we show that strain can lift this near-degeneracy and spatially separate distinct CDW states in NbSe2. Using van der Waals (vdW) interactions, we stabilize a micron-scale strain network that produces spatially inhomogeneous strain fields. Within this landscape, the intrinsic 3 * 3 CDW superlattice of pristine NbSe2 transforms into an isolated unidirectional 4 * 1 order under 1D-confined compression, and into a 2 * 2 order under biaxial tension. The 4 * 1 CDW has a multiband origin and exhibits markedly enhanced thermal stability, persisting up to 70 K. At strain-network nodes, it further develops into chiral spiral textures, which can be melted by voltage pulses. These results establish strain as a powerful approach to disentangle, stabilize and manipulate competing electronic orders.

</details>


### [15] [Electric field controlled spin transport in a topological insulator interfaced with a ferroelectric antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14031)
*Yogesh Kumar,Pushpendra Gupta,Xinyan Li,Richa Mudgal,Ashish Omar,Ryan Chen,Mito Funatsu,Maya Ramesh,Nicholas Reiterer,Yuanqi Lyu,Yiping Zeng,Darrell G. Schlom,Alessandra Lanzara,Robert J. Birgeneau,James G. Analytis,Ramamoorthy Ramesh,Sajid Husain*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究报告了在拓扑绝缘体 Bi₂Te₃ 与反铁磁多铁材料 BiFeO₃ 构成的界面中，通过电场控制实现自旋-电荷转换（spin-charge conversion）。利用非局域自旋输运器件，观察到自旋输运在 Bi₂Te₃ 厚度大于 10 nm 时保持稳健，低于 5 nm 时消失，归因于拓扑表面态（topological surface states）主导的界面自旋输运及厚度减小导致的平凡绝缘相（trivial insulating phase）转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑绝缘体通过磁性界面实现自旋-电荷互转换已被广泛研究，但在无外加磁场条件下自旋-电荷转换的真实响应尚待澄清，亟需直接且明确的实验证据。

Method: 采用非局域自旋输运器件，在拓扑绝缘体 Bi₂Te₃ 与反铁磁多铁材料 BiFeO₃ 的界面处施加电场，系统测量不同 Bi₂Te₃ 厚度下的自旋输运行为，并结合磁导（magnetoconductance）估算相干因子（coherency factor）以分析界面相变。

Result: Bi₂Te₃ 厚度大于 10 nm 时自旋-电荷转换保持稳健；厚度减小后转换效率迅速下降，至 5 nm 时完全消失。该行为与厚度降低导致的杂化诱导平凡绝缘相（hybridization-induced trivial insulating phase）一致，并由磁导估算的相干因子支持。

Conclusion: 自旋-动量锁定的表面态（spin-momentum-locked surface states）在解耦区域主导界面自旋输运，并在完全绝缘的磁性界面实现高效自旋-电荷互转换。溅射沉积的 Bi₂Te₃ 是高质量、可扩展的量子材料集成平台，非局域自旋输运方法为设计低功耗自旋器件提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Topological insulators have been explored extensively for spin-charge interconversion via magnetic interfaces, yet the true response of their spin-charge conversion, particularly in the absence of an external magnetic field, remains to be studied. Here, we report electric-field control of spin-charge conversion in the topological insulator Bi$_2$Te$_3$ with the antiferromagnetic multiferroic BiFeO$_3$, employing a nonlocal spin transport device. A systematic thickness dependence of the spin transport across the interface between Bi$_2$Te$_3$ and BiFeO$_3$ reveals a signature of topological surface-state-dominated spin transport in the bilayer system. The spin-charge conversion remains robust for thicknesses above 10 nm but falls rapidly with reducing thickness and vanishes at 5 nm. This is consistent with the hybridization-induced emergence of a trivial insulating phase, which is supported by the coherency factor estimated from the magnetoconductance of Bi$_2$Te$_3$. These results establish that spin-momentum-locked surface states dominate interfacial spin transport in the decoupled regime. Beyond presenting efficient spin-charge interconversion at an entirely insulating magnetic interface, this work also highlights sputter-deposited Bi$_2$Te$_3$ as a high-quality and scalable platform for integrating quantum materials into devices. The nonlocal spin transport approach presented here provides a simple and direct evidence of spin-charge conversion and opens an efficient and practical pathway toward designing energy-efficient spin-based devices.

</details>


### [16] [Quantum Transport and Apparent Work Function Distributions of Atomic Contacts via a 3D-Printed High-Vacuum Platform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14074)
*G. Pellicer,C. Sabater*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种低成本、3D打印的高真空平台，集成了机械可控断裂结（break-junction）系统和定制对数放大器，用于室温量子输运测量。以铜为高反应性测试案例，成功在真空和无水甘油中解析出$1G_0$电导量子；以金为稳健基准，从数千条隧穿曲线中提取表观功函数（$φ$），其统计分布严格服从非中心卡方分布（non-central chi-square distribution）。获得的功函数与文献一致，且与考虑原子尺度粗糙度、尖端几何和环境吸附物的理论模型完美吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子输运测量平台在低成本、可及性和对反应性材料的保护方面存在不足，大气氧化严重干扰高反应性金属（如铜）的可靠测量，亟需一种经济、易复制的集成化真空方案。

Method: 采用3D打印技术构建低成本高真空平台，集成机械可控断裂结系统（mechanically controllable break-junction）和定制对数放大器（logarithmic amplifier），在室温下分别以铜（高反应性材料）和金（稳健基准）进行电导量子解析与隧穿功函数统计提取。

Result: 在高真空和无水甘油中成功解析铜的$1G_0$电导量子，证明两种环境均能有效抑制大气氧化。从金的上万条隧穿曲线中提取的表观功函数$φ$严格服从非中心卡方分布（non-central chi-square distribution），且在所有环境条件下与文献值一致，虽低于体块值但完美符合考虑原子尺度粗糙度、尖端几何和环境吸附物的理论模型。

Conclusion: 该方法建立了一种可及且可复现的系统性纳米尺度研究框架，尤其适用于反应性材料的量子输运表征，为低成本、开放式的真空量子测量平台提供了新的可行范式。

Abstract: We present a low-cost, 3D-printed high-vacuum platform integrating a mechanically controllable break-junction system and a custom logarithmic amplifier for room-temperature quantum transport measurements. Using copper as a highly reactive test case, we successfully resolve the $1G_0$ conductance quantum under both high vacuum and anhydrous glycerol, demonstrating the effectiveness of these environments against rapid atmospheric oxidation. In parallel, utilizing gold as a robust benchmark, we systematically extract the apparent work function ($φ$) from thousands of tunneling traces across ambient air, vacuum, and glycerol. Our analysis demonstrates that the statistical distribution of $φ$ rigorously follows a non-central chi-square distribution. The obtained gold work functions match existing literature across all environments. Although lower than bulk values, they perfectly align with theoretical models accounting for atomic-scale roughness, apex geometry, and environmental adsorbates. Ultimately, this methodology establishes an accessible and reproducible framework for systematic nanoscale research on reactive materials.

### [17] [Phase diagram of one-dimensional bosons with Rydberg-dressed soft-core interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13623)
*Shengjie Yu,Laurent Sanchez-Palencia*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究利用精确路径积分量子蒙特卡罗（path-integral quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，系统研究了一维软芯里德伯缀饰（Rydberg-dressed）玻色气体的基态相图，揭示了从常规Tomonaga-Luttinger液体（TLL）到超越TLL区域再到团簇相（cluster phases）的丰富量子相变行为，并在TLL区域中发现了准超固体（quasi-supersolid）相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 里德伯（Rydberg）及里德伯缀饰原子气体最近成为凝聚态物理中多种模型的颇具前景的量子模拟器（quantum simulator），但一维软芯里德伯缀饰相互作用的玻色子系统的完整相图尚待阐明。

Method: 采用精确路径积分量子蒙特卡罗（path-integral quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，对具有软芯里德伯缀饰相互作用的一维玻色子体系进行数值研究。

Result: 相互作用势的有限程（finite-range）和负傅里叶分量（negative Fourier component）在有限动量处产生旋子模（roton mode）；粒子-空穴背散射（particle-hole backscattering）增强了一维系统在二倍费米动量（twice the Fermi momentum）处的响应。相图包含常规TLL区、超越TLL区以及团簇相（commensurate cluster phases）。在TLL区中，体系从Lieb-Liniger类行为（K>1）转变为硬杆类行为（hard-rod-like, K<1），并在K<1/2时出现准超固体（quasi-supersolid）相。

Conclusion: 强相互作用和高密度下出现偏离TLL理论的前驱行为，标志着团簇相（cluster phases）的开始，其中粒子聚集成稳定的多粒子团簇。各相的性质得到了详细讨论。

Abstract: Rydberg and Rydberg-dressed atomic gases have recently emerged as a promising quantum simulator for a variety of models in condensed matter physics. Here we investigate one-dimensional bosons with soft-core Rydberg-dressed interactions using exact path-integral quantum Monte Carlo simulations. The finite-range and the negative Fourier component of the interaction potential generate a roton mode at finite momentum, while particle-hole backscattering processes enhance the susceptibility of one-dimensional systems at twice the Fermi momentum. The competition between the corresponding length scales yields a rich phase diagram, featuring a conventional Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid (TLL) regime, a beyond-TLL regime, and commensurate cluster phases. In the TLL regime, the system transitions from Lieb-Liniger-like bnehavior with Luttinger parameter $K>1$ to hard-rod-like behavior with $K<1$, with a quasi-supersolid phase emerging for $K < 1/2$. For strong interactions and high densities, deviations from TLL theory appear as precursors for the onset of cluster phases, where particles aggregate into stable clusters of several particles. The properties of each phase is discussed in detail.

</details>


### [18] [Momentum Distribution and Contact Parameters of a mass-imbalanced three-body system across the Efimov-Unatomic transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13769)
*D. S. Rosa,R. M. Francisco,T. Frederico,G. Krein,M. T. Yamashita*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了质量不平衡三体系统在临界维度Dc处的单粒子动量分布与接触参数，发现该处存在一种由对数标度结构主导的渐近行为，需引入额外的三体接触参数描述，且该参数敏感地依赖于质量不平衡，可在特定动量尺度下抑制三体贡献，从而建立临界维度作为具有涌现标度性质的新奇体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索空间维度在三维与二维之间调谐时，离散标度不变性（discrete scale invariance）与连续标度不变性（continuous scale invariance）之间转变的临界点（critical dimension Dc）处的物理行为，尤其是质量不平衡三体系统的动量分布与接触参数结构。

Method: 通过解析分析质量不平衡三体系统在临界维度Dc处的单粒子动量分布渐近形式，考察对数标度结构的贡献，引入与二次对数项对应的额外三体接触参数，并分析质量不平衡对该参数的影响。

Result: 在Dc处，动量分布的渐近行为由独特的对数标度结构（logarithmic scaling structure）主导，区别于Efimov态的周期对数行为（log-periodic behavior）与无原子能区的幂律标度（power-law scaling）。需引入一个额外三体接触参数以完成有限且良好的描述；该参数依赖于质量不平衡，在不同质量构型下改变符号，且在全同粒子时为零。三体贡献可在特征动量尺度处被抑制，使渐近尾完全由两体接触决定。Efimov区与无原子区之间存在一个窄的中间标度区（intermediate scaling regime），其范围与性质受质量比强烈控制。

Conclusion: 临界维度展现为具有涌现标度性质（emergent scaling properties）的新奇体系，为实验探测少体量子系统中离散与连续标度不变性之间的转变提供了可观测的特征信号。

Abstract: We investigate the single-particle momentum distribution and contact parameters of mass-imbalanced three-body systems at the critical dimension Dc, where the transition between discrete and continuous scale invariance takes place as the spatial dimension is tuned between three and two dimensions. We show that the asymptotic momentum distribution at Dc is governed by a distinct logarithmic scaling structure, which differs fundamentally from both the log-periodic behavior of Efimov states and the power-law scaling of the unatomic regime. This structure requires the introduction of an additional three-body contact parameter associated with a quadratic logarithmic contribution, leading to a finite and well-defined description of the momentum tail at the transition. This additional three-body parameter depends sensitively on the mass imbalance, changing sign across different mass configurations and vanishing for identical particles. As a consequence, the three-body contribution to the momentum distribution can be suppressed at a characteristic momentum scale, leaving the asymptotic tail entirely determined by the two-body contact. We further analyze the narrow intermediate region connecting the Efimov and unatomic regimes, here identified as an intermediate scaling regime, whose extent and properties are strongly controlled by the mass ratio. These results establish the critical dimension as a regime with emergent scaling properties and provide experimentally accessible signatures for probing the transition between discrete and continuous scale invariance in few-body quantum systems.

</details>


### [19] [Dipolar mixtures in checker-board optical bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13980)
*Rukmani Bai,Luis Santos*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过二阶微扰理论与团簇-古茨威勒计算相结合的方法，研究了置于反幻零波长（anti-magic wavelength）分离双层结构中的二元偶极混合物，揭示了两种组分之间丰富的晶体相图，并发现晶格间跳跃（inter-site hopping）可通过超交换（super-exchange）机制诱导不同晶体相之间的固态-固态转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超冷偶极混合物在分量相关光势阱中能同时呈现组分内与组分间的各向异性长程相互作用，但二元体系在受限几何结构中的晶体相行为及其转变机制尚未被充分阐明。

Method: 采用二阶微扰理论（second-order perturbation theory）与团簇-古茨威勒计算（cluster-Gutzwiller calculations）相结合的理论方法，对置于反幻零波长位移双层结构中的二元偶极混合物进行建模分析。

Result: 揭示了两种组分可能存在的丰富晶体相（crystalline phases）；发现晶格间跳跃可通过超交换（super-exchange）机制驱动不同晶体相之间的固态-固态转变（solid-into-solid transitions）。

Conclusion: 这些晶体相及其相变可通过镧系元素混合物（lanthanide mixtures）在光学晶格（optical lattices）中实现实验验证，为研究各向异性长程相互作用与超交换效应提供了可控平台。

Abstract: Ultra-cold dipolar mixtures in component-dependent optical potentials constitute an interesting platform for the study of the interplay between intra- and inter-component anisotropic long-range interactions. We study the particular case of binary dipolar mixtures placed in separated bilayers which are displaced in an anti-magic wavelength configuration. Using a combination of second-order perturbation theory and cluster-Gutzwiller calculations, we unveil a rich landscape of possible crystalline phases for the two components, showing that, interestingly, inter-site hopping may result, via super-exchange, in solid-into-solid transitions between different crystalline phases. These crystalline phases and the corresponding transitions can be experimentally realized using e.g. lanthanide mixtures in optical lattices.

### [20] [A Showcase of Using the Partial-Structure R1 to Assemble Small-Molecule Crystal Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13836)
*Xiaodong Zhang*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过具体实例展示了利用部分结构R1因子（partial-structure R1, pR1）组装小分子晶体结构的方法与策略，包括从含重原子的片段开始组装、仅优化取向的便捷性，以及必须使用残余衍射强度（residual reflection intensities）来处理轻原子片段方向问题，表明pR1是一种有效的小分子晶体结构解析工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索并展示部分结构R1因子（partial-structure R1, pR1）在小分子晶体结构组装中的具体应用策略与可行性，为晶体结构解析提供一种实用的工具和操作指导。

Method: 通过若干具体实例，演示了使用pR1组装小分子晶体结构的几种策略：从含重原子的大片段或小片段开始进行取向和/或放置；仅需优化片段取向即可将其连接到部分模型（partial model）上；对于只含轻原子的片段，需从实测衍射强度中扣除含全部重原子的部分模型贡献，得到残余衍射强度（residual reflection intensities）后间接计算其取向。

Result: pR1方法能够有效启动和推进小分子晶体结构的组装流程，尤其是在处理含重原子的体系时，可从大片段或含重原子的小片段入手；轻原子片段的取向无法直接计算，必须依赖残余衍射强度来求解。

Conclusion: pR1是解析小分子晶体结构的一个有用工具，能够帮助解决部分结构模型搭建中的关键问题。

Abstract: Using a few concrete examples this paper has demonstrated a few observations on using the partial-structure R1 (pR1) to assemble small-molecule crystal structures. (1) Assembling can start with orienting and/or placing large fragments or small fragments containing heavy atom(s). (2) It is handy to attach a fragment to a partial model as only the orientation needs to be optimized. (3) In a structure containing heavy atoms it is impossible to directly calculate the orientations of a light-atom-only fragment. Instead, it is necessary to use residual reflection intensities in which the contribution of the partial model containing all heavy atoms is deducted away. These observations indicate that pR1 is a useful tool for solving some small-molecule crystal structures.

</details>

### [21] [Radiation effects on surface and bulk properties of ATLAS18 silicon sensors under low- and high-dose gamma irradiation and annealing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13932)
*Marcela Mikestikova,Vitaliy Fadeyev,Pavla Federicova,Petr Gallus,Jana Kozakova,Jiri Kroll,Magdalena Kutova,Jiri Kvasnicka,Igor Mandic,Pavel Tuma,Miguel Ullan,Yoshinobu Unno,Iveta Zatocilova*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了ATLAS18硅条传感器在HL-LHC ATLAS ITk探测器早期运行阶段（0.5–100 krad）至超高剂量（数百Mrad）伽马辐照下的表面与体效应，并结合退火实验分析了辐照损伤的热稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ATLAS Inner Tracker (ITk)的硅条传感器需承受高达1.6E15 1 MeV n_eq/cm²的注量和66 Mrad的总电离剂量（TID），现有辐射硬化n+-in-p技术已满足要求，但伽马辐照对表面和体效应的综合影响及退火行为尚需系统研究。

Method: 使用$^{60}$Co伽马源对ATLAS18生产晶圆上的分段微型条传感器（minis）和未分段MD8二极管进行低剂量（0.5–100 krad）和超高剂量（数百Mrad）辐照，测量总电流、体电流、表面漏电流和电容-电压（capacitance-voltage）曲线以提取全耗尽电压（full depletion voltage），并通过等时退火（80–300°C）和等温退火（60°C & 160°C）研究缺陷热稳定性。

Result: 低剂量区（0.5–100 krad）对应ITk早期运行相位，超高剂量（数百Mrad）远超ATLAS ITk要求；退火实验揭示了表面和体相关伽马诱导缺陷的热演化行为。

Conclusion: 低剂量与超高剂量辐照的联合分析为ATLAS18硅传感器中表面和体相关的伽马诱导效应及其热演化提供了全面描述。

Abstract: Silicon strip detectors for the ATLAS Inner Tracker (ITk) at the HL-LHC must withstand harsh radiation conditions, including fluences of up to 1.6E15 1 MeV n$_{eq}$/cm$^{2}$ and total ionizing doses (TID) of up to 66 Mrad. These requirements are met using radiation-hard n+-in-p technology implemented in the ATLAS18 silicon strip sensors currently under production. This work presents a combined study of gamma-irradiation effects in ATLAS18 silicon sensors, including both segmented miniature strip sensors (minis) and unsegmented MD8 diodes fabricated on ATLAS18 production wafers. The samples were irradiated with a $^{60}$Co gamma source to multiple low TIDs between 0.5 and 100 krad, corresponding to the dose range relevant for the early operational phase of the ITk tracker. Additional measurements extending up to a few Mrad were performed to investigate the saturation of surface related damage effects. Post-irradiation characterization included measurements of total, bulk, and surface leakage currents, as well as capacitance-voltage measurements used to extract the full depletion voltage. The thermal stability of radiation-induced defects was studied using isochronal annealing between 80°C and 300°C and isothermal annealing at 60°C and 160°C. In addition, complementary studies of MD8 diodes irradiated to ultra-high doses of several hundred Mrad, well beyond the ATLAS ITk requirements, are included to investigate possible bulk-related effects induced by pure gamma irradiation and their annealing behavior. The combined analysis of low- and ultra-high-dose irradiation provides a comprehensive picture of surface- and bulk-related gamma-induced effects in ATLAS18 silicon sensors and their thermal evolution.

</details>

### [22] [Exactly Solvable Diffraction-Grating Scattering Problems for TE and TM waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13287)
*Farhang Loran,Ali Mostafazadeh*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文展示了Berry于1998年提出的解析可解光栅（grating）属于一个更大的可精确求解的衍射光栅族，并利用非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）的动力学框架，在傍轴近似（paraxial approximation）之外，给出了TE波和TM波衍射束振幅的显式解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Berry（1998）针对一类特定势函数给出了原子衍射光栅的解析解，但其结果依赖傍轴近似（paraxial approximation）。本文旨在将该光栅推广到更广泛的、可精确求解的磁性或非磁性衍射光栅族，并突破傍轴近似的限制。

Method: 采用一种基于将定态散射问题映射到有效非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）生成的量子动力学的动力学表述，推导出TE和TM两种偏振状态下衍射束振幅的显式解析表达式。

Result: 证明了Berry光栅属于一个更大的可精确求解的衍射光栅族；给出了在傍轴近似之外有效的TE和TM波衍射束振幅的显式解析表达式；以Berry光栅的推广形式为例，给出了TE和TM波散射问题的精确解。

Conclusion: 本文建立的动力学框架能够统一处理更广类别的可解衍射光栅，并得到超越傍轴近似的精确解析结果。

Abstract: In J.~Phys.~A {\bf 31}, 3493 (1998), Berry provides an analytic solution of the problem of determining the diffracted beam intensities for atoms incident upon a grating given by the potential, $v(x,y):=iV_0(e^{i\mathfrak{K}\,y}-1)$ for $0\leq x\leq\ell$ and $v(x,y):=0$ otherwise, where $V_0, \mathfrak{K}$, and $\ell$ are positive real parameters. This result, which relies on the paraxial approximation, readily applies to the diffraction of transverse electric (TE) waves by the nonmagnetic optical grating given by the relative permittivity, $\hat\varepsilon(x,y):=1-v(x,y)/k^2$, where $k$ is the incident wavenumber. We show that Berry's grating belongs to a larger class of possibly magnetic diffraction gratings whose scattering problem for both TE and transverse magnetic (TM) waves are exactly solvable. Our analysis makes use of a recently developed dynamical formulation of stationary scattering that is based on the idea of mapping the scattering problem to the quantum dynamics generated by an effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonian operator. {We use this formulation to derive explicit analytic expressions for the diffracted beam amplitudes that are valid beyond paraxial approximation.} As a concrete example, we offer the exact solution of the scattering problem for TE and TM waves incident upon a generalization of Berry's grating.

</details>


### [23] [Symmetry-Informed Deep Learning for Electromagnetic Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12810)
*Viktor A. Lilja,Philippe Tassin*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出利用电磁散射问题中的对称性（symmetry）——基于麦克斯韦方程组的等变性（equivariance）——来提升深度学习代理模型的数据效率，通过系统数据增强和构建等变神经网络，在光子晶体板和自由衍射光栅上实现数量级的数据效率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习可加速电磁器件建模，但训练数据通常依赖昂贵的数值仿真，数据效率（data efficiency）低是核心瓶颈。本文旨在通过对称性这一尚未充分利用的途径克服该局限。

Method: 利用麦克斯韦方程组（Maxwell’s equations）的等变性导出通用变换规则，将电磁器件的对称性映射为散射参数（scattering parameters）的相应变换，据此实现系统数据增强（data augmentation）和精确等变神经网络（equivariant neural networks）的构建，并同时在离散和连续对称群上实施该框架。

Result: 在光子晶体板（photonic-crystal slabs）和自由衍射光栅（free-form diffraction gratings）上，引入对称性使数据效率相比标准架构提升一个数量级；等变模型还能精确强制物理约束。

Conclusion: 该方法具有通用性，与现有物理信息策略互补，为构建物理自洽的代理模型提供了第一性原理框架，并将对称性确立为计算电磁学（computational electromagnetics）及更广领域中数据高效且物理一致的统一归纳偏置（inductive bias）。

Abstract: Deep learning can accelerate the modeling of electromagnetic devices by replacing costly simulations with neural networks trained to map design parameters to scattering parameters. However, data efficiency remains a central bottleneck, as training data is typically generated through expensive numerical simulations. Here we show that symmetry provides a powerful and largely untapped route to overcoming this limitation in electromagnetic scattering problems. Leveraging the equivariance of Maxwell's equations, we obtain general transformation rules that map symmetries of electromagnetic devices to corresponding transformations of their scattering parameters. This enables both systematic data augmentation and the construction of exactly equivariant neural networks. We implement the framework for both discrete and continuous symmetry groups and demonstrate its effectiveness on photonic-crystal slabs and free-form diffraction gratings. Incorporating symmetry improves data efficiency by an order of magnitude compared to standard architectures, while equivariant models additionally enforce physical constraints exactly. Our approach is general and complementary to existing physics-informed strategies, provides a first-principles framework for constructing physically grounded surrogate models, and establishes symmetry as a unifying inductive bias for data-efficient and physically consistent learning in computational electromagnetics and beyond.

### [24] [Towards stealthy hyperuniform networks with optimal isotropic complete photonic band gaps using a novel inverse design procedure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13199)
*Joel Steinegger,Paul J. Steinhardt,Christoph Räth,Salvatore Torquato,Michael A. Klatt*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 提出一种两阶段逆向设计流程，用于构建二维无序隐身超均匀三价光子网络，实现了各向同性完全光子带隙（PBG），其带宽比此前最宽的各向同性完全PBG宽近一个数量级，且在大规模系综中具有高度均匀性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序系统随尺寸增大通常无法维持完全光子带隙（complete photonic band gap, PBG），而现有通过映射隐身超均匀（stealthy hyperuniform）点图案生成的三价网络虽然能保持带隙开启，但带隙较窄，原因在于TE与TM模带隙重叠有限以及局域缺陷态导致的宽带尾。因此，需要一种新的设计方法使网络本身成为隐身超均匀两相介质，以拓宽并优化完全PBG。

Method: 采用两阶段逆向设计流程（two-stage inverse design procedure），目标是使最终网络自身实现隐身超均匀性（stealthy hyperuniformity），从而优化TE与TM带隙的重叠并降低带边缺陷态密度。设计结果可通过增材制造（additive manufacturing）实现。

Result: 所得网络不仅实现了单个大带隙的构型，而且在大规模系综（有效探测含100,000个顶点的网络）中表现出显著的同质性。该系综级带隙宽度与具有相同网络参数的各向异性蜂窝光子晶体（honeycomb photonic crystal）的完全PBG相当，且比此前最宽的各向同性完全PBG宽近一个数量级。

Conclusion: 该两阶段逆向设计流程能够生成具有创纪录带宽的各向同性完全光子带隙的无序隐身超均匀光子网络，为利用增材制造技术调控电磁波提供了新途径。

Abstract: We present a two-stage inverse design procedure for producing disordered stealthy hyperuniform trivalent photonic networks in two dimensions with isotropic complete photonic band gaps (PBGs) blocking light regardless of direction or polarization (TE or TM) over a wide frequency range. Most ordinary disordered systems fail to maintain complete PBGs as system size increases. The only known exceptions that remain open in the largest simulations have been generated by mapping stealthy hyperuniform point patterns into trivalent networks. However, the resulting networks are not truly stealthy hyperuniform two-phase media. Although their PBGs remain open, they are relatively narrow due to limited overlap between the TE and TM band gaps and broad band tails caused by localized defect states. By contrast, our two-stage inverse design aims to make the final network itself stealthy hyperuniform, achieving unprecedented near-optimal overlap between the TE and TM band gaps and a small defect state density at the band edges. We obtain not only single realizations with large PBGs, but a striking homogeneity across a large ensemble, effectively probing a network with 100,000 vertices. This ensemble-based band gap is comparable in width to the complete PBG of an anisotropic honeycomb photonic crystal with the same network parameters and nearly an order of magnitude wider than the previously widest known isotropic complete PBGs. Our designs can be fabricated using additive manufacturing, offering new pathways to manipulate electromagnetic waves for photonic technologies.

### [25] [Imprinting topology on thermal light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13542)
*Tianle Chen,Kelsey Everts,Andrew Forbes,Yungui Ma*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文首次证明，热光（thermal light）可以通过空间工程携带斯格明子（Skyrmions）形式的光学拓扑（optical topologies）。这种拓扑结构对时间平均退相干（time-averaged decoherence）具有免疫性，作者利用这一特性，通过超表面（metasurface）设计从热光源实现了非相干拓扑（incoherent topologies）的生成。实验测量的斯格明子验证了方法的可行性，模拟表明超表面中的相干性管理（coherence management）可进一步增强功能。该工作报道了首个纯热光拓扑结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往光场的拓扑结构化（topological structuring）必须依赖光学相干性（optical coherence）来确保空间相位得以保持，这要求使用高相干性光源或在设计中嵌入相干性工程（coherence engineering）。本研究的动机是探索是否可以在热光这种低相干性的日常光源中实现和利用光学拓扑结构。

Method: 作者利用拓扑结构对时间平均退相干具有免疫性的特性，反向设计了一种超表面（metasurface）介导的方案，从热光源直接生成非相干拓扑结构。实验测量了生成的斯格明子拓扑态，并结合模拟分析了超表面设计中相干性管理对功能增强的作用。

Result: 实验测量表明生成的斯格明子具有良好的拓扑纯度（pristine nature），验证了该方法的可行性。模拟结果显示，通过在超表面设计中引入相干性管理可以进一步增强拓扑功能。此外，生成阶段继承了拓扑的鲁棒性（robustness），对材料和制造缺陷不敏感。

Conclusion: 该工作首次在纯热光中实现了光学拓扑结构，为在无处不在的日常光源中利用拓扑特性开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Topological structuring of light inevitably leverages on optical coherence to ensure that the imparted spatial phases are preserved, requiring highly coherent sources or coherence engineering embedded in the design. Now we show that thermal light can be spatially engineered to carry optical topologies in the form of Skyrmions. Such topologies are immune to time averaged decoherence, a fact we leverage on in reverse to create metasurface mediated incoherent topologies from a thermal source. The pristine nature of our measured Skyrmions validates the approach, while simulations reveal how coherence management in the metasurface design would further enhance the functionality. Remarkably, the generation stage inherits robustness from the topology, remaining immune to material and fabrication defects. Our work reports the first topologies from purely thermal light, opening a path to exploiting topology in ubiquitous everyday light sources.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用永久磁铁阵列在磁性石榴石薄膜上形成磁性全息图，构建菲涅耳波带片（Fresnel zone plate）图案；通过施加外部磁场脉冲，可逆切换透镜的聚焦状态；同时优化磁场施加系统以提升开关速度。

Conclusion: 磁光效应的本征响应可达皮秒（picosecond）量级，表明开关速度仍有进一步提升空间；该工作作为超快主动透镜的概念验证，为未来超高速光学元件提供了新路径。

Abstract: Active lenses based on metasurfaces have been demonstrated across broad applications, and their response speeds remain limited to the microsecond range. Here we report the experimental demonstration of a magneto-optical (MO) active lens based on a magnetic hologram formed on a magnetic garnet film. A Fresnel zone plate pattern was created using an array of permanent magnets, focusing a 633 nm laser beam of 12.5 mm diameter to a spot size of 0.7 mm at a focal length of 3.1 m with a modulation depth of ~91%. The focusing state was reversibly switched by applying an external magnetic field pulse. Through optimization of the magnetic field application system, a switching speed of 10.8 $μ$s was achieved, surpassing the operating speeds of conventional active lenses. The intrinsic picosecond-scale response of the MO effect indicates that further improvement in switching speed is achievable, establishing this work as a proof-of-concept for ultra-fast active lenses.

### [27] [When is the combined load identifiable from a stress-intensity profile? A coupled forward-inverse study on SIFBench finite-element data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13074)
*Giansalvo Cirrincione,Filippo Grassia*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文基于SIFBench有限元数据，研究从裂纹前沿应力强度因子（stress intensity factor, SIF）剖面反演裂纹所受拉、弯、承三种载荷相对大小的逆问题。核心贡献并非现场载荷恢复，而是严格刻画联合载荷可辨识性（identifiability）的条件，并提供一个在不可辨识区域仍能输出校准不确定性的估计器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在断裂力学中，裂纹前沿的应力强度因子（SIF）剖面可反映所承受的载荷分布，但不同载荷组合可能产生几乎相同的SIF剖面，导致逆问题病态（ill-posed）。现有方法缺乏对可辨识性条件的严格刻画，且未能定量处理不可辨识时的不确定性。

Method: 利用已知几何下载荷到SIF剖面的精确线性正映射（forward map），将可辨识性问题简化为三种基本载荷剖面沿裂纹前沿是否线性独立。提出一个受单纯形约束（simplex-constrained）的集值逆估计器（set-valued inverse estimator），其裂纹前沿算子（crack-front operator）兼具结构化正代理模型和可微映射功能。

Result: 在SIFBench角裂纹（corner-crack）场景中，数值实验与理论一致：典型几何下问题适定（well-posed），相当一部分几何确实病态（ill-posed），因此点估计（point estimate）在多数情况下可靠，在不可辨识情形下则明确无信息。验证基于受控合成噪声，未使用真实断裂案例。

Conclusion: 逆问题的病态程度由内在稳定裕度（intrinsic stability margin）控制，而非单纯的条件数（conditioning number）。所提估计器能在可辨识时给出可靠点估计，在不可辨识时仍输出经校准的不确定性，从而统一处理适定与病态情形。

Abstract: This work studies the inverse problem of recovering the relative magnitudes of the tension, bending, and bearing loads acting on a crack from its stress-intensity-factor profile along the crack front, using the public SIFBench finite-element data. The central claim is not forensic load recovery on field cases, but a rigorous characterization of when the combined load is identifiable at all, together with an estimator that returns calibrated uncertainty precisely in the regimes where it is not. For a known geometry the forward map from loads to profile is exactly linear, and identifiability reduces to a single geometric question: whether the three elementary load profiles are linearly independent as functions along the front. When they are nearly dependent, many different load combinations produce almost the same profile and the inverse problem is illposed; the analysis shows that the degree of ill-posedness is controlled by an intrinsic stability margin, not by the conditioning number alone. A single crack-front operator serves both as a structured forward surrogate and as the differentiable map required by a simplex-constrained, set-valued inverse estimator. On the SIFBench corner-crack scenario the empirical behaviour matches the theory: the typical geometry is well posed while a sizable minority is genuinely ill-posed, so a point estimate is reliable on the majority and provably uninformative on the rest. Validation is on controlled synthetic noise; no real fracture cases are used or claimed.

</details>


### [28] [Tensor-Network Finite Elements for Analytic Operator Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13129)
*Abhijatmedhi Chotrattanapituk,Michael J. Landry,Chu-Liang Fu,Mingda Li*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出一个连接有限元方法（finite-element method）与张量网络（tensor network）的统一框架，将算子方程（operator equations）离散化为由多线性相互作用张量构成的代数系统，并将求解转化为张量网络自由度上的加权残差优化问题。一维线性和非线性扩散问题的矩阵乘积态（matrix-product-state）计算表明，该方法能以可控误差保持连续性及纽曼边界条件（Neumann boundary condition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限元方法（finite-element method）离散连续算子方程，张量网络（tensor network）提供离散系统的变分表示，但二者之间缺乏直接的数学联系。作者希望建立一套统一的变分语言，将微分、积分、非线性、记忆和延迟方程纳入同一种代数结构，从而为基于张量网络和量子启发方法求解算子方程提供通用基础。

Method: 该方法的核心在于：有限元离散化诱导出一组多线性相互作用张量（multilinear interaction tensors），使得微分、积分、非线性、记忆和延迟方程均能用该公共代数结构表达；随后将所得系统重新表述为张量网络自由度上的加权残差优化问题（weighted-residual optimization problem）。

Result: 针对一维线性和非线性扩散方程，采用矩阵乘积态（matrix-product state, MPS）计算能够重现常规数值解，同时以可控误差保持连续性（continuity）和纽曼边界条件（Neumann boundary condition）。

Conclusion: 该框架为解析算子方程提供了统一的变分语言，建立了有限元数值形式与张量网络变分算法之间的直接联系，为张量网络基础和量子启发方法求解算子方程奠定了通用基础。

Abstract: Operator equations (OEs) underpin quantitative modeling across science and engineering. Finite-element (FE) methods discretize continuous OEs into finite-dimensional algebraic systems, whereas tensor networks (TNs) provide flexible variational representations of correlated discrete systems. Here, we develop a framework that connects FE with TN for analytic OEs. The power of this method comes from its ability to convert highly non-linear partial differential equations into linear matrix equations. In particular, we show that FE discretization induces a hierarchy of multilinear interaction tensors, through which differential, integral, nonlinear, memory, and delay equations can be expressed within a common algebraic structure. The resulting systems are reformulated as weighted-residual optimization problems over TN degrees of freedom. Matrix-product-state calculations for one-dimensional linear and nonlinear diffusion reproduce conventional solutions with controlled error while preserving continuity and Neumann boundary conditions. The framework provides a common variational language for analytic OEs and establishes a direct connection between FE numerical formalism and TN variational algorithms, offering a general foundation for TN-based and quantum-inspired approaches to solving OEs.

</details>

### [29] [DeepCormack: Fermi surface tomography using model-based data-driven algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13107)
*Georg F. B. Lovric,Bryn Drury,Carola-Bibiane Schönlieb,Stephen B. Dugdale,Ander Biguri*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出DeepCormack，一种将监督式深度学习模型（CNN、MLP、UNet）与Cormack方法相结合的数据驱动重建算法，用于从正电子湮灭角关联测量（ACAR）数据中重建三维双光子动量密度（TPMD）。该方法利用奇异值分解与动态模态分解生成逼真的合成训练数据，仅需单个DFT参考动量密度。在测试数据上，DeepCormack在2亿计数下比标准方法提升约8.5 dB PSNR，并能在更低计数下保持稳定，将原本数月的采集时间缩短至数周量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于正电子湮灭角关联测量（angular correlation of electron-positron annihilation radiation, ACAR）的三维双光子动量密度（two-photon momentum density, TPMD）重建是研究材料费米面（Fermi surface）的重要方法，不受低温、超高真空或强磁场的限制，并能研究自旋分辨的电子结构。然而，该问题是一个具有挑战性的逆问题（inverse problem）：标准重建方法（modified Cormack method, MCM）因信噪比低，获取可用于费米面研究的足够数据需要数月时间。因此，亟需一种能显著提升重建质量或加速数据采集的方法。

Method: 提出了DeepCormack，一系列基于模型的数据驱动重建算法，在MCM的不同阶段集成监督式深度学习模型（CNN、MLP、UNet）。为克服缺乏大规模实验训练集的困难，提出利用奇异值分解（singular value decomposition）与动态模态分解（dynamic mode decomposition）生成逼真的合成TPDM体积数据，仅需一个通过密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算的参考动量密度即可生成训练数据。

Result: 在测试数据上，DeepCormack在2亿计数（200M counts）下将重建质量较MCM提升约8.5 dB PSNR，且在更低计数下仍保持稳定，从而显著缩短采集时间。该方法对实验数据的泛化能力强烈依赖于训练分布与目标样本的匹配程度。

Conclusion: 建议将DeepCormack与目标材料的DFT计算配对使用，以生成样本特定的训练数据。该方法可提供质量更高的重建，或将原本需要数月的采集时间缩短至数周量级。

Abstract: The experimental reconstruction of the 3D two-photon momentum density (TPMD) via angular correlation of electron-positron annihilation radiation (ACAR) is a particularly useful method for studying material Fermi surfaces. It does not rely on low temperatures, UHV conditions, or strong magnetic fields, and enables the study of the spin-resolved electronic structure of materials. Yet, it remains a challenging inverse problem. Typically, 10^8 positron annihilation events are measured for 3--6 projections of the TPMD at different angles. The standard reconstruction approach is an ACAR adaptation of Cormack's method (the MCM) that leverages the inherent symmetry in the crystal's structure. However, the poor signal-to-noise ratio means collecting data of sufficient quality for Fermi surface studies can take months per sample. We present DeepCormack, a family of data-driven model-based reconstruction algorithms that augments the MCM by integrating supervised deep-learning models (CNN, MLP, and UNet) at various stages. To overcome the lack of large experimental training sets, we propose a method which leverages singular value decomposition with dynamic mode decomposition to generate realistic synthetic TPMD volumes, requiring only a single reference momentum density computed via density functional theory. On test data, DeepCormack improves reconstruction quality over MCM by about 8.5 dB PSNR at 200M counts and remains stable at reduced counts, enabling significantly faster acquisition times. Generalisation to experimental data depends strongly on how well the training distribution from the reference momentum density matches the sample. We therefore recommend pairing DeepCormack with a DFT calculation of the target material to create sample-specific training data. Our proposed method offers either much higher quality reconstructions, or enables significantly faster ones, on the order of weeks.

</details>


### [30] [Synthesis of the Elusive Bulk Iodide Double-Perovskite Semiconductor, Cs2AgBiI6: Microcrystals and Photoconductive Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13180)
*Faris Horani,Nicolas Nguyen,Carmelita Ro-Mendez,Nicholas J. Adams,Daniel R. Gamelin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文首次报道了三维碘化物双钙钛矿 Cs₂AgBiI₆ 的体相合成，包括微晶和薄膜两种形式，并首次展示了其光电导测量结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维碘化物双钙钛矿（3D iodide double-perovskite）半导体因其作为太阳能应用中潜在的无铅金属卤化物吸收层而受到关注，但此前主要局限于理论计算，合成上几乎不可行，原因在于其预测的热力学不稳定性（thermodynamic instability）。本工作旨在突破这一合成瓶颈。

Method: 首先制备相纯的 Cs₂AgBiBr₆ 微晶（microcrystalline），再通过阴离子交换（anion exchange）合成体相 Cs₂AgBiI₆ 微晶粉末；识别并消除体相 Cs₂AgBiBr₆ 中的痕量水分是实现完全卤素交换及分离相纯 Cs₂AgBiI₆ 的关键因素。进一步采用闪蒸热蒸发（flash thermal evaporation）制备 Cs₂AgBiBr₆ 薄膜，再经阴离子交换获得相纯 Cs₂AgBiI₆ 薄膜。

Result: 合成的 Cs₂AgBiI₆ 在可见光区具有宽吸收，光学带隙（optical bandgap）为 1.70 ± 0.05 eV，近红外光致发光（photoluminescence）中心位于 1.03 eV。在惰性气氛中，微晶 Cs₂AgBiI₆ 在室温储存数月或加热至约 70 °C 时均未发生分解，在干燥空气中同样稳定。薄膜样品的电导测量（photoconductivity measurements）首次证实了该材料中的光生载流子产生与输运。

Conclusion: 本研究成功实现了此前被认为热力学不稳定、难以合成的三维碘化物双钙钛矿 Cs₂AgBiI₆ 的体相合成与薄膜制备，并首次完成了其光电性能测量，为无铅卤化物钙钛矿太阳能材料的研究开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Three-dimensional (3D) iodide double-perovskite (elpasolite) semiconductors have attracted interest as potential lead-free metal-halide absorber layers for solar applications. Although studied extensively by computational methods, they have remained largely inaccessible synthetically, consistent with their predicted thermodynamic instability. Here, we report the first synthesis of bulk Cs2AgBiI6, demonstrating both microcrystalline and thin-film forms. Microcrystalline powders of Cs2AgBiI6 were prepared via anion exchange from phase-pure Cs2AgBiBr6 microcrystals. The resulting iodide elpasolite shows broad absorption throughout the visible with a 1.70 +/- 0.05 eV optical bandgap and near-infrared photoluminescence centered at 1.03 eV. We identify the elimination of trace moisture in bulk Cs2AgBiBr6 as the critical factor enabling complete halide exchange and isolation of bulk Cs2AgBiI6 with phase purity. In inert atmosphere, microcrystalline Cs2AgBiI6 shows no decomposition when stored for months at room temperature or heated to ~70 °C, and it appears equally stable in dry air. Building upon these insights, we then demonstrate the preparation of phase-pure Cs2AgBiI6 films by flash thermal evaporation of Cs2AgBiBr6 followed by anion exchange. Photoconductivity measurements on such Cs2AgBiI6 films demonstrate photocarrier generation and transport, marking the first optoelectronic measurement on this elusive 3D iodide double perovskite.

### [31] [Multiwavelength Raman investigation of mono- and few-layer MoS2 grown by Pulsed Laser Deposition on SiO2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13211)

Abstract: Molybdenum disulfide (MoS$_2$) is a semiconductor whose vibrational and excitonic properties are highly sensitive to layer number and structural disorder. We demonstrate the growth of MoS$_2$ monolayers on inert, electronics-compatible SiO$_2$ substrates using room-temperature pulsed laser deposition (PLD). Control of the process parameters enables tuning from monolayer to multilayer films, which we investigate by multiwavelength Raman spectroscopy. The evolution of the Raman-shift difference between the $E_{2g}^{1}$ and $A_{1g}$ modes, combined with an assessment of defect density, tracks film growth as a function of the number of deposition laser pulses. Although excitonic effects strongly influence the optical response of two-dimensional transition-metal dichalcogenides, experimental reports of symmetry-selective exciton-phonon coupling remain limited. We provide experimental evidence of symmetry-dependent exciton-phonon coupling in PLD-grown monolayer MoS$_2$. Specifically, we observe modulation of the resonant behaviour of the out-of-plane $A_{1g}$ and in-plane $E_{2g}^{1}$ modes, related to their different coupling to A excitons, predominantly derived from Mo $d_{z^2}$ orbitals, and C excitons, characterized by mixed orbital contributions from Mo $d_{z^2}$ and S $p_x$ and $p_y$ states. Comparison with mechanically exfoliated monolayers reveals the role of growth-induced defects in modulating these interactions. These findings establish room-temperature PLD as a viable approach for growing two-dimensional MoS$_2$ on inert, electronics-compatible substrates and provide insight into the interplay between excitonic resonances and growth-induced disorder in two-dimensional MoS$_2$.

Conclusion: 这些观测结果支持随机场模型（random-field model），即PNRs从顺电基体（paraelectric matrix）中涌现，其生长和集体相互作用受CORs相关的随机局域场（random local fields）约束。

Abstract: Polar nanoregions (PNRs) are central to understanding the exceptional dielectric and piezoelectric properties of relaxor ferroelectrics and are key to advancing dielectrics for high-energy storage. However, direct real-space imaging of their formation and evolution remains a major challenge in condensed matter physics. Here, we report the real-space mappings of both PNRs and chemically ordered regions (CORs) in the prototypical relaxor Pb(Mg1/3Nb2/3)O3 and their temperature dependence using convergent-beam electron diffraction (CBED) combined with four-dimensional scanning transmission electron microscopy (4D-STEM). The results reveal that CORs, with sizes of 2-5 nm, remain static with temperature and act to suppress PNR growth. In contrast, PNRs evolve from isolated 2-5 nm regions at room temperature to interconnected structures ~10 nm in size at low temperatures, indicative of a percolation transition. These observations support the random-field model, in which PNRs emerge from a paraelectric matrix and their growth and collective interactions are constrained by random local fields associated with CORs.

### [33] [Resistivity in Dilute Cu-3d Alloys Governed by Disorder-Induced Band Broadening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13419)
*Kenji Yamaguchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，研究室温下稀Cu-3d过渡金属合金的电阻率机制。结果表明，只有在无序局域磁矩（disordered local moment, DLM）框架下才能复现实验趋势；电阻率与费米面上Bloch谱函数（Bloch spectral function, BSF）的半高宽（full width at half maximum, FWHM）强相关，遵循共同的幂律标度关系，揭示电阻率由动量空间中的无序诱导能带展宽主导，而非局域态密度效应，从而为Cu基合金中Linde规则的失效提供了统一的微观解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解室温下稀Cu-3d过渡金属合金的电阻率机制，该温区与大多数实际应用相关，且不同于此前理论工作关注的低温近藤屏蔽（Kondo-screened）区间；同时解释实验中观察到的Linde规则为何在这些合金中失效。

Method: 采用基于Korringa–Kohn–Rostoker相干势近似（coherent potential approximation, CPA）并结合Kubo–Greenwood形式论的第一性原理计算；顺磁态通过无序局域磁矩（DLM）框架描述，对应于局域矩顺磁体而非Pauli顺磁体。

Result: 仅在DLM描述下能复现实验观察到的电阻率趋势，而非磁和铁磁状态均无法捕捉正确的元素依赖关系；电阻率与费米面上BSF的FWHM呈现强相关性，并在不同磁态间表现出共同的幂律标度关系。

Conclusion: 电阻率由动量空间中的无序诱导能带展宽（即源于散射率的寿命展宽）主导，而非由费米能级处的局域态密度（density of states）效应决定，为Cu基合金中Linde规则的失效提供了统一的微观解释。

Abstract: The mechanism governing the resistivity in dilute Cu-3d transition-metal alloys at ambient temperature -- the regime relevant to most practical applications and distinct from the low-temperature, Kondo-screened regime addressed by earlier theoretical work -- is investigated using first-principles calculations based on the Korringa--Kohn--Rostoker coherent potential approximation combined with the Kubo--Greenwood formalism. The paramagnetic state is described within the disordered local moment (DLM) framework, corresponding to a local-moment paramagnet rather than a Pauli paramagnet. We show that the experimentally observed resistivity trends are reproduced only within the DLM description, while nonmagnetic and ferromagnetic states fail to capture the correct element dependence. Contrary to conventional interpretations based on the density of states at the Fermi level, the resistivity exhibits a strong correlation with the full width at half maximum (FWHM) of the Bloch spectral function (BSF) on the Fermi surface. This correlation reflects the disorder-induced lifetime broadening of electronic states, directly related to the scattering rate that governs electrical resistivity. A common power-law scaling between resistivity and BSF broadening is identified across different magnetic states. These results demonstrate that the resistivity is governed by disorder-induced band broadening in momentum space rather than by local density-of-states effects, providing a unified microscopic interpretation of the breakdown of Linde's rule in Cu-based alloys.

### [34] [Physics-Informed Residual Deep Learning for Constitutive Modeling of Hot Deformation and Dynamic Recrystallization in a Mo-Rich $α+β$ Titanium Alloy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13467)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究开发了两种堆叠残差物理信息神经网络（Stacked Residual Physics-Informed Neural Networks, STAR-PINNs）：Enhanced STAR-PINN引入热机械本构约束，DRX-Aware STAR-PINN采用双输出架构并整合了JMAK-Avrami正则化、DRX饱和约束及可调参数Arrhenius一致性约束，通过自动微分（automatic differentiation）施加物理信息约束，并利用潜在特征融合（latent-feature fusion）将预测的DRX分数直接关联到应力输出。

Result: DRX-Aware STAR-PINN取得了RMSE = 11.69 MPa、MAE = 4.83 MPa、R² = 0.9850的性能，交叉验证RMSE为12.47 ± 0.26 MPa。该模型准确再现了温度相关的流变曲线、DRX动力学和Zener-Hollomon关系，同时保持了物理一致的本构行为。

Conclusion: 物理信息深度学习（physics-informed deep learning）为本构建模提供了鲁棒且可解释的框架，为钛合金先进工艺建模提供了实用方法。

Abstract: Accurate constitutive modeling of hot deformation behavior is essential for designing thermomechanical processes in advanced structural alloys. Conventional Arrhenius-type and empirical models do not adequately capture the combined effects of strain hardening, dynamic recovery (DRV), and dynamic recrystallization (DRX) across broad processing conditions. In this study, two Stacked Residual Physics-Informed Neural Networks (STAR-PINNs) were developed to simulate the hot deformation response of a Mo-rich $α+β$ titanium alloy (Ti-6Al-4Mo-1V-0.1Si). The Enhanced STAR-PINN incorporated thermomechanical constitutive constraints, while the DRX-Aware STAR-PINN employed a dual-output architecture to account for recrystallization kinetics. Both models used a shared residual encoder trained on experimental flow stress data collected at temperatures from 800 to 1050 degrees C and strain rates between 0.01 and 10 per second. Physics-informed constraints, including thermal softening, strain-rate sensitivity, strain hardening, and post-peak softening, were enforced through automatic differentiation. The DRX-Aware model further integrated JMAK-Avrami regularization, DRX saturation constraints, and Arrhenius-based consistency with tunable parameters, directly linking the predicted DRX fraction to stress output via latent-feature fusion. The DRX-Aware STAR-PINN achieved RMSE = 11.69 MPa, MAE = 4.83 MPa, R^2 = 0.9850, and a cross-validated RMSE of 12.47 +/- 0.26 MPa. This model accurately reproduced temperature-dependent flow curves, DRX kinetics, and Zener-Hollomon relationships, while maintaining physically consistent constitutive behavior. These results demonstrate that physics-informed deep learning provides a robust and interpretable framework for constitutive modeling, offering a practical approach for advanced process modeling of titanium alloys.

### [35] [Hybridization-controlled re-entrant electronic phase switching and moire-confined states in twisted bilayer PtTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13529)
*Seoung-Hun Kang,Jeonghwan Ahn,Young-Kyun Kwon*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭转范德华双层（twisted van der Waals bilayer）不仅改变莫尔周期（moiré periodicity），还会改变局部堆叠（local stacking）和层间杂化（interlayer hybridization）。摘要旨在揭示扭转双层PtTe₂中电子能隙随扭转角度的演化行为及其微观机制。

Method: 采用全弛豫第一性原理计算（fully relaxed first-principles calculations），并包含自旋-轨道耦合（spin–orbit coupling）、能带展开（band unfolding）以及布里渊区积分态密度（Brillouin-zone-integrated densities of states）分析。
