Conclusion: 层间杂化的重新分布（redistribution of interlayer hybridization）是扭转双层PtTe₂中重返式能隙演化（re-entrant gap evolution）的微观起源。

Abstract: Twisting a van der Waals bilayer changes not only the moiré periodicity but also the local stacking and interlayer hybridization. Here, we show, using fully relaxed first-principles calculations including spin--orbit coupling, band unfolding, and Brillouin-zone-integrated densities of states, that bilayer PtTe$_2$ exhibits a non-monotonic evolution between gapless and gapped electronic regimes. The $7.34^\circ$ structure remains gapless, whereas finite direct gaps appear at the sampled intermediate angles. The gap closes at the sampled $60^\circ$ configuration and reopens at higher angles. The direct gap shows an overall increase with the minimum local interlayer Pt--Pt separation, although the complete distribution of local stacking environments is required to account for deviations from this trend. At $7.34^\circ$, the low-energy states are concentrated predominantly in the AA-like regions of the otherwise gapless moiré cell. Controlled interlayer-separation scans show that increasing the layer spacing removes the near-$E_F$ crossings and opens a gap, consistent with weakened interlayer Te-$p_z$ hybridization. These results identify the redistribution of interlayer hybridization as the microscopic origin of the re-entrant gap evolution in twisted bilayer PtTe$_2$.

### [36] [Rotation topological states: theory and material realization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13575)
*Chun-Xue Liu,Yilin Han,Runze Li,Yulong Liu,Zhi-Ming Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于旋转对称性（rotational symmetry）的 $\mathbb{Z}_2^n$ 拓扑不变量（topological invariant），用于揭示传统 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 不变量无法检测的隐藏在旋转子空间中的拓扑态，并以 CsCl 体材料为例，通过第一性原理计算和对称性分析，证实了其存在非平庸的 $\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ 和 $\mathbb{Z}_2^4$ 不变量，分别导致双外尔点（double Weyl points）出现在 (111) 和 (001) 表面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的拓扑材料表征依赖于从全部占据能带计算拓扑不变量，但该方法在材料具有旋转对称性时可能遗漏隐藏在旋转子空间中的拓扑态。本文旨在填补这一诊断缺陷。

Method: 作者将占据的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）按不同旋转本征值（rotation eigenvalues）分解为多个子空间，定义了一种新的 $\mathbb{Z}_2^n$ 拓扑不变量（其中 $n$ 为子空间数量），并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和对称性分析（symmetry analysis）对体材料 CsCl 进行验证。

Result: 研究发现，时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）将共轭旋转本征值配对，使两个子空间具有相同的 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 不变量，导致拓扑性质对传统的全局不变量始终“隐藏”。在 CsCl 中，传统方法将其判定为拓扑平庸，而本文方法揭示其沿 Γ-R 路径存在非平庸 $\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ 不变量，沿 Γ-Z 和 M-R 路径存在非平庸 $\mathbb{Z}_2^4$ 不变量，分别产生 (111) 和 (001) 表面上的双外尔点。

Conclusion: 本文提出的子空间 $\mathbb{Z}_2^n$ 不变量为对称性保护的拓扑相（symmetry-protected topological phases）提供了必要的精细化诊断，将有助于识别大量被现有方法忽略的拓扑态。

Abstract: The conventional characterization of topological materials relies on topological invariants calculated from the entire set of occupied bands. However, when a system possesses rotational symmetry, the occupied Hilbert space can be decomposed into multiple subspaces labeled by distinct rotation eigenvalues. We show that this decomposition reveals hidden topological states characterized by a novel $\mathbb{Z}_2^n$ topological invariant, where $n$ is the number of subspaces, while the conventional $\mathbb{Z}_2$ invariant may fail to detect the topology hidden in the rotation subspaces. Remarkably, time-reversal symmetry pairs conjugate rotation eigenvalues and guarantees that the two subspaces have the same $\mathbb{Z}_2$ invariants, making the topology always hidden from the conventional global invariant. We formulate the theory of rotation-subspace topology and demonstrate its material realization in bulk CsCl. Using first-principles calculations and symmetry analysis, we show that bulk CsCl, which is diagnosed as topologically trivial by the conventional approach, features a nontrivial $\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ invariant along the $Γ$-R path and a nontrivial $\mathbb{Z}_2^4$ invariant along the $Γ$-Z and M-R paths, leading to double Weyl points on the (111) and (001) surfaces, respectively. The subspace $\mathbb{Z}_2^n$ invariant proposed here serves as a necessary refinement for symmetry-protected topological phases and will facilitate the identification of a large class of topological states overlooked by existing diagnostics.

</details>


### [37] [Research progress in high-pressure tuning of layered magnetic materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13632)
*Yue Dongdong,Gao Xin,Mu Congpu,Liu Zhongyuan,Zhai Kun*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文系统介绍了三类原位高压实验方法：金刚石对顶砧（diamond anvil cell）结合X射线与光谱技术、高压磁输运测量，以及新兴的NV中心量子传感（NV-center quantum sensing）技术。

Abstract: Two-dimensional van der Waals materials have enormous potential applications in many fields due to their unique layered structure and excellent properties. Compared with three-dimensional bulk materials, layered systems are coupled by weak van der Waals interactions between layers, endowing them with much higher structural compressibility, particularly along the interlayer direction, which is more sensitive to external pressure. High pressure can expand the accessible phase space, enabling the synthesis of new materials or the retention of metastable phases. On the microscopic level, pressure can significantly tune the interlayer structure and interactions, induce changes in the electronic structure, and consequently give rise to a variety of rich physical properties. This article systematically introduces in situ high-pressure experimental approaches, including diamond anvil cells combined with X-ray and spectroscopic techniques, high-pressure magnetic transport measurements, and emerging NV-center quantum sensing. It further reviews representative pressure-induced phenomena and underlying tuning mechanisms in layered magnetic materials, such as high-spin to low-spin transitions of transition-metal ions and the accompanying structural phase transitions and superconductivity; substantial enhancement of the Curie temperature and continuous switching of magnetocrystalline anisotropy; and antiferromagnetic-to-ferromagnetic transitions achieved by modulating exchange interactions or via stacking engineering. Finally, we discuss future directions, including synergistic multi-field control by combining pressure with electric fields and twisted heterostructures, as well as strategies such as pressure quenching to retain high-pressure metastable magnetic phases at ambient conditions.

### [38] [Role of small-radius and high-electronegativity A-Site dopants in enhancing proton transport and stability of perovskite electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13657)
*Hang Ma,Ying Liang,Tianxing Ma*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）并结合机理分析（mechanistic analysis），系统研究Ca掺杂BaCeO₃的电子结构、离子键合、缺陷形成及表面吸附行为。

Abstract: The practical application of BaCeO$_3$-based electrolytes is limited by their poor chemical stability in proton-conducting solid oxide fuel cells. Commonly employed B-site doping strategies typically improve proton transport with limited improvement in stability. Recent experiments show that A-site Ca doping can simultaneously enhance both properties. Here, through first-principles calculations and mechanistic analysis of Ca-doped BaCeO$_3$, we identify the synergistic roles of small-radius, high-electronegativity A-site dopants in governing proton transport and chemical stability in perovskite electrolytes. We show that the higher electronegativity of A-site dopant weakens the A-O ionic bonding, facilitating oxygen-vacancy formation and enhancing proton uptake by increasing the basicity. This weakened A-O interaction also suppresses the formation of impurity phases and reduces the adsorption strength of acidic gases such as CO$_2$ and SO$_2$. The lattice contraction induced by the smaller ionic radius improves thermal stability and can enhance proton diffusion in systems where proton transfer is the rate-limiting step. Furthermore, we find that Ca surface segregation can mitigate grain-boundary resistance effects. Our results demonstrate the advantages of A-site Ca doping in Ba-based electrolytes, clarify the mechanisms by which small-radius, high-electronegativity dopants influence proton transport and chemical stability, and provide guidance for the design of high-performance proton-conducting electrolytes.

### [39] [Mapping recrystallization trajectories in GaAs using latent space diffraction analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13779)
*Ellis Rae Kennedy,Kwanghwi Je,Erik Thiede*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于潜空间框架（latent space framework）的方法，利用原位四维扫描透射电子显微镜（4D-STEM）衍射数据和卷积自编码器（convolutional autoencoder）来映射无序固体中再结晶（recrystallization）的路径。应用于离子辐照砷化镓（GaAs）后，该方法在约250°C处识别出两种再结晶机制，揭示了生长主导与孪晶主导的转变、杂化中间态的存在，以及传统衍射分析无法捕捉的弱对称性结构前驱体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序固体中的再结晶通过局域结构重排序列进行，而传统的衍射分析难以解析这些微妙的短程有序（short-range order）、漫散射（diffuse scattering）和缺陷介导的对称性涌现信号。因此，需要一种能直接从原位衍射数据中提取并映射这些有序化路径的新方法。

Method: 该方法构建了一个潜空间框架：首先使用卷积自编码器对原位4D-STEM衍射数据中的结构基元（structural motifs）进行紧凑表征，然后通过无监督聚类（unsupervised clustering）识别重复出现的微观结构状态，包括非晶态（amorphous）、准晶态（paracrystalline）、晶态（crystalline）、孪晶态（twinned）以及杂化中间态（hybrid intermediates）。最后通过追踪不同温度下的状态演变，构建相轨迹模型（phase trajectory models）。

Result: 应用于离子辐照GaAs后，该方法在约250°C附近识别出两个截然不同的再结晶区域：低温区以生长为主导，非晶态和晶态占优；高温区相景观重新组织，杂化和缺陷态成为孪晶的亚稳前驱体，多晶区域稳定化，孪晶结构成为主要终态。此外，潜空间表征还识别出具有弱对称性特征的非晶态模式，这些模式出现在再结晶之前，是传统描述符无法捕捉的结构前驱体。

Conclusion: 该潜空间框架能够揭示再结晶景观的拓扑结构（topology of the recrystallization landscape），包括亚稳态盆地（metastable basins）、分支路径（branching pathways）、杂化态（hybrid states）以及温度驱动的可达态重组，为理解再结晶如何被引发提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Recrystallization in disordered solids proceeds through a sequence of local structural rearrangements that are difficult to resolve using conventional diffraction analysis. In amorphous and partially ordered materials, subtle variations in diffuse scattering, short-range order, and defect-mediated symmetry emergence encode the pathways through which ordering initiates and propagates. Here, we introduce a latent space framework for mapping these pathways directly from \textit{in situ} 4D-STEM diffraction data. A convolutional autoencoder provides a compact representation of structural motifs, and unsupervised clustering identifies recurring microstructural states, including amorphous, paracrystalline, crystalline, twinned, and hybrid intermediates. By tracking these states across temperature, we construct phase trajectory models that reveal the topology of the recrystallization landscape, including metastable basins, branching pathways, hybrid states, and temperature-dependent reorganizations of accessible states.
  Applied to ion irradiated GaAs, this approach uncovers two distinct recrystallization regimes separated by a transition near 250\textdegree{}C. At low temperature, recrystallization is growth-dominated and dominated by the persistence of amorphous and crystalline states. At high temperature, the transformation landscape reorganizes: hybrid and faulted states become metastable precursors to twinning, polycrystalline regions stabilize, and twinned structures emerge as dominant end states. The latent space representation also identifies amorphous patterns with weak symmetry signatures that precede recrystallization. This reveals structural precursors to ordering that are not captured by conventional descriptors give new insights into how recrystallization is initiated.

### [40] [First-principles Study of Structural and Electronic Properties of Mn-doped Cu2NiXY4 (X=Sn, Ge, Si; Y=S, Se) Chalcogenide Semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13846)
*Iskandar Raufzoda,Dilshod Nematov,Amondullo Burhonzoda*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用密度泛函理论（DFT）结合mBJ+U方法，系统研究了Mn部分替代Ni对kesterite体系Cu2NiXY4（X = Sn, Ge, Si; Y = S, Se）结构和电子性质的影响。结果表明，Mn替代保持了四方结构，但显著改变了电子结构，导致带隙从1.028–3.397 eV缩小至1.007–3.333 eV。带隙变窄源于Mn-3d、Cu-3d与S/Se-p轨道在带边附近的杂化，证明Mn替代是调控该类kesterite电子性质的有效策略，在需要可调带隙的光电子器件中具有应用前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前尚未对Mn替代整个Cu2NiXY4（X = Sn, Ge, Si; Y = S, Se）家族进行系统的比较研究。本研究旨在填补该空白，探究Mn部分替代Ni对该类kesterite体系结构与电子性质的调控作用。

Method: 采用基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的mBJ+U方法以提高带隙计算的准确性。由于kesterite晶胞的晶体学限制，单个Ni原子被Mn替代对应50%的替代浓度，该构型被用于研究Mn替代的影响。

Result: Mn部分替代Ni保留了kesterite的四方结构，但显著改变了电子结构。所有化合物带隙均下降，从1.028–3.397 eV降至1.007–3.333 eV；例如Cu2NiSnS4体系中带隙从1.59 eV降至1.49 eV。带隙窄化来源于Mn-3d、Cu-3d与S/Se-p轨道在带边附近的杂化，导致费米能级（Fermi level）附近电子态重新分布。

Conclusion: Mn替代是调控Cu2NiXY4 kesterite电子性质的有效策略，在需要可调带隙的光电子器件中具有重要应用前景。更低浓度Mn替代的影响需通过超胞（supercell）方法进行后续研究。

Abstract: In this work, the effect of partial substitution of Mn by Ni on the structural and electronic properties of kesterite systems Cu2NiXY4 (X = Sn, Ge, Si; Y = S, Se) was studied using density functional theory (DFT). The mBJ+U method was used to characterize the bandgap more accurately. To the best of our knowledge, a systematic comparative study of Mn substitution in the entire Cu2NiXY4 (X = Sn, Ge, Si; Y = S, Se) family has not been previously performed. Due to crystallographic constraints of the kesterite unit cell, the substitution of a single Ni atom with Mn corresponds to 50%. This configuration was chosen to study the effect of Mn substitution on the structural and electronic properties of Cu2NiXY4 (X = Sn, Ge, Si; Y = S, Se) compounds, whereas the study of lower concentrations requires the use of a supercell and is the subject of further research. The calculation results show that the partial substitution of Ni with Mn preserves the tetragonal structure of kesterite and significantly alters the electronic structure. In all the compounds studied, the bandgap decreases from 1.028-3.397 to 1.007-3.333 eV. For example, in the Cu2NiSnS4 system, the bandgap width decreases from 1.59 eV to 1.49 eV. The narrowing of the bandgap results from hybridization between the Mn-3d, Cu-3d, and S/Se-p orbitals near the band edges, leading to a redistribution of electronic states around the Fermi level. The results demonstrate that Mn substitution is an effective strategy for controlling the electronic properties of Cu2NiXY4 kesterites, offering great promise for use in optoelectronic devices where adjustable bandgaps are required.

### [41] [Temperature-driven sodium-ion dynamical-to-static crossover in the zig-zag ordered phase of Na$_{0.5}$CoO$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13848)
*Shangfei Wu,Hengxin Tan,Dong Wu,Mingshu Tan,Xinyu Zhou,Tianchen Hu,Tao Dong,Feng Jin,Qingming Zhang,Nanlin Wang*

TL;DR: 本文通过偏振分辨拉曼光谱（polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy）结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），首次在钠之字形有序钴酸盐 Na₀.₅CoO₂ 中探测到两个钠离子声子模式，并发现其出现温度（~300±50 K）远低于钠之字形有序温度（~460 K），且伴随宽线宽展宽。研究将这一声子异常解释为从动力学到静态的交叉（dynamical-to-static crossover），并指出钠离子逐渐冻结和之字形有序的建立为 CoO₂ 层中电子与磁有序的出现提供了前提条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用偏振分辨拉曼光谱实验测量，并结合基于正交晶胞（orthorhombic unit cell）的第一性原理声子计算（first-principles phonon calculations）。

Result: 首次探测到两个钠声子模式（sodium phonon modes），其频率与第一性原理计算结果一致。这些模式在约 300±50 K 以下出现，具有大线宽展宽（linewidth broadening），远低于钠之字形有序温度 460 K，并随温度降低而窄化。

Conclusion: 钠声子异常发生在 T*~300±50 K，被解释为动力学到静态的交叉（dynamical-to-static crossover），主要涉及钠离子运动。钠离子的逐渐冻结以及低于 T* 时明确的静态钠之字形有序（static sodium-zigzag order）为 CoO₂ 层中电子和磁有序的出现奠定了基础。

Abstract: We employ polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy combined with first-principles calculations to study the sodium-ion lattice dynamics in a sodium zig-zag ordered cobaltate compound Na$_{0.5}$CoO$_2$. We detect two sodium phonon modes for the first time, and their mode frequencies are consistent with first-principles phonon calculations based on an orthorhombic unit cell. We find that they appear below around $T^*\sim300\pm50$K with large linewidth broadening, much lower than the sodium zig-zag ordering temperature $T_\text{S}\sim460$K, and then narrow at lower temperatures. We interpret the sodium-phonon anomalies occurring at $T^*$ as a dynamical-to-static crossover involving mainly the motion of sodium ions. Our results suggest that the gradual freezing of the sodium ions and the well-defined static sodium-zigzag order below $T^*$ set the stage for the emergent electronic and magnetic orders in the CoO$_2$ layer of Na$_{0.5}$CoO$_2$.

Method: 在混合分子束外延（hybrid molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）腔内，利用反射高能电子衍射（reflection high energy electron diffraction, RHEED）枪提供的电子束辐照TiO₂薄膜表面，通过辐解效应驱动原子重排实现晶化；并通过调节衬底温度和电子束剂量来控制薄膜结晶度。采用扫描电子显微镜（SEM）和原子级分辨率扫描透射电子显微镜（atomic-resolution STEM）进行表征。

Conclusion: 电子束辐解可作为建设性力在低温下驱动晶体薄膜生长，为原子级可控的低温柔性衬底上晶体材料制备提供了新途径。

Abstract: A new approach for growing crystalline thin films is developed that takes advantage of electron beam radiolysis being a constructive force to rearrange atoms into a crystalline structure. Here, rutile TiO2 films were grown using hybrid molecular beam epitaxy (MBE) allowing atomic level control of growth as well as an observation of radiolysis-driven crystallization. Analysis was carried out using a combination of SEM and atomic-resolution STEM imaging. It is also shown that by tuning the temperature of the substrate and the dose of the electron beam, the degree of crystallinity of the film can be controlled.

### [43] [Ultrafast altermagnetophononics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13863)
*Chenyu Wang,Yaxian Wang,Sheng Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出“交替磁子-声子学”（altermagnetophononics）作为一种通过相干声子（coherent phonons）诱导选择性对称性破缺来实现交替磁体（altermagnet）中磁性超快动力学调控的新路径，并在α-MnTe和CrSb等材料中验证了其可行性与普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交替磁体（altermagnet）因其对称性决定的非平凡自旋劈裂（spin splitting）而有望用于下一代自旋电子学（spintronics），但其超快动力学操控尚未被充分探索。

Method: 以原型交替磁体α-MnTe为例，通过相干声子（coherent phonons）选择性激发B$_{1g}$模，打破保护交替磁性（altermagnetism, AM）的对称性约束，从而驱动超快相变。

Result: 成功实现从交替磁体向瞬态补偿亚铁磁相（compensated ferrimagnetic phase, cFiM）的超快转变，该相具有全局自旋劈裂（global spin splitting）但无净磁化（net magnetization）。此外，在金属性CrSb中实现了具有可逆磁矩（reversible magnetic moment）的铁磁序（ferrimagnetic order），并展示了多模对称性破缺路径的广泛适用性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了通过相干声子控制自旋劈裂（spin splitting）来获得交替磁体中理想非平衡性质的潜力，为超快磁性调控提供了新方向。

Abstract: Altermagnets feature symmetry-dictated nontrivial spin splitting in electronic structure promising for next-generation spintronics, yet their ultrafast dynamical manipulation remains largely unexplored. Here, we establish altermagnetophononics as an efficient route for magnetic control via selective symmetry breaking induced by coherent phonons. Using the prototypical altermagnet $α$-MnTe as an example, we demonstrate that the targeted excitation of B$_{1g}$ mode selectively lifts the symmetry constraints protecting altermagnetism (AM), driving ultrafast transition into a transient compensated ferrimagnetic (cFiM) phase characterized by a global spin splitting without net magnetization. Further, we show that the proposed mechanism is broadly applicable by demonstrating a multi-mode symmetry breaking pathway, and by realizing a ferrimagnetic order with reversible magnetic moment in metallic CrSb. These findings elucidate the potential to obtain desirable nonequilibrium properties in altermagnets via coherent phononic control over their spin splittings.

### [44] [Revealing the MoS2 Growth Mechanism in Chemical Vapor Deposition: Real-Time Imaging and Statistical Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13893)
*Faizal Arifurrahman,Tianshu Zhai,Yuguo Wang,Jing Zhang,Andrew L. Hitt,Jun Lou,Ming Tang*

TL;DR: 本研究开发并应用了一套半自动化图像处理流程，对MoS₂化学气相沉积（CVD）生长过程中的原位光学显微镜影像进行分析，实现了对单个实验中超过400个晶体的完整生长轨迹的高通量重建。统计分析表明，MoS₂结晶受边缘附着限制（edge-attachment-limited）机制主导，而非前驱体扩散（precursor diffusion），且晶体间呈现非竞争性生长（non-competitive growth），为二维过渡金属硫族化合物（TMD）的CVD生长理性优化提供了定量证据和方法论基础。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 化学气相沉积（CVD）是规模化合成二维过渡金属硫族化合物（TMD）如MoS₂的 promising 方法，但由于对其动态生长机制的了解不完整，可重复性和可控性方面的挑战依然存在。尽管原位表征方法能提供有价值的见解，但追踪大量晶体以实现定量、统计分析仍具困难。

Method: 开发并应用了一套半自动化图像处理流程（semi-automated image processing pipeline），对MoS₂生长的原位光学显微镜（in-situ optical microscopy）影像进行分析，实现单个实验中超过400个晶体的完整生长轨迹的高通量重建。

Result: 统计分析表明，MoS₂结晶由边缘附着限制（edge-attachment-limited）机制主导，而非前驱体扩散（precursor diffusion）；MoS₂晶体呈现非竞争性生长（non-competitive growth），表明前驱体供应在物理接触（impingement）发生前并不限制相邻晶体的生长。

Conclusion: 这些发现为理解TMD生长提供了直接、定量的证据，建立了一种用于理性优化二维材料CVD生长的强力方法论。

Abstract: Chemical Vapor Deposition (CVD) is a promising method for scalable synthesis of two-dimensional transitional metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) such as MoS2, but challenges in reproducibility and controllability persist due to an incomplete understanding of their dynamic growth mechanisms. While in-situ characterization methods could provide valuable insights, it remains challenging to track a large ensemble of crystals to enable quantitative, statistical analysis. Here, we address this gap by developing and applying a semi-automated image processing pipeline to analyze in-situ optical microscopy footage of MoS2 growth. This framework enables the high-throughput reconstruction of complete growth trajectories for over 400 individual crystals from a single experiment. Our statistical analysis demonstrates that MoS2 crystallization is governed by an edge-attachment-limited mechanism rather than by precursor diffusion. Furthermore, MoS2 crystals exhibit non-competitive growth, indicating that precursor supply does not limit the growth of neighboring flakes until physical impingement occurs. These findings provide direct, quantitative evidence that advances the fundamental understanding of TMD growth, establishing a powerful methodology for rational optimization of the CVD growth of two-dimensional materials.

### [45] [Chemical short-range order controls deformation pathways in a complex concentrated alloy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13896)
*Angelo F. Andreoli,Gabriela B. Ribeiro,Guilherme C. Stumpf,Maria F. L. Valverde,Gustavo Bertoli,Vinícius P. Bacurau,David D. S. Silva,Pedro H. F. Oliveira,Eric M. Mazzer,Mamta Silwal,Garritt J. Tucker,Rodrigo Freitas,Martin Sahlberg,Daniel Miracle,Francisco G. Coury*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 化学短程序（CSRO）是复杂浓缩合金（CCAs）的固有特征，但因其在变形过程中的定量表征不明确，CSRO对变形机制的影响一直存在争议。

Method: 通过对比淬火（贫CSRO）与时效（富CSRO）两种状态（晶粒结构和相组成相同），结合量热法（calorimetry）、同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron X-ray diffraction）、电子显微镜（electron microscopy）和原子模拟（atomistic simulations）进行系统研究。

Result: 量热法确认CSRO可逆形成；同步辐射X射线衍射与电镜显示CSRO抑制了室温和低温下的变形诱导fcc-hcp马氏体相变；原子模拟表明CSRO同时提高了稳定和不稳定堆垛层错能，提高了不全位错（partial dislocation）活动的能垒。

Conclusion: CSRO可作为调节堆垛层错能和控制复杂浓缩合金变形路径的一个新增自由度。

Abstract: Chemical short-range order (CSRO) is an intrinsic feature of complex concentrated alloys (CCAs), yet its influence on deformation mechanisms is controversial because of the inconclusive state of concurrent CSRO quantification during deformation. Here, we provide experimental evidence that CSRO acts as an intrinsic thermodynamic state variable governing stacking-fault energetics and deformation pathways in a Co30Cr40Ni30 alloy. By comparing quenched (CSRO-lean) and aged (CSRO-enriched) conditions with equivalent grain structure and phase constitution, we isolate the influence of atomic-scale chemical ordering on mechanical behavior. Calorimetry confirms reversible CSRO formation, while synchrotron X-ray diffraction and electron microscopy reveal that CSRO suppresses deformation-induced fcc-hcp martensitic transformation at both room and cryogenic temperatures. Despite differences in transformation dynamics, the macroscopic tensile response is still broadly similar. Atomistic simulations show that CSRO increases both stable and unstable stacking-fault energies, raising the energetic barrier for partial-dislocation activity and stabilizing the fcc lattice against transformation. Together, the experimental and computational results establish CSRO as an added degree of freedom for tuning stacking-fault energetics and controlling deformation pathways in complex concentrated alloys.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于白云石型材料家族的高晶体对称性，提出化学合成策略；以SnCo(BO3)2和SnMn(BO3)2为实例进行合成；通过结构分析确定Co²⁺和Mn²⁺离子形成A-B-C堆叠方式的等边三角形晶格；采用磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）和比热（specific heat）测量表征其磁性质。

Conclusion: 白云石型M'M(X)₂体系（M'和M位点可容纳多种价态组合，如+4/+2或+3/+3；X = CO₃²⁻或BO₃³⁻）被确立为一个化学灵活且结构完美的材料平台，可用于探索阻挫磁性（frustrated magnetism）和低温磁热效应（low-temperature magnetocaloric applications）。

Abstract: Equilateral triangular lattice magnets provide a versatile materials platform for exploring exotic quantum spin phenomena, while their field-tunable magnetic entropy offers opportunities for low-temperature adiabatic demagnetization refrigeration. Inspired by the natural mineral, we proposed a chemical strategy to achieve equilateral TL magnets, leveraging the high crystal symmetry of a large family of dolomite-type materials. As typical examples, the dolomite-type materials SnM(BO3)2 (M = Co, Mn) were synthesized, and structural analysis reveals that Co2+ and Mn2+ ions form equilateral triangular lattices with an A-B-C stacking fashion. The magnetic susceptibilities and specific heat measurements reveal dominant antiferromagnetic interactions, with Neel temperatures of 0.49K for SnCo(BO3)2 and 0.96K for SnMn(BO3)2, respectively. Our results establish the dolomite-type M'M(X)2 (M'and M sites allow various valence states, e.g., +4/+2 or +3/+3; X = CO32- or BO33-) system as a chemically flexible and structurally perfect material platform for exploring frustrated magnetism and low-temperature magnetocaloric applications.

### [47] [Using superpixels for interpretable feature reduction in large 2D diffraction datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13979)
*Andreas Werbrouck,Nikhila C. Paranamana,Andrew C. Meng,Xiaoqing He,Matthias J. Young*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种将像素分组为可变面积超像素（superpixels）的预处理方法，用于加速大规模二维衍射数据（如4D-STEM电子衍射或同步辐射X射线数据）的处理。通过方差最小化聚类（K-means与凝聚聚类）结合高斯随机投影（Gaussian random projection），在保持信息的前提下实现数据压缩，并在4D-STEM相映射（phase mapping）任务中取得超过100倍的加速效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模二维衍射数据集（如4D-STEM或同步辐射X射线数据）体量巨大，标准降维方法（如裁剪探测器或像素合并（pixel binning））存在信息损失或处理瓶颈。现有机器学习方法虽具有分析潜力，但数据规模成为处理流程中的关键瓶颈。

Method: 提出将像素分组为可变面积超像素（superpixels）的预处理方法：高信息区域密集采样，低信息区域合并为较大超像素，从而捕获并利用数据中的对称性。比较了两种方差最小化方法——K-means聚类（自上而下）和凝聚聚类（自下而上, agglomerative clustering），并采用高斯随机投影（Gaussian random projection）加速基于距离的超像素构建。

Result: 自下而上的凝聚聚类方法在扩展性（scaling）和可解释性（interpretability）上优于K-means。高斯随机投影可有效加速超像素构建。在4D-STEM数据集上，使用超像素作为预处理步骤进行非负矩阵分解（Non-negative matrix factorization, NMF）相映射，实现了超过100倍的加速。

Conclusion: 超像素预处理方法能够显著加速大规模二维衍射数据的分析流程，尤其适用于需要高计算效率的场景，如4D-STEM中的相映射任务。

Abstract: Large 2D diffraction datasets, consisting of hundreds or thousands of measurements, are commonly acquired with 4D-STEM electron diffraction or at synchrotron X-ray beamlines. Machine learning and artificial intelligence offer great promise for analyzing these datasets. However, the sheer volume of data presents a significant data processing bottleneck. Cropping the detector and pixel binning are standard ways to reduce data size. Here we propose grouping and averaging pixels into superpixels of variable area. High-information regions are sampled densely, while low-information areas are collected into larger superpixels. In the process, symmetries in the data are captured and exploited, making this approach suitable for preprocessing 2D diffraction data. We compare two variance-minimizing methods: K-means clustering (top-down) and agglomerative clustering (bottom-up) and demonstrate superior scaling and interpretability for the bottom-up method. As these methods are distance-based, we demonstrate that the construction of superpixels can be accelerated using Gaussian random projection. Finally we show over 100-fold acceleration for phase mapping with Non-negative matrix factorization on a 4D-STEM dataset when superpixels are used as a preprocessing step.

### [48] [The WEST code for large-scale excited-state materials simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14025)
*Victor Wen-zhe Yu,Siyuan Chen,Yu Jin,Vrindaa Somjit,Stefano Paolo Villani,Jiawei Zhan,Marco Govoni,Giulia Galli*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文介绍WEST，一个用于大规模激发态材料模拟的开源平面波赝势代码，阐述了其理论基础、软件架构与能力。WEST在全频GW、量子缺陷嵌入理论、Bethe-Salpeter方程及含时密度泛函理论中采用统一算法框架，避免显式计算虚电子态，并通过密度泛函与密度矩阵微扰理论、低秩表示及局域化技术实现良好的系统尺寸扩展性。该代码支持准粒子与中性激发能量、光学与光致发光谱、激发态力及非绝热耦合计算，并具备与量子化学、振动耦合及量子计算软件包互操作的工作流。层次化并行策略与GPU加速使代码在数千GPU上实现近理想强扩展，可模拟超过一千个原子的系统。固态自旋缺陷的完整光学循环、金属卤化物钙钛矿中的自陷激子、液态水与冰的光学响应等代表性应用展示了代码的精度与通用性，确立了其作为预测性激发态模拟、高通量材料发现及机器学习高保真数据集生成的可扩展平台地位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激发态材料模拟对理解光学过程与量子现象至关重要，但现有方法面临计算量巨大、扩展性差的瓶颈，尤其是虚电子态的显式求解限制了系统规模。开发一种能够高效处理大体系激发态、同时保持高精度与良好并行扩展性的开源代码具有迫切需求。

Method: WEST采用统一算法框架，在全频GW、量子缺陷嵌入理论、Bethe-Salpeter方程及含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent density functional theory）中避免显式求解虚电子态。该方法结合密度泛函理论（DFT）与密度矩阵微扰理论（density matrix perturbation theory）、介电屏蔽与精确交换的低秩表示（low-rank representation）以及局域化技术，实现随系统尺寸的有利计算标度。代码采用层次化并行策略与GPU加速，支持异构工作流集成。

Result: WEST在数千GPU上实现了近理想强扩展（near-ideal strong scaling），可精准模拟超过一千个原子的体系。代表性应用包括固态自旋缺陷的完整光学循环、金属卤化物钙钛矿中自陷激子（self-trapped excitons）以及液态水与冰的光学响应，覆盖多种材料类别并验证了代码的精度与通用性。

Conclusion: WEST被确立为用于预测性激发态模拟、高通量材料发现（high-throughput materials discovery）以及为计算材料科学中机器学习生成高保真数据集（high-fidelity datasets）的可扩展平台。该代码的成功开发标志着大规模激发态材料模拟领域的重要进展，为跨学科材料研究提供了开源工具基础。

Abstract: We present WEST, an open-source plane-wave pseudopotential code for large-scale excited-state materials simulations, and describe its theoretical foundations, software architecture, and capabilities. WEST implements full-frequency GW, quantum defect embedding theory, the Bethe-Salpeter equation, and time-dependent density functional theory within a common algorithmic framework that avoids the explicit computation of virtual electronic states. By combining density functional and density matrix perturbation theory, low-rank representations of the dielectric screening and exact exchange, and localization techniques, WEST achieves favorable computational scaling with system size. The code supports the calculation of quasi-particle and neutral excitation energies, optical and photoluminescence spectra, excited-state forces, and non-adiabatic couplings, with interoperable workflows connecting to quantum chemistry, vibronic coupling, and quantum computing packages. A hierarchical parallelization strategy and GPU acceleration deliver near-ideal strong scaling to thousands of GPUs, enabling accurate excited-state simulations of systems with more than a thousand atoms. Representative applications, spanning the full optical cycle of solid-state spin defects, self-trapped excitons in metal-halide perovskites, and the optical response of liquid water and ice, demonstrate the accuracy and versatility of the code across diverse material classes. The capabilities implemented in WEST establish the code as a scalable platform for predictive excited-state simulations, high-throughput materials discovery, and the generation of high-fidelity datasets for machine learning in computational materials science.

### [49] [Orbital Hybridization Induces Giant Cubic Rashba Effect at Cu/WO$_{3}$ Interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14069)
*Md Aktar Hossain,Saikat Das*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，以Cu(001)/WO₃(001)异质结构为模型，证明将轻金属Cu与带状绝缘体WO₃界面化可以产生一种界面态，该界面态由于线性Rashba效应与三次Rashba效应的共同作用，表现出稳健的Rashba自旋分裂，其自旋轨道耦合主要来源于W原子，并通过界面处W-Cu轨道杂化实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，利用Rashba自旋轨道相互作用（spin-orbit interaction）及相关自旋电子学（spintronic）功能依赖于含有重金属的金属表面或界面。本文旨在探索使用轻金属（如Cu）与绝缘氧化物界面化是否也能产生显著的Rashba效应，从而拓展材料平台。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），以Cu(001)/WO₃(001)异质结构为模型体系，分析界面态的电子结构和自旋分裂特性，并考察不同Cu厚度及界面几何取向（包括(110)和(111)）对Rashba参数的影响。

Result: 界面处的Rashba自旋分裂源于W原子的强自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）以及W-Cu轨道杂化（orbital hybridization）。三次Rashba贡献随Cu厚度渐近增长，可由真空/Cu与Cu/WO₃界面之间的交叉耦合（cross-coupling）解释；当Cu厚度增大时交叉耦合减弱，提取的本征三次Rashba参数约为-1.93 eV·Å³。线性Rashba参数受交叉耦合影响较弱，变化范围约为0.30–0.49 eV·Å。该效应在多种界面几何和Cu表面取向下依然显著。

Conclusion: 本研究确定了Cu/WO₃界面作为一种新型的轻金属/重元素基氧化物平台（light-metal/heavy-element-based oxide platform），可用于探索包括线性和非线性自旋轨道现象在内的丰富Rashba物理（Rashba physics）。

Abstract: Harnessing Rashba spin-orbit interaction and related spintronic functionalities has traditionally relied on metallic surfaces or interfaces containing elemental heavy metals. Here, using first-principles calculations and Cu(001)/WO$_3$(001) as a model heterostructure, we show that interfacing a light metal, Cu, with a band insulator, WO$_3$, yields an interface state that exhibits a robust Rashba spin splitting arising from the interplay between linear and cubic Rashba effects. The spin splitting is driven by the strong spin-orbit coupling of W atoms and enabled by W-Cu orbital hybridization at the interface. The cubic Rashba contribution asymptotically grows with Cu thickness and can be explained in terms of cross-coupling between the vacuum/Cu and Cu/WO$_3$ interfaces. This interfacial cross-coupling, however, diminishes at larger Cu thicknesses, allowing us to extract the intrinsic cubic Rashba parameter, which has a giant value of approximately -1.93 eV $Å^3$. In contrast, the linear Rashba parameter is only weakly affected by this cross-coupling and varies from approximately 0.30 to 0.49 eV Å. We further show that sizable linear and cubic Rashba effects persist across several interface geometries and Cu surface orientations, including (110) and (111). Our work identifies the Cu/WO$_3$ interface as a novel light-metal/heavy-element-based oxide platform for exploring the rich spectrum of Rashba physics, including linear and nonlinear spin-orbit phenomena.

</details>

### [50] [Three-form dark energy: constraints and multi-probe comparison with $Λ$CDM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27436)
*Mariam Bouhmadi-López,Hsu-Wen Chiang,Carlos G. Boiza,Javier Ortega del Río,Thomas J. Broadhurst,Pisin Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究具有高斯势的三形式场（three-form field）暗能量模型，利用多种宇宙学观测数据与贝叶斯方法进行参数估计与模型比较。结果表明该模型能较好描述宇宙膨胀历史，在数据间存在严重张力时略微优于ΛCDM，虽未显著缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension），但提供了一种物理动机良好的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三形式场源自高维理论（higher-dimensional theories），为暗能量（dark energy）提供了理论动机充分的框架，但该模型在宇宙学观测中的具体表现与竞争性尚待检验。本研究旨在利用当前多类观测数据，系统评估三形式场暗能量模型的有效性及其与ΛCDM的比较。

Method: 采用最小耦合的三形式暗能量模型（minimally coupled three-form dark energy model），并引入高斯势（Gaussian potential）。参数估计基于贝叶斯马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Bayesian Markov-chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）框架，模型比较则利用多种信息准则（information criteria）、贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence）及张力统计量（tension statistics）。观测数据包括CMB位移参数（CMB shift parameters）、DESI DR2重子声学振荡（BAO）、Pantheon+超新星（含与不含SH0ES标定）、宇宙时钟（cosmic chronometers）及伽马射线暴（gamma-ray bursts）。

Result: 该模型为宇宙膨胀历史提供了可行且具有竞争力的描述。在早期与晚期数据集（CMB+BAO与Pantheon+SH0ES）之间存在较大张力时，模型略微优于ΛCDM；而对于其他张力较小的数据组合，偏好降至中性；单独使用早期或晚期数据时，信息准则为中性或倾向于ΛCDM。尽管模型允许更高的H₀值，但未能显著缓解哈勃张力。

Conclusion: 三形式场暗能量模型的额外自由度（additional degrees of freedom）有助于在统一框架内协调不同来源的宇宙学观测。该模型重建的暗能量动力学在中等红移处呈现特征性的幻影相（phantom phase），而在早期和晚期趋近于宇宙学常数行为，提供了独特的观测特征。模型整体上与当前观测一致，是ΛCDM的一个动机良好的替代方案，其预测可由未来巡天项目检验。

Abstract: Three-form fields provide a theoretically well-motivated framework for dark energy, arising in higher-dimensional theories and exhibiting a rich cosmological phenomenology. We investigate a minimally coupled three-form dark energy model with a Gaussian potential and constrain it using current cosmological observations, including CMB shift parameters, DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation measurements, Pantheon+ supernovae with and without SH0ES calibration, cosmic chronometers, and gamma-ray bursts. Parameter estimation is performed within a Bayesian Markov-chain Monte Carlo framework, while model comparison relies on several information criteria and the Bayesian evidence, as well as tension statistics. We find that the three-form model provides a viable and competitive description of the expansion history of the Universe. It is mildly preferred over $Λ$CDM for the combination of early and late-time datasets that are heavily tensioned (CMB+BAO and Pantheon+SH0ES). This preference decreases to neutrality for the other, less tensioned combination of early and late-time data, while for individual early-time or late-time datasets analysed separately, the information criteria are neutral or favour $Λ$CDM. This suggests that the additional degrees of freedom of the three-form field may help accommodate cosmological observations of different origins within a common framework. The reconstructed dark energy dynamics exhibit a characteristic phantom phase at intermediate redshifts while approaching a cosmological-constant-like behaviour at early and late times, providing a distinctive observational signature. Although the model does not significantly alleviate the Hubble tension despite allowing higher values of $H_0$, it remains consistent with current observations and offers a well-motivated alternative to $Λ$CDM whose predictions can be tested by future cosmological surveys.

</details>


### [51] [Evaporating cosmologically coupled black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13857)
*Marco Calzà,Davide Pedrotti,Massimiliano Rinaldi,Sunny Vagnozzi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文首次在准绝热近似下研究蒸发中的宇宙学耦合黑洞（CCBH），发现耦合效应可显著延迟霍金辐射或导致质量持续增长，并基于γ射线观测对原初CCBH的丰度给出了弱于非耦合情形的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将宇宙学耦合黑洞（CCBH）视为纯经典天体，忽略了霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）与宇宙学耦合（cosmological coupling）机制的竞争效应，本文旨在首次探讨蒸发中的CCBH，填补这一空白。

Method: 采用准绝热近似（quasi-adiabatic approximation），即霍金辐射率由瞬时CCBH质量评估；宇宙学耦合机制通过质量与尺度因子的标度关系 $M \propto a^k$ 进行唯象建模。

Result: 耦合强度 $k$ 决定了演化行为：即使晚期激活的耦合也能显著延迟霍金蒸发，或导致渐近的耦合主导质量增长。基于γ射线观测对原初CCBH丰度施加的限制弱于非耦合情形，因为CCBH远离蒸发终点的时间更长。与标准原初黑洞不同，CCBH的形成质量与当前质量不再近似相等。

Conclusion: 同一群原初CCBH可能同时受到过去蒸发历史（来自蒸发限制）和当前质量（如微引力透镜限制）的约束，这对限制原初CCBH的丰度和演化具有重要意义。

Abstract: Cosmologically coupled black holes (CCBHs), whose masses evolve in response to the cosmological expansion, have recently attracted significant theoretical and observational interest. Existing studies have treated CCBHs as purely classical objects, neglecting the effect of Hawking radiation (HR), which competes with the cosmological coupling (CC) mechanism. We take a first step towards studying evaporating CCBHs, adopting a quasi-adiabatic approximation in which the HR rate is evaluated at the instantaneous CCBH mass, and modeling the CC mechanism through the phenomenological scaling of the mass with the scale factor, $M \propto a^k$. We show that, depending on the coupling strength $k$, even late-time CC activation can significantly delay Hawking evaporation, or lead to asymptotic CC-dominated mass growth, with important implications. We set limits on the abundance of primordial CCBHs from $γ$-ray observations, finding limits which are weaker than their uncoupled counterparts, as CCBHs are kept farther from the endpoint of evaporation for a longer time. Unlike standard primordial black holes, the CCBH formation and present-day masses no longer approximately coincide, even for formation masses $M_{\text{form}} \gtrsim 10^{15}\,{\text{g}}$. Therefore, the same population of primordial CCBHs may be subject to evaporation limits through its past emission history, as well as to other limits (such as microlensing) through its present-day mass.

### [52] [Emergent Yielding from Structural Load Transfer in Disordered Soft Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13176)
*Lalit Kumar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序软固体的屈服机制长期以来缺乏统一解释，现有理论往往依赖预设屈服准则、本构切换或发散粘度等假设，无法自然描述从弹性承载向摩擦相互作用的渐进过渡过程。

Method: 该研究基于变形诱导的结构演化机制，构建了一个非奇异的统一本构框架；该框架通过承载能力从可恢复弹性网络向摩擦相互作用的渐进再分配，实现有限屈服应力和光滑固-液转变的自然涌现。

Result: 该框架无需预设屈服准则、本构切换或发散粘度，即可捕捉Herschel-Bulkley行为、应力过冲（stress overshoots）、滞后现象（hysteresis）、粘度分叉（viscosity bifurcation）、柱塞流形成（plug-flow formation）以及触变性稳态剪切带（thixotropic steady-state shear banding）等多种瞬态和稳态流变现象。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，无序软固体中的屈服行为可由承载能力从弹性网络向摩擦相互作用的渐进再分配机制统一解释，所提出的非奇异本构框架为描述屈服转变提供了一种无需奇异假设的理论途径。

Abstract: Yielding in disordered soft solids originates from the progressive redistribution of load-bearing capacity from recoverable elastic networks to frictional interactions through deformation-induced structural evolution. We present a unified, non-singular constitutive framework demonstrating that this mechanism naturally generates a finite yield stress and a smooth solid-to-fluid transition without prescribed yield criteria, constitutive switching, or divergent viscosities. The framework captures diverse transient and steady rheological phenomena, including Herschel-Bulkley behavior, stress overshoots, hysteresis, viscosity bifurcation, plug-flow formation, and thixotropic steady-state shear banding.

Method: 首先对单胞和不同尺寸点阵进行拉伸、压缩及非单调加载的系统实验；随后将Ma等人(2026)的高保真粘塑性变形本构模型通过用户材料子程序（user material subroutine）植入Abaqus/Explicit；提出基于存储弹性能（stored elastic energy）和等效塑性应变（equivalent plastic strain）的非晶态聚合物损伤起始准则；采用Konale和Srivastava(2025)的梯度损伤（gradient-damage）框架在Abaqus中实现损伤模型。

Result: 所提出的损伤模型和数值模拟能力通过非单调加载下单胞及拉伸下点阵结构的实验结果进行了定量与定性验证。

Conclusion: 该损伤模型与仿真能力使得聚合物点阵结构可通过计算机模拟（in silico）进行设计。

Abstract: Architected triply periodic minimal surface (TPMS) lattices offer superior specific energy absorption, toughness, fatigue strength, and tunability. While recent advancements have established rate-dependent viscoplastic constitutive models to capture the complex nonlinear deformation response of additively manufactured polymeric TPMS structures, predicting fracture and the resulting structural failure remains a significant challenge. We address this by performing systematic experiments on unit cells and lattices of various sizes under tension, compression, and non-monotonic loading. The experiments inform the development of a new constitutive model that captures the damage and fracture behavior of polymeric TPMS lattices. We first implement a high-fidelity viscoplastic deformation constitutive model from Ma et al. (2026) into finite element software Abaqus/Explicit via a user material subroutine. We then propose a damage initiation criterion for amorphous polymers based on stored elastic energy and equivalent plastic strain. The damage model is implemented in Abaqus using gradient-damage framework following Konale and Srivastava(2025). The damage model and numerical simulation capability are quantitatively and qualitatively validated using experimental results for a unit cell under non-monotonic loading and lattices under tension. The proposed damage model and simulation capability enable in silico design of architected polymer structures.

### [54] [Fundamental Relation between Conductance of Biomolecules and the Fukui Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13309)
*Gabor Vattay*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文在密度泛函理论（DFT）及其时间依赖扩展框架内，严格推导了耦合到金属导线的分子的有限温度电导；通过双微扰展开和快热化条件，证明热导率由有限温度Fukui函数支配，建立了电子输运与化学反应活性之间的基本联系，并指出该条件在量子临界性导致的安德森金属-绝缘体转变下的蛋白质中成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论缺乏从密度泛函理论（DFT）第一性原理出发、严格建立分子电导与化学反应活性之间统一框架的推导。本文旨在填补这一空白，并为生物电子传感与计算架构设计提供理论基础。

Method: 从Mermin巨势出发，系统构建了Kohn-Sham方程、Fukui函数以及开放量子系统的单粒子密度矩阵主方程；通过声子浴的偏迹得到非平衡电子-声子耗散子；对无相互作用费米子应用Wick定理，获得具有完全交换对称性且严格保持泡利不相容原理的碰撞积分；依次进行电压（线性响应）和分子-导线耦合（弱耦合）的双微扰展开。

Result: 在快热化条件下，复杂的交换-关联自洽场响应被慢Liouvillian模的对角结构解析地投影掉；热导率由有限温度Fukui函数——概念密度泛函理论的核心反应性描述符——所支配；该快热化条件在安德森金属-绝缘体转变处量子临界性导致的蛋白质扩展多分形波函数中成立。

Conclusion: 该推导建立了电子输运与化学反应活性之间的基本联系，将导电路径识别为反应位点；为连接药物设计与电导实验的新技术途径铺平道路，并为下一代生物电子传感与计算架构的设计提供理论基础。

Abstract: The finite-temperature conductance of a molecule coupled to metallic leads is derived entirely within the framework of density functional theory (DFT) and its time-dependent extension for open quantum systems. Starting from the Mermin grand potential, the foundational Kohn-Sham equations, the Fukui function, and the open-system master equation for the single-particle density matrix are systematically formulated. The non-equilibrium electron-phonon dissipator is obtained from the partial trace over the phonon bath. By applying Wick's theorem for non-interacting fermions, a fully exchange-symmetric collision integral is obtained that strictly preserves Pauli exclusion at the operator level. Performing a double perturbation expansion, initially in the applied voltage (linear response), and subsequently in the molecule-lead coupling (weak coupling), it is demonstrated that under the fast-thermalization condition, the complex exchange-correlation self-consistent field response is analytically projected out by the diagonal structure of the slow Liouvillian mode. Consequently, the thermal conductance is governed by the finite-temperature Fukui function, the central reactivity descriptor of conceptual density functional theory. This condition is satisfied in proteins, whose wave functions are extended and multifractal due to quantum criticality at the Anderson metal-insulator transition. This derivation establishes a fundamental link between electronic transport and chemical reactivity, identifying conducting paths with reactive sites. It opens new technological avenues connecting drug design to conductance experiments and also provides a foundation for designing next-generation bioelectronic sensing and computing architectures.

### [55] [Microscopic constitutive theory of stress overshoot, yielding, and strain hardening in amorphous materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13734)
*Ankit Singh,Valeriy V. Ginzburg,Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于非仿射弹性（nonaffine elasticity）耦合不可逆多体弛豫（irreversible many-body relaxation），发展了一个微观本构理论，统一描述了金属和聚合物玻璃从线弹性、应力过冲、屈服到稳态塑性流动的全应力—应变响应，并通过少量物性参数定量复现了多种非晶固体的实验曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶固体（amorphous solids）如金属玻璃和聚合物玻璃的非线性变形机制尚未被统一且微观的框架所解释，尤其是应力过冲（stress overshoot）的起源、屈服（yielding）与塑性流动（plastic flow）之间的关系缺乏基于原子/分子尺度的理论描述。

Method: 将非仿射弹性与不可逆多体弛豫耦合，构建微观本构理论；通过应变驱动的机械连接性（mechanical connectivity）丧失描述非仿射弹性失稳，结合结构弛豫（structural relaxation）的黏性耗散；对聚合物玻璃引入有限链伸展性（finite chain extensibility）以解释大变形应变硬化（strain hardening）；通过应力或模量弛豫测量独立获得拉伸指数弛豫指数（stretched-exponential relaxation exponent）作为主要动力学输入。

Result: 模型定量复现了金属玻璃、聚碳酸酯（polycarbonate）、PMMA和环氧树脂（epoxy resins）在广泛应变率范围内的实验应力—应变曲线；表明应力过冲源于原子/分子层面机械连接性丧失引起的非仿射弹性失稳与结构弛豫相关黏性耗散之间的竞争。

Conclusion: 该理论建立了一个统一的微观框架，将非晶固体的弛豫动力学（relaxation dynamics）、屈服、塑性流动和应变硬化联系起来，仅需少量物理上有意义的参数即可定量描述多种非晶材料的非线性力学行为。

Abstract: We develop a microscopic constitutive theory for the nonlinear deformation of metallic and polymer glasses based on nonaffine elasticity coupled to irreversible many-body relaxation. The theory predicts the full stress--strain response, from linear elasticity through stress overshoot and yielding to steady plastic flow. We show that stress overshoot originates from the competition between a nonaffine elastic instability induced by strain-driven loss of mechanical connectivity at the atomic/molecular level, and viscous dissipation associated with structural relaxation. For polymer glasses, finite chain extensibility naturally accounts for strain hardening at large deformation. The stretched-exponential relaxation exponent is obtained independently from stress or modulus relaxation measurements and provides the primary dynamical input to the theory. Using a small set of physically meaningful parameters, the model quantitatively reproduces experimental stress--strain curves for metallic glasses, polycarbonate, PMMA, and epoxy resins over a broad range of strain rates. These results establish a unified microscopic framework linking relaxation dynamics, yielding, plastic flow, and strain hardening in amorphous solids.

</details>


### [56] [Driven Odd Elasticity in Passive Mechanical Metamaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13997)
*Mohamad Rahimi,Harold S Park*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过手性齿轮和方格子超材料的被动机械组件，在机械超材料中实现了驱动型奇弹性（driven odd elasticity），展示了奇剪切模量（odd shear modulus）及其导致的非保守功（non-conservative work）与非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索是否可以在纯被动机械结构（不含电子反馈或机器人控制系统）中实现奇弹性（odd elasticity），从而拓展奇弹性在机械超材料中的实现途径。

Method: 利用手性齿轮（chiral gears）和方格子超材料（square lattice metamaterial）这些被动机械组件，构建一种将拉伸与剪切以非互易方式（non-reciprocal way）耦合的机械机制。

Result: 该机制产生了奇剪切模量（odd shear modulus），在标准准静态应变循环（standard quasistatic strain cycle）中实现了非保守功（non-conservative work），并在动力学中进一步实现了非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，仅使用被动元件（passive elements）而不依赖电子组件或反馈控制系统，即可在机械结构中实现奇弹性。

Abstract: We present a mechanical mechanism leveraging passive mechanical components, i.e. chiral gears and a square lattice metamaterial, to demonstrate driven odd elasticity in a mechanical metamaterial. The mechanism couples tension and shear in a non-reciprocal way, resulting in an odd shear modulus. The emergence of this odd shear modulus enables non-conservative work in a standard quasistatic strain cycle, and further enables the non-Hermitian skin effect in dynamics. Our results demonstrate that odd elasticity can be achieved in mechanical structures using passive elements without electronic components coupled with feedback or robotic control systems.

### [57] [Gelation of functional peptides by trivalent cations at the air-water interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14061)
*Stephen A. Crane,Felipe Jimenez Angeles,Monica Olvera de la Cruz,Ivan J. Dmochowski,Kathleen J. Stebe*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文报告了一种由多价阳离子介导桥接驱动的流体界面凝胶化机制。在气-水界面处，结合镧系阳离子的肽发生配位几何转变，将金属从单肽结合态转变为多肽桥接态，导致电荷反转并形成凝胶。该凝胶由可逆金属-配体配位键稳定，可抵抗体相盐屏蔽，与静电电荷反转凝胶化机制根本不同。研究揭示了肽配位球瓦解是界面凝胶化的独特途径，独立于控制体相蛋白质聚集的扩散静电机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索流体界面凝胶化的新机制，特别是多价阳离子介导桥接在其中的作用，以区别于已知的体相静电凝胶化机制。

Method: 通过研究结合镧系阳离子的肽在气-水界面的行为，观察到配位几何转变（coordination-geometry transition），该转变使金属从单肽结合态转变为多肽桥接态，驱动电荷反转（charge inversion）和凝胶形成。表面吸附（surface adsorption）和非理想界面静电学（non-ideal interfacial electrostatics）被推测参与这一转变。

Result: 形成的凝胶由可逆金属-配体配位键（reversible metal-ligand coordination bonds）稳定，能够抵抗体相盐屏蔽（bulk salt screening）。该机制与蛋白质中静电电荷反转凝胶化（electrostatic charge-inversion gelation）机制根本不同。

Conclusion: 肽配位球（coordinating sphere）的瓦解是一种独特的界面凝胶化途径，独立于控制体相蛋白质聚集的扩散静电机制（diffuse electrostatic mechanisms）。

Abstract: We report a mechanism for gelation at fluid interfaces driven by multivalent-cation-mediated bridging. At the air-water interface, peptides with bound lanthanide cations undergo a coordination-geometry transition that converts the metal from a single-peptide bound state to a multi-peptide bridging state, driving charge inversion and gel formation. Surface adsorption and non-ideal interfacial electrostatics are implicated in this transition. The gel is stabilized by reversible metal-ligand coordination bonds that resist bulk salt screening, fundamentally distinct from electrostatic charge-inversion gelation in proteins. This reveals the breakdown of the peptide's coordinating sphere as a distinct pathway for interfacial gelation, independent of the diffuse electrostatic mechanisms governing bulk protein aggregation.

### [58] [Boundary Thermalization in Superdiffusive Energy Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13229)
*Tomasz Komorowski,Stefano Olla*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，具有随机动量交换和端点Langevin热浴的一维非钉扎谐和链在超扩散时间标度下，其微观能量分布收敛到由Neuman分式拉普拉斯算子及热浴引入的非局部边界项构成的分式热方程，为开放链的超扩散热输运提供了宏观边界条件的严格推导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分式热方程已在无限链情形下被严格推导，但有限尺寸系统与热浴接触时的边界条件仍不明确，原因在于分式拉普拉斯算子（fractional Laplacian）所具有的非局域性（nonlocality）。

Method: 在超扩散时间标度 $t\sim n^{3/2}$（$n$为系统尺寸）下，通过取极限 $n\to+\infty$，证明微观平均能量分布收敛到定义在区间 $[0,1]$ 上的分式热方程，生成元为Neuman分式拉普拉斯算子（Neumann fractional Laplacian），并包含热浴诱导的非局部边界项。

Result: 严格推导了开放链中超扩散热输运的宏观边界条件，给出了由物理模型驱动的分式拉普拉斯算子新边界条件。

Conclusion: 该工作为有限系统中超扩散热输运的宏观描述提供了严格的数学基础，并提出了具有物理动机的分式拉普拉斯边界条件。

Abstract: We study energy transport in a finite one-dimensional unpinned harmonic chain with stochastic nearest-neighbor momentum exchanges and Langevin heat baths at its endpoints. Such systems are known to exhibit superdiffusive transport driven by long-wavelength acoustic modes, leading to fractional macroscopic behavior. While fractional heat equations have been rigorously derived for infinite chains, the corresponding boundary conditions for finite systems in contact with heat baths remain unclear due to the nonlocality of the fractional Laplacian. Under the superdiffusive time scaling $t\sim n^{3/2}$, where $n$ is the system size, we prove that the averaged microscopic energy profile converges, as $n\to+\infty$, to a temperature field solving a fractional heat equation on $[0,1]$,
  with the generator given by a Neumann fractional Laplacian and
  additional nonlocal boundary terms induced by the heat baths. Our results provide a
  rigorous derivation of macroscopic boundary conditions for
  superdiffusive heat transport in open chains and introduce new
  boundary conditions for fractional Laplacians, that are motivated by
  a physical model.

</details>


### [59] [Spectral Analysis and Liouville-Green Asymptotics for a Radial Sturm-Liouville Operator with Variable Coefficients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13349)
*Victor S. Gerasimchuk,Bohdan O. Yevdokymenko,Igor V. Gerasimchuk*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个径向对称初边值问题，通过变量分离将其转化为具有显式系数和正权函数的正则自伴Sturm-Liouville问题。该问题包含一个由几何诱导的特殊系数对，定义了非标准加权谱结构。作者推导了精确的超越谱方程，并利用Liouville-Green变换得到了高频区间的渐近特征值、特征函数以及Liouville-Green准模。数值计算验证了渐近量化公式的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究源于一类具有几何诱导系数的径向对称初边值问题，其变量分离产生了一个非标准加权的Sturm-Liouville谱结构。该结构的显式分析与渐近逼近是理解和求解原演化问题的关键。

Method: 首先通过变量分离将原问题转化为一个正则自伴Sturm-Liouville问题；然后推导精确的超越谱方程；接着对径向Sturm-Liouville方程应用Liouville-Green变换（Liouville-Green transformation）以分析高频区域，得到渐近特征值与特征函数的显式公式以及Liouville-Green准模（quasimodes）；最后在精确算子的谱框架下验证准模的加权正交性与渐近完备性（asymptotic completeness）。

Result: 得到了一个离散实谱和相应加权Hilbert空间中的完备标准正交特征函数系，建立了演化问题的精确谱表示。推导了显式的渐近特征值与特征函数公式及准模，并证明了其加权正交性和渐近完备性。利用渐近谱数据构造了原边值问题的近似解，并给出了谱重构的误差估计。数值计算显示精确谱与Liouville-Green预测高度一致。

Conclusion: 本文提出的渐近量化公式得到数值验证，证明所提出的谱近似方法具有良好的准确性。

Abstract: We investigate a radially symmetric initial-boundary value problem whose separation of variables leads to a regular self-adjoint Sturm-Liouville problem with explicitly determined coefficients and a positive weight function. The resulting Sturm-Liouville operator is defined by a special geometry-induced coefficient pair that gives rise to a nonstandard weighted spectral structure. The associated radial operator possesses a discrete real spectrum and a complete orthonormal system of eigenfunctions in the corresponding weighted Hilbert space, yielding an exact spectral representation of the evolution problem. An exact transcendental spectral equation governing the eigenvalues is derived. To analyze the high-frequency regime, the Liouville-Green transformation is applied directly to the radial Sturm-Liouville equation. This yields explicit asymptotic formulas for the eigenvalues and eigenfunctions together with corresponding Liouville-Green quasimodes. Their weighted orthogonality properties and asymptotic completeness are established within the spectral framework of the exact operator. The resulting asymptotic spectral data are used to construct approximate solutions of the original boundary-value problem and to obtain error estimates for the spectral reconstruction. Numerical computations of the exact Sturm-Liouville spectrum show excellent agreement with the Liouville-Green predictions, thereby validating the asymptotic quantization formula and confirming the accuracy of the proposed spectral approximation.

### [60] [Perturbative algebraic quantum field theory with smoothened boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13765)
*Kasia Rejzner,Michele Schiavina*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文在微扰代数量子场论（pAQFT）框架下，结合 Batalin-Fradkin-Vilkovisky（BV/BFV）形式论，对具有标记超曲面的全局双曲洛伦兹流形上的规范场理论进行了量子化，给出了修正后的主方程（master equations）的 pAQFT 表述，并构建了重整化的量子 BFV 算子。研究发现引入边界后，量子同伦 dg 李代数（dg Lie algebra）会变为弯曲的，从而将量子主方程的失效编码为 L∞ 代数的非平凡曲率项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有规范场论在处理具有边界的流形时，缺乏将局域函子方法（local functorial approach）中的关键方面融入代数框架的系统性方案。本研究旨在通过 pAQFT 与 BV/BFV 形式论的结合，填补这一空白，使得边界效应能够在代数量子场论中得到严格处理。

Method: 在全局双曲洛伦兹流形上标记超曲面，利用 pAQFT 框架并借助 BV/BFV 形式论进行量子化。论文给出了修正后的经典与量子主方程的 pAQFT 表述，并构造了重建模的量子 BFV 算子，用以纠正量子主方程因边界项导致的失效。同时，通过异常主 Ward 恒等式（Anomalous Master Ward Identity）导出了重整化后的量子同伦 dg 李代数结构。

Result: 当考虑边界时，由异常主 Ward 恒等式导出的重整化量子同伦 dg 李代数是弯曲的（curved），这意味着量子主方程的失效表现为 L∞ 代数中的一个非平凡曲率项。作为副产品，论文恢复了 Hollands 关于（边界）BRST 荷与 BV 算子之间关系的结果，并在阿贝尔杨-米尔斯理论（Abelian Yang–Mills theory）中因果柱面（causal cylinders）上恢复出 CMR 关于量子 BFV 算子在领头阶微扰下的 ansatz。

Conclusion: 该工作将 pAQFT 与 BV/BFV 形式论成功结合，为具有边界的流形上的规范场论提供了严格的代数量子化框架。边界效应的引入导致量子同伦 dg 李代数变弯曲，揭示了量子主方程失效的代数几何本质，并为未来研究更一般的边界问题和拓扑效应奠定了形式化基础。

Abstract: We formulate quantisation of gauge field theories on globally hyperbolic Lorentzian manifolds with marked hypersurfaces within the framework of perturbative algebraic quantum field theory (pAQFT) enriched by the Batalin, Fradkin, Vilkovisky formalism (BV/BFV). This allows one to incorporate some crucial aspects of the local functorial approach to gauge field theory on manifolds with boundary within the algebraic setting. In particular, we provide a pAQFT-formulation of the modified classical and quantum master equations (after Cattaneo, Mnev and Reshetikhin CMR), as well as a constructive way to build a renormalised quantum BFV operator correcting the failure of the Quantum Master Equation by means of boundary terms (in the appropriate sense). We find that the renormalised quantum homotopy dg Lie algebra arising from the Anomalous Master Ward Identity becomes curved when boundaries are considered. The failure of the quantum master equation is thus encoded by a nontrivial curvature term in an $L_\infty$ algebra. As a byproduct, we recover previous results of Hollands' on the relation between the (boundary) BRST charge and the BV operator, and we recover CMR's ansatz for the quantum BFV operator at leading perturbative order on causal cylinders in Abelian Yang--Mills theory.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 假设最小化测度的支撑集为光滑流形 $\tilde{M}$，引入密切真空（osculating vacua）概念；在一般维度的因果变分原理（causal variational principles）框架下分析几何结构（联络、黎曼度量与曲率）；在四维时空的因果费米子系统中特化为洛伦兹（Lorentzian）情形。

Abstract: The causal action principle for causal fermion systems is analyzed for a minimizing measure whose support is assumed to have the structure of a smooth manifold $\tilde{M}$. The concept of osculating vacua is introduced. It is shown that the Lagrangian induces on $\tilde{M}$ a Lorentzian metric. Moreover, the Euler-Lagrange equations of the causal action imply that the Ricci tensor must satisfy the Einstein equations of general relativity for an energy momentum tensor given in terms of a power expansion in the regularization length. The gravitational coupling constant is found to be the square of the regularization length. Our methods provide a systematic procedure for deriving corrections to the Einstein equations.
  The paper includes a self-contained introduction to causal variational principles and the causal action principle. Most geometric structures (connection, Riemannian metric and curvature) are introduced and analyzed in the general setting of causal variational principles for an arbitrary dimension of $\tilde{M}$. The Lorentzian setting works only for causal fermion systems and is worked out only in four spacetime dimensions.

### [62] [Log-Sobolev inequalities for boundary-driven anharmonic chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13953)
*Jianfeng Lu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了弱非谐振荡器链在非平衡稳态下的对数型Sobolev不等式，证明了其常数与链长N无关，并在均匀钉扎链条件下得到了与谐振链相同的O(N^3)弛豫时间尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究弱非谐振荡器链（weakly anharmonic chain）在非平衡稳态（non-equilibrium steady state）下的弛豫行为，特别是证明对数型Sobolev不等式（logarithmic Sobolev inequality）的常数与系统尺寸N无关，并建立更精细的时空不等式以刻画弛豫时间尺度。

Method: 采用微扰性弱非谐条件（perturbative weak-anharmonicity condition），通过从边界噪声中提取有限维高斯分量（finite-dimensional Gaussian component），并利用变量替换（change of variables）比较条件终端态律（conditional terminal-state laws）来完成证明。

Result: 证明了全梯度对数Sobolev不等式（full-gradient logarithmic Sobolev inequality），其常数不依赖于链长N。对于均匀钉扎链（homogeneous pinned chains），在额外的定量正则性假设下，得到了边界时空对数Sobolev不等式（boundary space-time logarithmic Sobolev inequality），其相对熵衰减时间尺度为O(N^3)，与谐振链（harmonic chain）相同。这些估计对有限正温度一致成立，且不要求温度差处于近平衡态。

Conclusion: 弱非谐性不会显著改变非平衡稳态的弛豫时间尺度，系统仍保持与谐振链一致的O(N^3)行为。该结果在无近平衡假设下成立，对有限正温度具有一致性。

Abstract: We study the non-equilibrium steady state of a weakly anharmonic chain of $N$ oscillators driven at its boundary by Langevin thermostats at unequal temperatures. Under a perturbative weak-anharmonicity condition, we prove a full-gradient logarithmic Sobolev inequality whose constant is independent of the chain length $N$. For homogeneous pinned chains, an additional quantitative regularity assumption yields a boundary space-time logarithmic Sobolev inequality and relative-entropy decay on the same $O(N^3)$ relaxation time scale as the harmonic chain. The proof extracts a finite-dimensional Gaussian component from the boundary noise and compares conditional terminal-state laws by a change of variables. The estimates are uniform over bounded positive temperatures and require no near-equilibrium assumption on their difference.

### [63] [Real Fluid Quasi-Conservative Method: Mechanical Equilibrium Mechanism and Liquid-Upwind Anomaly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13996)
*Bai Haotong,Yang Yixin,Xie Wenjia,Yi Ping,Sun Mingbo*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文从连续介质热力学（continuum thermodynamics）角度重新审视了真实流体有限体积方法中的压力振荡问题，阐明了真实流体准守恒（RFQC）方法的物理机制。研究发现RFQC方法在极端相变情形下存在一种“液体迎风异常（Liquid-upwind Anomaly, LUA）”，该异常由相变时等熵斜率的大幅跳变引发，可通过在初始间断处引入正则化策略予以消除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决真实流体有限体积方法中出现的压力振荡问题，并澄清真实流体准守恒（RFQC）方法的物理对应物，进而分析其适用极限并处理极端相变情形下的数值异常。

Method: 从连续介质热力学（continuum thermodynamics）视角出发，RFQC方法沿流线（pathlines）演化等熵内能-压力关系中的仿射参数xi和E0来恢复机械平衡压力，并通过热力学重投影（thermodynamic re-projection）将等熵轨迹的偏差转化为内能误差，从而保证热力学一致性与数值稳定性。针对极端相变情形，提出在初始间断处引入正则化策略来消除液体迎风异常（LUA）。

Result: 识别出RFQC方法在极端相变中的适用极限——液体迎风异常（LUA）：当液侧迎风平移速度超过某一阈值时，相变过程中仿射斜率xi的数量级跳变会延迟下游低压单元的压力恢复，同时重投影持续移除正压力增量，导致该单元被困于低压恢复延迟的循环中。所提出的正则化策略可有效解决该启动异常。

Conclusion: 液体迎风异常（LUA）是一种启动异常（start-up anomaly），通过初始间断处的正则化策略可以解决。经此改进，RFQC方法在极端热力学流动（如声速相变射流）中具备更高的精度和鲁棒性。

Abstract: From the perspective of continuum thermodynamics, we revisit the pressure oscillation problem in finite-volume methods for real fluids and clarify the physical counterpart of the Real Fluid Quasi-Conservative (RFQC) method. The RFQC method recovers the mechanical-equilibrium pressure by evolving the affine parameters xi and E0 of the isentropic internal energy-pressure relation along pathlines, while the thermodynamic re-projection converts the deviation from the isentropic trajectory into an internal-energy error, thereby ensuring the thermodynamic consistency and numerical stability of the method. We then investigate the applicability limit of the RFQC method and identify a Liquid-upwind Anomaly (LUA) in extreme phase-change cases. For a Riemann problem involving liquid-vapor phase change, a numerical anomaly may occur if a liquid-upwind translational velocity is initially superimposed and exceeds a certain threshold. Theoretical analysis reveals that this anomaly is initiated by the orders-of-magnitude jump in the affine slope xi during phase change, which subsequently delays the pressure rise in the downstream low-pressure cell. Concurrently, the re-projection equivalently removes the positive pressure increment. As a result, a large re-projection internal-energy error is repeatedly generated in this anomalous cell, and the cell is trapped in a cycle of delayed low-pressure recovery. The analysis indicates that the LUA is a start-up anomaly, which can be resolved by introducing a regularization strategy at the initial discontinuity. With the proposed regularization strategy, the RFQC method is equipped with enhanced accuracy and robustness for extreme thermodynamic flows, such as sonic phase-change jets.

</details>

### [64] [Half dualization and non-invertible particle-vortex duality defect on lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13138)
*Zhi-Qiang Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出“半对偶化”（half dualization）作为构造非可逆对偶缺陷（non-invertible duality defects）的一般原理，在（2+1）维Villain化电荷-n XY模型及其Z_n规范推广中展示了构造过程，并分析了缺陷的融合性质与红外行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对偶缺陷的构造缺乏统一的一般性原理，特别是在非可逆对偶缺陷（non-invertible duality defects）的构建上。本文旨在提出一种普适的、不依赖时空维度的构造方法。

Method: 提出“半对偶化”（half dualization）方法：仅在时空子区域（subregion）内执行对偶变换（duality transformation），在原始理论与其对偶理论之间留下一个界面（interface），该界面可承载非可逆对偶缺陷。该方法适用于任何存在局域对偶变换的理论，不限于特定维度。

Result: 在（2+1）维Villain化电荷-n XY模型（Villainized charge-$n$ XY model）的立方晶格上，半对偶化产生非可逆的粒子-涡旋对偶缺陷（particle-vortex duality defect），其与反向缺陷融合后在融合面上产生（1+1）维Z_n规范理论。在Z_n规范化的XY模型（Z_n-gauged XY model）中，界面承载的是规范协变对偶墙（gauge covariant duality wall），而非真正的规范不变对偶缺陷；当Z_n规范理论处于禁闭（confined）或希格斯（Higgsed）相时，该墙在红外流变为可逆对偶缺陷（invertible duality defect）。

Conclusion: 半对偶化为构造非可逆对偶缺陷提供了一个通用框架，既适用于未规范理论也适用于规范理论，并能自然地描述缺陷在红外流形下的行为变化。

Abstract: We introduce half dualization as a general principle to construct non-invertible duality defects. The construction performs a duality transformation only in a subregion of spacetime, leaving an interface between the original theory and its dual. A non-invertible duality defect can be hosted on this interface. Half dualization is applicable whenever a local duality transformation is available, and does not depend on the spacetime dimension. We demonstrate the construction procedure in the (2+1)-dimensional Villainized charge-$n$ XY model on a cubic lattice. Half dualization yields a non-invertible particle-vortex duality defect whose fusion with its orientation reverse produces a (1+1)-dimensional $\mathbb{Z}_n$ gauge theory on the fusion surface. We then apply half dualization to the $\mathbb{Z}_n$-gauged XY model relevant to the 3D XY$^\ast$ transition. In the gauged model, the half dualization interface hosts a gauge covariant duality wall, rather than a genuine gauge invariant duality defect. It flows to an invertible duality defect in infrared when the $\mathbb{Z}_n$ gauge theory is confined or Higgsed.

</details>


### [65] [Exact collective first-passage statistics of N trail-interacting walkers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13213)
*Paul Pineau,Julien Brémont,Olivier Bénichou,Raphaël Voituriez*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了通过共享踪迹场（trail field）耦合的一维随机游走者（random walkers）的集体首通现象（collective first-passage phenomena），推导了饱和响应下的持久指数（persistence exponents）和分裂概率（splitting probabilities）的精确表达式，并发现分裂概率在同步与顺序探索下保持精确不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环境记忆（environmental memory）已知会显著影响活性物质（active matter）的输运行为，但其对集体首通现象的影响尚未被充分探索。

Method: 研究了一维空间中$N$个通过共享踪迹场相互作用的随机游走者，分析了第$k$个到达固定目标的时间，以及恰好$k$个游走者在区间$[0,1]$内先到达某一边界的概率。针对具有饱和响应（saturating response）的自相互作用游走者（self-interacting walkers）这一广泛类别，推导出了持久指数和分裂概率的精确表达式。

Result: 尽管共同环境产生了强历史依赖的相关性，但分裂概率在游走者同时探索或依次探索时完全相同；这一不变性（invariance）在非饱和踪迹相互作用（nonsaturating trail interactions）下被破坏。

Conclusion: 研究结果源于对集体踪迹场的精确表示（exact representation），为通过持久环境记忆（persistent environmental memory）耦合的系统中的首通现象建立了理论框架。

Abstract: Memory encoded in the environment mediates interactions between active agents, from trail-following organisms to synthetic active matter depositing persistent tracks. Although such memory is known to strongly affect transport, its consequences for collective first-passage phenomena remain largely unexplored. Here we study $N$ one-dimensional random walkers interacting through a shared trail field. We characterize the $k^{\rm th}$ (among $N$) arrival time at a fixed target, and the probability that exactly $k$ walkers in $[0,1]$ reach one boundary before the other. For the broad class of self-interacting walkers with a saturating response to the trail, we derive exact expressions for the corresponding persistence exponents and splitting probabilities. Strikingly, despite the strong history-dependent correlations generated by the common environment, splitting probabilities are exactly identical whether walkers explore simultaneously or one after another. This invariance breaks down for nonsaturating trail interactions. Our results follow from an exact representation of the collective trail field and establish a framework for first-passage phenomena in systems coupled through persistent environmental memory.

### [66] [A Loewner-Theoretic Approach to the Nonlinear Generalized Langevin Equation: The Role of Entropy in Colored Noise Environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13384)
*Yusuke K. Shibasaki*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用基于弦向Loewner方程（chordal Loewner equation）的共形变换（conformal transformation）分解方法，形式化推导了一维非线性广义Langevin方程（nonlinear generalized Langevin equation）。通过改进的Mori-Zwanzig方法（Mori-Zwanzig method），重新表述了不同类型的涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation, FDR），并利用记忆核（memory kernel）模拟细胞迁移实验，通过数值仿真获得了两种FDR共有的能量耗散标度律（scaling law）。此外，研究引入Loewner熵（Loewner entropy）概念，在有色噪声（colored noise）环境下估计正则系综（canonical ensemble）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在利用共形映射与Loewner演化理论，扩展经典非平衡统计力学框架，特别是推广Mori-Zwanzig投影算子方法，以在更一般的几何变换下形式化描述非线性随机动力学系统。

Method: 采用基于弦向Loewner方程（chordal Loewner equation）的共形变换（conformal transformation）分解方法，将离散Loewner演化（discrete Loewner evolution）导出的算子替换传统Mori-Zwanzig方法中的投影算子，从而推导一维非线性广义Langevin方程（nonlinear generalized Langevin equation）。随后，通过共形映射对涨落-耗散关系（FDR）进行数学重述，并利用记忆核（memory kernel）模拟细胞迁移实验，进行数值仿真以提取能量耗散标度律（scaling law）。同时，引入Loewner熵（Loewner entropy）概念用于有色噪声（colored noise）环境下的正则系综（canonical ensemble）估计。

Result: 成功推导出由Loewner演化驱动的非线性广义Langevin方程，并在共形变换框架下重新表述了两种不同类型的涨落-耗散关系（FDR）。数值仿真结果显示，两种FDR对应的能量耗散具有共同的标度律（scaling law）。

Conclusion: 共形变换与Loewner演化理论能够有效扩展非平衡统计力学方法，为理解具有复杂几何背景的随机动力学系统（如细胞迁移）提供新的数学工具；Loewner熵在有色噪声环境下对正则系综（canonical ensemble）的估计亦具有理论适用性。

Abstract: In this study, the formal derivation of a one-dimensional nonlinear generalized Langevin equation is demonstrated using a decomposition method based on the conformal transformation governed by the chordal Loewner equation. Here, we used a modified Mori-Zwanzig method whose operator is substituted by that is derived from the discrete Loewner evolution. By this approach, the different types of fluctuation-dissipation relation (FDR) were reformulated using mathematical terms affected by the conformal maps. Dealing with a memory kernel that models the cell migration experiment, the numerical simulation was performed to obtain the specific scaling law of energy dissipation that is common among the two obtained types of FDRs. In addition, the concept of Loewner entropy is used for the estimation of the canonical ensemble in the colored noise environment throughout the theoretical analyses.

</details>


### [67] [The nonequilibrium statistical mechanics of Markov interacting particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13391)
*Dalton A R Sakthivadivel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究耦合随机系统（coupled stochastic systems）中边界变量（boundary variables）导致路径条件律（conditional law of histories）因子分解的条件，通过Radon–Nikodym导数、Girsanov定理、Föllmer熵恒等式及条件互信息（conditional mutual information）等工具，为边界屏蔽（boundary screening）、路径似然推断及非平衡统计物理中的信息热力学价值提供统一语言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核心动机是理解耦合随机系统中边界变量何时使路径条件律（conditional law of histories）满足因子分解性质，以及这种路径空间上的结构如何被对数似然、Girsanov测度变换和非平衡统计物理中的信息论量所检测。

Method: 以路径空间上的正则条件概率（regular conditional probability）为基本对象，在钳制参考律（clamped reference laws）支配下，将边界性质转化为Radon–Nikodym导数的乘性分离或路径对数似然的加性分离。对于Itō扩散，利用Girsanov定理计算对数似然，其期望即为Föllmer熵恒等式（Föllmer entropy identity）和薛定谔桥（Schrödinger bridge）随机控制表述中的二次控制能量（quadratic control energy）。当精确因子分解不成立时，用条件互信息（conditional mutual information）——即真实边界条件化路径律与其条件边缘乘积之间的相对熵——度量剩余耦合。

Result: 建立了边界屏蔽、路径似然推断、路径律的控制改变以及互信息的热力学价值之间的统一框架。当因子分解成立时，边界性质表现为Radon–Nikodym导数的乘性分离等价于路径对数似然的加性分离；当因子分解失效时，条件互信息量化了耦合强度。

Conclusion: 该框架为耦合随机系统中边界变量的角色提供了统一的数学语言，衔接了边界屏蔽、路径似然推断、受控路径律变化以及非平衡统计物理中互信息的热力学价值等不同研究方向。

Abstract: We consider coupled stochastic systems decomposed into exterior, boundary, and interior variables, with the boundary variables sometimes carrying the directed structure of a sensor and actuator. The central question is when the conditional law of histories factorises, and how this path space statement is detected by log likelihoods, by Girsanov changes of measure, and by information theoretic quantities used in nonequilibrium statistical physics. The basic object is a regular conditional probability on a path space. Under domination by clamped reference laws, the boundary property becomes multiplicative separation of a Radon--Nikodym derivative, or equivalently additive separation of a path log likelihood. For Itō diffusions this log likelihood is computed by Girsanov's theorem; its expectation is the quadratic control energy appearing in the Föllmer entropy identity and in the stochastic control formulation of Schrödinger bridge problems. When exact factorisation fails, the remaining coupling is measured by conditional mutual information, namely the relative entropy between the true boundary-conditioned path law and the product of its conditional marginals. This gives a common language for boundary screening, path likelihood inference, controlled changes of path law, and the thermodynamic value of mutual information.

### [68] [An exactly solvable macroscopic fluctuation theory of single-file diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14073)
*Sandeep Jangid,Soumyabrata Saha,Kapil Sharma,Jitendra Kethepalli,Benjamin Guiselin,Jacopo De Nardis,Tridib Sadhu*

TL;DR: 本文证明扩展布朗硬棒（Brownian hard rods, BHR）气体的宏观涨落理论（macroscopic fluctuation theory, MFT）可通过正则变换（canonical transformation）精确求解，并计算了示踪粒子位置和积分电流的大偏差统计（large-deviation statistics），同时将该方法推广至有限体积排斥的晶格气体模型，并通过稀有事件模拟验证了结果。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 通过正则变换，成功获得了连续布朗硬棒气体及有限体积排斥晶格气体在两种系综下的示踪粒子与电流的大偏差统计；稀有事件模拟（rare-event simulations）的结果与理论预测一致，验证了该方法的正确性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，扩展布朗硬棒气体的宏观涨落理论可通过正则变换精确求解，且该方法可推广至晶格气体模型。这为单文件扩散系统的涨落统计提供了统一的分析框架。

Abstract: Single-file diffusion is a ubiquitous phenomenon in low-dimensional systems, arising in transport inside narrow channels. Its natural continuum model is a one-dimensional gas of extended Brownian hard rods (BHR). Perhaps owing to the perceived intractability of this problem, much of the literature has traditionally focused on lattice exclusion models, where integrability methods have yielded remarkable, albeit limited, exact results. A major recent advance comes from a formal solution of macroscopic fluctuation theory (MFT) for the exclusion process. Yet, despite the formal solution, only a handful of properties have been made explicit. We show that the corresponding MFT of the extended BHR gas is in fact exactly solvable through a canonical transformation. We demonstrate this by explicit computation of the large-deviation statistics of the tracer-position and integrated-current in both annealed and quenched ensembles. We further show that an analogous canonical transformation applies to the MFT of lattice gases with finite-volume exclusion, yielding corresponding tracer and current statistics. We validate our results using rare-event simulations for both the continuum and the lattice models.

Method: 采用随机几何图（random geometric graph）限制投票者动力学（voter dynamics）的相互作用范围；当局部重连（local rewiring）不可行时，删除不协调边（discordant link）。通过动力学和结构可观测量（dynamical and structural observables）对系统进行分析。

Abstract: We investigate a spatially constrained coevolving nonlinear voter model. Using a random geometric graph, we constrain the interaction range of voter dynamics. If local rewiring is not possible, the discordant link is deleted. Our results reveal absorbing states that differ not only in magnetization and activity, but also in mean degree and spatial state organization. By exploring dynamical and structural observables, we found that distinct regimes from the existing coevolving nonlinear voter model are characterized by a reduced consensus region, spatially segregated fragmentation, and isolated node formation. Additionally, we develop a phenomenological description of the evolution of the mean degree and terminal non-conserved quantities that is consistent with the numerical results. Our model highlights how local geometric accessibility reshapes the structure of the absorbing states.

### [70] [Cooling rate and glassy behavior in the Fermi--Pasta--Ulam system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13833)
*Matteo Razza,Andrea Carati,Luigi Galgani*

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究Fermi–Pasta–Ulam（FPU）系统在与冷却气体接触时的冷却过程。研究发现弱随机阈值导致FPU系统偏离平衡态，在温度趋近于零时系统仍保留残余能量，且该能量与系统尺寸和冷却速率呈幂律标度关系：E₀ ∼ (ξN)^{2/3}。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，将FPU系统置于温度T以冷却速率ξ降低的气体环境中，通过数值计算观测系统的冷却过程及能量变化。

Result: 在弱随机阈值以下，FPU系统的比能（specific energy）高于其温度，系统偏离平衡态。温度T → 0时系统保留有限残余能量E₀，且该能量与系统尺寸N和冷却速率ξ满足幂律标度关系：E₀ ∼ (ξN)^{2/3}。

Conclusion: 弱随机阈值对FPU系统的冷却过程具有显著影响，导致系统在低温下无法达到热平衡而残留能量。残余能量的幂律标度行为揭示了系统尺寸与冷却速率之间的耦合关系。

Abstract: In this work, we numerically studied the cooling process of a Fermi--Pasta--Ulam system, which occurs when the FPU system is placed in contact with a gas whose temperature $T$ is reduced with a certain cooling rate $ξ$. It was found that the existence of a weak stochastic threshold has a significant impact on the cooling process, because below such a stochastic threshold the specific FPU energy is larger than its temperature, i.e., the FPU system falls out of equilibrium. The difference remains finite in the limit $T \to 0$, so that the FPU system maintains a residual amount of energy $E_0$ at vanishing temperature. Our numerical simulations reveal that this energy exhibits a power--law dependence on both the system size and the cooling rate, scaling approximately as $E_{0} \sim (ξN)^{2/3}$.

### [71] [Modified Family-Vicsek Scaling and Probability Distributions for Brownian Castle Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13922)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引入并验证一种新的界面生长模型“布朗城堡（Brownian Castle, BC）”，探索其是否属于不同于传统弹道沉积的崭新普适类（universality class）。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，对BC界面的宽度进行标度分析，测量生长指数（growth exponent）β与粗糙度指数（roughness exponent）α；并分析界面高度的概率分布以及高度变化的概率分布。

Result: 发现BC界面的宽度呈现修正的Family-Vicsek标度性质，β=0.470±0.012，α=1.01±0.018；短时间尺度上存在依赖于系统尺寸的修正标度行为。高度分布显著偏离高斯分布，高度变化分布符合柯西-洛伦兹（Cauchy-Lorentz）形式，表明过程中存在较大跳跃。

Conclusion: 布朗城堡模型定义了一个全新的普适类，其标度行为与高度统计特征均区别于现有模型，为界面生长领域提供了新的研究方向。

Abstract: The Brownian Castle is a new interface growth model that is a variation on the well-known ballistic deposition model that results in an entirely new universality class. We present numerical verification that the interface width for BC interfaces displays modified Family-Vicsek scaling properties up to finite size corrections. Specifically, we find a growth exponent of $β=0.470 \pm 0.012$ and a roughness exponent of $α=1.01 \pm 0.018$. The scaling is modified at short times with a size scaling exponent that described the early time dependence of interface width on length. The probability distribution of heights for the BC interface shows significant deviations from simple Gaussian behavior and the probability distribution of height changes shows a Cauchy-Lorentz form consistent with expectations for a process involving relatively large jumps.

</details>

### [72] [Robust topological oscillators govern a tunable phase transition to synchronized circadian rhythms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13322)

Result: 发现了一个仅由单振荡子相干性决定的同步化相变；在该相变的上方和下方，系统表现出不同的标度性质。该机制能够解释多个已有实验结果，并预测外部变化可通过提高单振荡子相干性的补偿性变化得到抵消。

Conclusion: 研究表明，随机振荡子的同步存在一种由单振荡子相干性调控的相变机制，并呈现尺度依赖的标度行为；这揭示了从随机单振荡子到鲁棒集体节律之间的一条可调谐（tunable）路径。

Abstract: While synchronization has been well-studied in deterministic oscillators, most underlying oscillators are stochastic in both natural and man-made systems. Yet, the effects of intrinsic stochasticity remain poorly understood. Here, we develop a new mechanism for synchronizing circadian KaiC molecules that have topologically protected cycles. We find a phase transition to synchronization that depends only on the single-oscillator coherence, across a range of molecular changes that determine this coherence. Examining both mesoscopic and macroscopic numbers relevant for cellular and in vitro conditions respectively, we find different scaling properties above and below the phase transition. Our results shed light on several existing experiments and further predict that external changes can be offset by compensatory changes that improve the single-oscillator coherence - demonstrating a tunable pathway between stochastic single oscillators and their robust collective rhythms.
