### [73] [Confinement effects on protein stability in a freezing water environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13966)
*Yanis R. Espinosa,H. Ariel Alvarez,C. Manuel Carlevaro*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本研究利用分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，显式地模拟冰 Ih 的形成，分析了酵母 frataxin（Yfh1）蛋白在其水环境结晶过程中的构象动力学。结果表明，溶剂结晶将蛋白的构象空间从连续、高度连通的液体态重塑为离散的受限态；冰的形成通过几何约束限制了构象采样，但同时保留了甚至增密了界面水化层，揭示了水结构是冷冻条件下蛋白稳定性的关键决定因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蛋白质在低温下的行为是生物物理学（biophysics）的核心问题，直接影响冷变性（cold denaturation）和低温保存（cryopreservation）。尽管过冷液态中的冷变性已被广泛研究，但嵌入生长冰晶格中的蛋白质行为在实验中几乎无法触及。

Method: 使用显式模拟冰 Ih 形成的分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，以四个独立的冰种复制（ice-seeded replica）和液态水对照，在三个温度下表征 Yfh1 的构象动力学。通过溶剂密度、势能和局部键序参数（local bond-order parameters, W4, W6）验证固-液相变，并采用主成分分析（PCA）、二面角主成分分析（dPCA）及自由能地貌（free-energy landscape）分析构象空间。

Result: 溶剂的结晶将蛋白的构象空间从连续、高连通态重塑为以受限态为主的离散地貌；溶剂可及表面积（SASA）、回转半径（radius of gyration）和氢键分析表明，第一壳层水保持液态但其表面密度在冷冻下增加，同时构象采样收缩。

Conclusion: 蛋白质在低温下的行为并非仅由温度决定，而是受周围水的结构组织调控。冰形成通过施加几何约束限制构象采样，同时保留并增密界面水化层，突出了水结构作为冷冻条件下蛋白稳定性决定因素的作用。

Abstract: Understanding how proteins behave at low temperatures remains a central challenge in biophysics, with direct implications for cold denaturation and cryopreservation. While cold denaturation of proteins in the supercooled liquid regime has been studied extensively, the behavior of a protein embedded in a growing ice lattice remains largely inaccessible to experiments. Here we use molecular dynamics simulations that explicitly capture ice Ih formation to characterize the conformational dynamics of yeast frataxin (Yfh1) as its aqueous environment crystallizes. Using four independent ice-seeded replicas and liquid-water controls at three temperatures, we first validate the liquid-solid transition through convergent changes in solvent density, potential energy, and local bond-order parameters (W4, W6). Principal component analysis (PCA), dihedral PCA (dPCA), and free-energy landscapes then reveal that crystallization of the solvent markedly reshapes the accessible conformational space, shifting it from a continuous, highly connected regime in liquid water toward a discretized landscape dominated by confined states. Complementary analyses of solvent-accessible surface area (SASA), radius of gyration, and hydrogen bonding indicate a solvent-driven reorganization of protein-water interactions: although first-shell water remains liquid-like, its surface density increases under freezing, while conformational sampling contracts. Together, these results indicate that protein behavior at low temperatures is governed not by temperature alone but by the structural organization of the surrounding water. By imposing geometrical constraints on the solvent, ice formation restricts conformational sampling while preserving -- and even densifying -- the interfacial hydration layer, highlighting the role of water structure as a determinant of protein stability under freezing conditions.

</details>

### [74] [Neural-Accelerated Bayesian Calibration of Chiral Mean-Field Models to Nuclear Saturation and Vacuum Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13268)
*Isaac Legred,Mateus Reinke Pelicer,Veronica Dexheimer,Jacquelyn Noronha-Hostler,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一个基于神经网络加速的贝叶斯推断框架，用于校准手征核相互作用模型参数，发现可行参数解稀少但分布广泛，且不同饱和相容模型会给出定性的致密核物质与中子星描述差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征核相互作用模型（chiral models of nuclear interactions）虽是描述致密物质的重要唯象工具，但其拉格朗日参数（Lagrangian parameters）难以标定，原因包括：这些模型并非受控有效理论（controlled effective theories）；重复模型评估计算成本高昂；大多数参数选择无法再现核饱和性质（saturation properties）或真空中的强子质量（hadron masses）。

Method: 开发一个贝叶斯推断框架（Bayesian inference framework），通过神经网络代理近似（neural-network surrogate approximation）加速从模型参数到可观测量（nuclear and particle observables）的重复映射。该框架基于MUSES计算引擎、Bilby推断库和PyTorch机器学习工具包，并应用于具有新型广义四次矢量自相互作用项（generalized quartic vector self-interaction sector）的手征平均场模型（chiral mean-field model）。

Result: 可行参数解在参数空间中罕见但分布广泛；数据对耦合组合（combinations of couplings）的约束强于对单个拉格朗日参数（individual Lagrangian parameters）的约束。由此产生的简并性（degeneracies）意味着不同饱和相容模型（saturation-compatible models）会给出定性的致密核物质描述差异，进而影响中子星（neutron stars）的预测。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，仅依赖核饱和性质与真空约束仍无法唯一确定模型参数，强调了结合地面实验（terrestrial experiments）与天体物理信息（astrophysical information）的必要性。

Abstract: Chiral models of nuclear interactions provide approximate, phenomenological descriptions of dense matter that respect the symmetries of quantum chromodynamics. Their Lagrangian parameters, however, are difficult to calibrate because these models are not controlled effective theories. Furthermore, repeated model evaluations are computationally expensive, and most parameter choices fail to reproduce acceptable saturation properties or hadron masses in vacuum. To address this, we develop a Bayesian inference framework to identify parameter regions consistent with nuclear saturation properties and vacuum experimental constraints. We implement this framework through a neural-network surrogate approximation that accelerates the repeated mapping from model parameters to nuclear and particle observables. Our fully-modular, neural-accelerated Bayesian framework interfaces the open-source MUSES Calculation Engine, the Bilby inference library, and the PyTorch machine-learning toolkit. We then apply the framework to the chiral mean-field model with a new generalized quartic vector self-interaction sector. We find that viable solutions are rare but broadly distributed within certain regions of parameter space, with the data constraining combinations of couplings more strongly than individual Lagrangian parameters. The resulting degeneracies imply that distinct saturation-compatible models can lead to qualitatively different descriptions of dense nuclear matter and, thus, of neutron stars, highlighting the need to combine terrestrial and astrophysical information.

</details>


### [75] [Lorentz-Covariant Spectral Bounds from Thermal Quantum Field Theory: Retarded Green's Functions, Kubo Relations, and Holographic Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13482)
*Alisher Sanetullaev,Sarbinaz Bazarbaeva,Marhabo Beymamatova,Shokir Tursunov*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文将从线性化经典动力学扩展至热量子场论（thermal QFT）框架，基于谱函数（spectral function）的解析性与正定性、洛伦兹协变性及KMS条件，推导出非流体力学准正态模（quasinormal spectrum）在复频率平面上的严格边界，并证明该边界由静止系谱权重与最大群速度唯一确定。在AdS/CFT对偶的全息理论中，通过准正规模计算验证了该边界，并发现引导极点随洛伦兹增压（boost）深入复平面——松弛率增大，而非时间膨胀所预期的减速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有洛伦兹协变松弛界（Lorentz-covariant relaxation bounds）仅在经典线性化动理学与流变学理论中建立，尚缺乏在完整量子场论框架下的第一性原理推导。论文旨在填补这一空白，为强关联量子系统（如夸克-胶子等离子体、中子星超流态、量子临界电子液体）提供非微扰的普适光谱约束。

Method: 直接利用有限温度与密度下的推迟两点关联函数（retarded two-point function），结合谱函数的解析性与正定性（analyticity and positivity）、洛伦兹协变性（Lorentz covariance）以及KMS条件（Kubo–Martin–Schwinger condition），推导非流体动力学奇点在复频率平面中的帧依赖约束。同时在全息对偶框架下，于渐近反德西特时空（asymptotically anti-de Sitter spacetime）中进行准正规模（quasinormal mode）的显式计算验证。

Result: 证明了任意增压参考系中非流体力学准正规模谱被限制在一条带状区域内，带宽由静止系零空间动量的谱权重与理论的最大群速度（maximal group velocity）唯一决定。推导了谱密度（spectral density）在洛伦兹增压下的协变求和规则（covariant sum rules），并建立了流体力学梯度展开（hydrodynamic gradient expansion）收敛半径与静止系数据的变换关系。全息计算确认：引导增压极点随速度增大深入复平面（松弛率增大），全程满足该界限；进一步给出了高阶导数引力修正项。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了热量子场论中洛伦兹协变光谱约束的非微扰第一性原理推导，适用于夸克-胶子等离子体、中子星超流相及量子临界点附近强关联电子系统，并为这些系统在任意参考系中的非平衡动力学给出了严格的普适性边界条件。

Abstract: We extend the recently established framework of Lorentz-covariant relaxation bounds from linearized classical kinetic and rheological theories to the full quantum setting of thermal quantum field theory (QFT). Working directly with retarded two-point functions at finite temperature and density, we show that the analyticity and positivity properties of spectral functions -- combined with Lorentz covariance and the Kubo--Martin--Schwinger (KMS) condition -- impose rigorous frame-dependent constraints on the location of singularities in the complex frequency plane. Specifically, we prove that the non-hydrodynamic quasinormal spectrum in any boosted frame is confined to a strip whose width is determined solely by the rest-frame spectral weight at zero spatial momentum and the maximal group velocity of the theory. We derive covariant sum rules for the spectral density under Lorentz boosts and establish that the convergence radius of the hydrodynamic gradient expansion transforms in a manner dictated by the same rest-frame data. In holographic theories dual to Einstein gravity in asymptotically anti-de Sitter spacetime, we verify the bounds by an explicit quasinormal-mode computation: the leading boosted pole moves deeper into the complex plane -- the observed relaxation rate increases with boost velocity, in sharp contrast to naive time dilation -- while respecting the bound throughout; we further derive corrections from higher-derivative gravitational terms. Our results provide a first-principles, non-perturbative derivation of Lorentz-covariant spectral constraints applicable to the quark-gluon plasma, superfluid phases of neutron star matter, and strongly correlated electrons near quantum critical points.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文介绍了JUNO（江门地下中微子观测站）新开发的多信使触发系统（multi-messenger trigger system），该系统相比标准全局触发系统（global trigger system）具有更低的能量阈值和独立监测能力，2025年运行中实现了约110±10 keV的有效能量阈值，并集成了天体物理监测器（astrophysical monitor）和瞬态中微子暴监测器（Transient Neutrino Burst Monitor），可实时监测来自约250 kpc内核心塌缩超新星（core-collapse supernovae）的中微子暴事件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JUNO作为目前质量最大的液体闪烁体中微子探测器（liquid scintillator neutrino detector），其标准全局触发系统在低能事件探测和独立监测能力方面存在局限，因此需要开发一套多信使触发系统以扩展探测能力。

Method: 开发了一个多信使触发系统，该系统通过提供更低能量阈值和独立监测功能扩展了全局触发系统的能力；基于该系统进一步集成了天体物理监测器用于接收和处理来自引力波观测（gravitational-wave observations）等外部信使的警报，以及瞬态中微子暴监测器用于探测短时间尺度的中微子暴事件。

Result: 该系统在2025年运行中实现了约110±10 keV的有效能量阈值，具备进一步降至100 keV以下的潜力，并对约250 kpc距离内的核心塌缩超新星中微子暴具有探测灵敏度。

Conclusion: 多信使触发系统为JUNO提供了更低能量阈值配置和独立监测能力，适用于低能事件分析，并为实时监测瞬态天体物理现象（如超新星中微子暴）提供了有效工具，增强了JUNO作为MeV中微子高精度测量前沿观测站的能力。

Abstract: The Jiangmen Underground Neutrino Observatory (JUNO) is a 20-kiloton liquid scintillator neutrino detector, located 650 meters (1800 m.w.e.) underground in Jiangmen, Guangdong, China. JUNO is primarily designed for reactor neutrino measurements and has been taking data since 2025. With the largest mass of its kind and an excellent energy resolution, JUNO is a leading observatory for high-precision measurements of MeV neutrinos. The standard global trigger system serves as the primary trigger for JUNO. We present a newly developed multi-messenger trigger system that extends the capabilities of the global trigger by providing a lower energy threshold and an independent monitoring capability. During the 2025 operation, it achieved an effective energy threshold of approximately 110 +/- 10 keV, providing a lower threshold configuration suitable for low-energy event analysis. The system shows the potential to further reduce the threshold to well below 100 keV. Based on the multi-messenger trigger system, an astrophysical monitor has been developed to receive and process external alerts from other messengers, such as gravitational-wave observations. A Transient Neutrino Burst Monitor is integrated to detect short-time-scale neutrino burst events and enables real-time monitoring of transient astrophysical phenomena. The system is sensitive to neutrino bursts from core-collapse supernovae within a distance of about 250 kpc.

</details>


### [77] [Measurement of $Ξ^-/\barΞ^{+}$ production in jets from $Z$ boson decays with the DELPHI open data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13804)
*Zhouyue Fan,Yuzhi Che,Xinchou Lou,Zhaoru Zhang,Jinfei Wu,Gengyuan Zhang,Gang Li,Yanping Huang,Manqi Ruan*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于DELPHI合作组1992–1995年收集的320万例Z→强子（hadrons）事件开放数据，首次测量了Z玻色子衰变中能量排序喷注（energy-ranked jets）内的Ξ⁻/Ξ⁺重子产生率与动量谱，并导出胶子喷注与夸克喷注中Ξ⁻/Ξ⁺产生率相对于平均带电粒子多重性的比值R^{Ξ⁻}_{g/q}=1.21±0.18(stat.)±0.26(syst.)，该结果与JETSET模型预期及OPAL合作组对K_S^0和Λ的测量结果在误差内一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ξ⁻/Ξ⁺重子在喷注中的产生过程为研究非微扰量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）中的双奇异度产生（double-strangeness creation）与重子形成机制提供了探针。目前尚缺乏在Z玻色子衰变中针对能量排序喷注内Ξ⁻/Ξ⁺产生的系统测量。

Method: 采用DELPHI合作组1992–1995年采集的320万例Z→强子事件开放数据，利用Durham算法（y_cut=0.005）重建喷注，并通过三喷注事件（three-jet events）中喷注的能量排序获得富夸克喷注（quark-enriched jets）和富胶子喷注（gluon-enriched jets）样本，进而测量能量排序喷注中Ξ⁻/Ξ⁺的平均产生率。

Result: 测量得到胶子喷注与夸克喷注中Ξ⁻/Ξ⁺产生率相对于平均带电粒子多重性的比值R^{Ξ⁻}_{g/q}=1.21±0.18(stat.)±0.26(syst.)，该结果与JETSET模型的预期值以及OPAL合作组对K_S^0和Λ的比值测量结果在不确定度范围内一致。

Conclusion: 本研究首次实现了Z玻色子衰变中能量排序喷注内Ξ⁻/Ξ⁺产生的测量，为双奇异重重子形成的非微扰QCD过程提供了新的实验约束。

Abstract: The $Ξ^{-}/\barΞ^{+}$ baryon production in jets provides a probe of double-strangeness creation and baryon formation in the non-perturbative quantum chromodynamics (QCD) process. This study measures the $Ξ^{-}/\barΞ^{+}$ production rates and momentum spectra in energy-ranked jets using 3.2 million $Z\to\text{hadrons}$ events from the DELPHI open data collected from 1992 to 1995. Jets are reconstructed with the Durham algorithm with $y_{\text{cut}}=0.005$, and quark- and gluon-enriched jet samples are obtained from the energy ordering of jets in three-jet events. The average $Ξ^{-}/\barΞ^{+}$ production in energy-ranked jets are measured. The ratio of $Ξ^{-}/\barΞ^{+}$ production rates in gluon and quark jets relative to the mean charged-particle multiplicity is derived from the measurements. We obtain $R^{Ξ^{-}}{g/q}=1.21\pm0.18\mathrm{(stat.)}\pm0.26\mathrm{(syst.)}$, consistent with the JETSET expectation and the OPAL results for $R^{K_S^0}_{g/q}$ and $R^Λ_{g/q}$ within uncertainties. This study is the first measurement of $Ξ^{-}/\barΞ^{+}$ production in energy-ranked jets in $Z$ boson decays.

</details>


<div id='hep-th'></div>

### [78] [Magic without a phase: phase-independent stabilizer Rényi entropy in gluon scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13134)
*Jinwei Chu,Savan Kharel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将量子计算中的“魔法”（magic，即非稳定子性）概念推广至与相位无关的形式，定义了广义的稳定子Rényi熵（generalized stabilizer Rényi entropy），并将其应用于高能物理中高多重数树级胶子散射过程，发现相位无关的魔法在3→2散射中普遍大于2→2散射的最大值，并在2→3散射的软极限（soft limit）下趋于非零最小值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 魔法（magic）的原始定义依赖于计算基（computational basis）的选择，但在某些物理场景中，可用数据仅能确定该基矢至局部相位（local phase）约定内。因此需要一种与相位无关的魔法表述，以更广泛地适用于此类物理系统。

Method: 将魔法概念推广为相位无关的形式，定义广义的稳定子Rényi熵（generalized stabilizer Rényi entropy）。以高多重数树级胶子散射（higher-multiplicity tree-level gluon scattering）为案例，将出射螺旋度（helicities）解释为量子比特（qubits），螺旋度数据自然确定每个量子比特的局部基矢但保留相位模糊性。

Result: 对于3→2散射，末态相位无关的魔法普遍大于2→2散射所能达到的最大值。对于2→3散射，在软极限（soft limit）下魔法趋近一个非零最小值；当三个出射动量对称时，魔法达到局部最小值，仅比软极限值高出几个百分点。在所有考察情况下，颜色依赖（color dependence）从相位无关的稳定子Rényi熵中抵消。

Conclusion: 所提出的相位无关魔法框架有效消除了局部相位模糊性的影响，并揭示了胶子散射过程中魔法随散射道数和动量配置变化的非平凡行为，为量子信息概念在高能散射问题中的应用提供了新视角。

Abstract: Magic, also known as non-stabilizerness, measures the usefulness of a quantum state for quantum computation. While magic is defined relative to a choice of computational basis, in some physical settings the available data determine this basis only up to local phase conventions. In this paper, we generalize the notion of magic and formulate it in a phase-independent manner, and hence define a generalized stabilizer Rényi entropy. As a case study, we consider higher-multiplicity tree-level gluon scattering, interpreting the outgoing helicities as qubits. In this setting, the helicity data naturally determine a local basis for each qubit but leave a phase ambiguity. For $3\to 2$ scattering, we find that the final-state phase-independent magic is generically larger than the maximum attainable in $2\to 2$ scattering. For $2 \to 3$ scattering, we find a nonzero minimal value approached in the soft limit. Moreover, when the three outgoing momenta become symmetric, the magic approaches a local minimum only a few percent above the soft-limit value. In all cases considered, the color dependence cancels from the phase-independent stabilizer Rényi entropy.

</details>


### [79] [Out-of-time-ordered Correlators in de Sitter Revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13137)
*Alexey Milekhin,Vladimir Narovlansky,Jiuci Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用de Sitter背景下的引力eikonal近似研究标量场的4点超时有序关联子（OTOC），发现树图级Lyapunov指数达到最大值2π/β_dS，但圈图级出现红外问题，导致渐近展开中所有牛顿常数奇次幂消失，且领头阶Lyapunov指数为最大值的两倍；同时发现OTOC在微扰下可增长，这违反了量子混沌上限，且这种增长由引力子传播子中的大微分同胚（large diffeomorphisms）所介导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究de Sitter时空中的量子混沌现象，具体通过标量场的超时有序关联子（out-of-time-ordered correlator, OTOC）在引力微扰框架下的行为，检验量子混沌界限是否在de Sitter背景下依然成立。

Method: 采用eikonal近似描述de Sitter背景下的引力效应；通过将算符缠绕（dressing）到观测者方式实现规范不变定义；在任意维数和任意标量场体质量下进行树图和圈图水平的微扰计算。

Result: 树图水平得到最大Lyapunov指数2π/β_dS；圈图水平存在与引力子传播子矢量部分相关的红外问题；正则化后所有牛顿常数奇次幂在渐近展开中消失，简单算符配置下领头项对应两倍最大Lyapunov指数；微扰OTOC可出现初始增长。

Conclusion: de Sitter空间中的微扰OTOC可在初始阶段增长，这直接违反了量子混沌的界限（quantum bound on chaos）；这种反常增长源于引力子传播子中的大微分同胚效应。

Abstract: We study the 4-point out-of-time-ordered correlator (OTOC) of scalar fields using the eikonal approximation to gravity around a de Sitter background. It can be defined in a gauge-invariant way by dressing the operators to an observer. We consider de Sitter space in any dimension and any bulk masses of the scalar fields. At tree level we find the maximal Lyapunov exponent of $2 π/β_{\rm dS}$. However, we describe an IR problem in this calculation at the loop level associated with the vector part of the graviton propagator. Regularizing this divergence leads to the vanishing of all odd powers in Newton's constant in the asymptotic expansion, so that the leading answer comes with twice the maximal Lyapunov exponent in simple operator configurations. We find that the perturbative OTOC in de Sitter can initially grow, which is not allowed by the quantum bound on chaos. Interestingly, we find that this growth is mediated by large diffeomorphisms in the graviton propagator.

</details>


### [80] [From Fredholm Determinants to AdS/CFT Observables: A Universal Strong-Coupling Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13140)
*Bercel Boldis,Dennis le Plat*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引入倾斜变形（tilted deformation），利用Fredholm行列式与矩阵Bessel核表示，研究了$\mathcal{N}=4$超对称杨-米尔斯理论（supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory）中尖点反常维度（cusp anomalous dimension）和O(6) sigma模型质量间隙（mass gap）在强't Hooft耦合下的trans级数（trans-series）结构与重联结构（resurgence structure），并建立了两个可观测物理量之间的精确全阶关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强耦合区间的非微扰结构在AdS/CFT对偶中隐藏较深，难以直接揭示。本文的动机是通过引入一个可控的变形参数（倾斜），使非微扰标度自然分离，从而系统性地揭示尖点反常维度和O(6)质量间隙在强耦合下的trans级数和重联结构，并建立两者之间的深层联系。

Method: 采用Fredholm行列式（Fredholm determinant）与矩阵Bessel核（matrix Bessel kernel）表示强耦合展开；引入倾斜尖点（tilted cusp）和倾斜质量间隙（tilted mass gap）作为单参数变形，使非微扰尺度自然分离；基于Fredholm行列式表示构建Alien微积分（Alien calculus），从微扰展开直接生成所有非微扰扇区（non-perturbative sectors）。

Result: 确定了O(6)质量间隙在强耦合下的完整trans级数和重联结构；扩展并证明了相继非微扰修正之间猜想的递推关系；通过Alien微积分实现了从微扰展开到所有非微扰扇区的系统性生成；推导了O(6)质量间隙与平面$\mathcal{N}=4$超对称杨-米尔斯理论尖点反常维度在强耦合trans级数间的精确全阶关系。

Conclusion: 倾斜变形是一种有效的理论工具，能够揭示AdS/CFT可观测物理量中隐藏的非微扰结构。O(6)质量间隙与$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM尖点反常维度在强耦合trans级数层面存在深刻的精确对应关系，该发现进一步支持了AdS/CFT对偶中不同可观测物理量之间的统一性。

Abstract: We investigate the trans-series structure of the cusp anomalous dimension of $\mathcal{N}=4$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory and the dynamically generated mass gap of the $\mathrm{O}(6)$ sigma model at strong 't Hooft coupling. We consider the one-parameter deformation of the cusp anomalous dimension, known as the tilted cusp, and review its strong-coupling expansion obtained through its representation in terms of Fredholm determinants with a matrix Bessel kernel. The advantage of this deformation is that the non-perturbative scales separate naturally, revealing structures that remain hidden in the physical limit. Motivated by this observation, we introduce the tilted mass gap, which reduces to the physical $\mathrm{O}(6)$ mass gap at a special value of the deformation parameter and exhibits a deep connection with the tilted cusp. This formulation allows us to determine the complete strong-coupling trans-series and resurgence structure of the $\mathrm{O}(6)$ mass gap, while extending and proving conjectured relations between successive non-perturbative corrections. Building on the underlying Fredholm determinant representation, we construct an Alien calculus that generates all non-perturbative sectors of these AdS/CFT observables directly from their perturbative expansions. Finally, we derive an exact all-orders relation between the strong-coupling trans-series of the $\mathrm{O}(6)$ mass gap and the cusp anomalous dimension of planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory.

</details>


### [81] [Some Remarks on the Spectral Geometry of the Gribov Horizon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13228)
*Daniel G. Tedesco*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个局域谱（local spectral）框架来区分Landau规范Gribov视界上的规范轨道投影与规范固定Hessian算符的退化性。在环面上移除残余全局色核后，约化Faddeev–Popov算符成为轨道范数泛函的标准Morse–Bott Hessian，作者证明了二次型指标定理和谱流跳跃公式，并针对SU(2) hedgehog构型精确确定了稳定性区间 −2<g<1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gribov视界（Gribov horizon）的处理中，规范轨道投影与规范固定Hessian算符退化性之间的区分长期模糊，需要建立严格的局域谱框架来厘清这两者的数学结构与物理后果。

Method: 采用局域谱分析框架，结合Morse–Bott理论（Morse–Bott theory）、仿射焦丛（affine focal pencil）方法、投影Feynman–Hellmann关系以及二次Schur约化（Schur reduction），对Faddeev–Popov算符在Gribov视界附近的谱行为进行刻画。

Result: 在环面上，移除非平凡全局色核（global-color kernel）后，约化Faddeev–Popov算符即为轨道范数泛函的Morse–Bott Hessian；对于仿射焦丛证明了指标定理。在正则孤立穿越点处，临界投影子P和可逆压缩导数Γ决定了谱流跳跃和源鬼预解式（sourced ghost resolvent）的首项Laurent系数；对于简单零点，还给出了壁共法向量（wall conormal）。沿仿射射线从正区域到达的穿越点具有负定Γ，包括对称性保护的多重态。对SU(2) hedgehog构型，在每个耦合自旋-轨道通道中都构造了可归一化的阈值态，并通过全栈极小化获得精确稳定性区间 −2<g<1。

Conclusion: 本文建立的局域谱框架统一了Gribov视界的几何与谱分析，所获得的精确稳定性区间无需数值拟合即可由连续极限直接得到，并且Dirichlet盒谱逼近这些阈值，提供了有限体积比较的可行途径。

Abstract: We develop a local spectral framework for the Landau-gauge Gribov horizon that distinguishes gauge-orbit projection from degeneracy of the gauge-fixing Hessian. On a flat torus, spatially constant ghosts form a residual global-color kernel; after removal of this kernel, the reduced Faddeev--Popov operator is the normal Morse--Bott Hessian of the orbit-norm functional, whereas the covariant Laplacian defines the orthogonal connection. For the associated affine focal pencil, we prove a quadratic-form index theorem with a Morse--Bott endpoint. At a regular isolated crossing, the critical projector $P$ and invertible compressed derivative $Γ=P\dot{\mathcal{M}}P$ determine the spectral-flow jump and leading Laurent coefficient of the sourced ghost resolvent; for a simple zero, they also give the wall conormal. Crossings reached along affine rays from the positive region have negative-definite $Γ$, including symmetry-protected multiplets, while a second Schur reduction determines pole orders along tangential paths. A projected single-harmonic model checks the projected Feynman--Hellmann relation. For an $SU(2)$ hedgehog on $\mathbb R^3$, we construct a normalizable threshold state in every coupled spin--orbit channel and minimize over the full tower to obtain the exact stability interval $-2<g<1$. Dirichlet-box spectra approach these thresholds and serve as finite-volume comparisons; no numerical fit enters the continuum result.

</details>


### [82] [Worldline representation of multiloop amplitudes in quantum electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13321)
*Victor M. Banda Guzmán,Uwe Müller,Cristofer Nava Jacuinde,Christian Schubert,Carlos J. Servin Tomas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 综述了世界线方法（worldline approach）在量子电动力学（QED）多圈计算中的应用，重点介绍了近期在标量QED双圈真空极化（vacuum polarisation）计算中取得的进展及相关主积分公式（master integral formulas）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在将世界线方法（worldline approach）——一种能一次性整合大量费曼图（Feynman diagrams）的积分表示技术——应用于实际的多圈（multiloop）计算，解决传统费曼图方法在圈数增加时计算量爆炸的问题。

Method: 采用世界线方法（worldline approach）构建积分表示，对标量QED（scalar QED）和旋量QED（spinor QED）中的真空极化函数（vacuum polarization functions）以及电子反常磁矩（electron anomalous magnetic moment）进行计算。近期工作聚焦于标量QED的双圈真空极化（two-loop vacuum polarisation）及其相关的主积分公式（master integral formulas）。

Result: 完成了标量QED中双圈真空极化（two-loop vacuum polarisation）的计算，并得到了一些在此过程中获得的主积分公式（master integral formulas）。

Conclusion: 世界线方法（worldline approach）有潜力简化多圈QED计算，但仍面临非标准数学挑战（non-standard mathematical challenges），当前进展表明该方法在双圈层面已取得具体成果。

Abstract: The worldline approach to quantum electrodynamics allows one to construct integral representations combining large numbers of Feynman diagrams. Here I review the state-of-the-art of a long-term effort to make this fact useful for actual multiloop calculations, such as of the scalar and spinor QED vacuum polarization functions and the electron anomalous magnetic moment. After a short historical introduction, and a discussion of the non-standard mathematical challenges involved, I focus on a recent calculation of the two-loop vacuum polarisation in scalar QED and some master integral formulas obtained in this context.

</details>


### [83] [An adaptive inverse-problem framework for one-loop five-gluon BCJ numerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13412)
*Lin Mai,Yaobo Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文形式化地提出了BCJ分子构造（Bern–Carrasco–Johansson numerator construction）作为一个精确的自适应逆问题（exact adaptive inverse problem），并通过四点和一环五胶子纯杨-米尔斯理论（pure Yang–Mills theory）的具体算例展示了该方法从规范设定、矩阵编译、解纤维分类到验证测试的完整流程，最终成功重构了已知的分子并生成了独立可验证的检验结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 逆问题（inverse problem）在物理中广泛存在，但如何系统性地将BCJ分子构造转化为一个数学结构清晰、可自适应修改的逆问题框架仍缺乏形式化描述。本文旨在建立这一框架，使分子系数的重构、解空间的分类和验证过程具备确定性和可扩展性。

Method: 本文将BCJ分子构造编译为三元组$\mathcal{P}_σ=(A,b;\mathcal{S};\mathcal{T})$，其中方程$Ax=b$重构分子系数，$\mathcal{S}$对解纤维（solution fiber）进行分类，$\mathcal{T}$在留出信息上进行验证。左零空间（left-null）的障碍识别候选分子基方向，候选测量在右零空间（right kernel）上的作用识别信息性的新切割方程。方法在四点手动演示，并应用于一环五胶子纯杨-米尔斯理论。

Result: 经过运动学和图对称性约化后，候选分子基包含1127个独立坐标；最大割、盒割、三角割和对割联合秩为920，得到207维仿射解纤维。指定的$R_{12345}$颜色环读取$\mathcal{S}$湮灭所有核方向，整个纤维对应单一可观测量类。已有的前极限分子（forward-limit numerator）位于此纤维内，新切割、独立积分约化和螺旋度振幅基准验证了结果。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个确定性的BCJ分子构造逆问题框架，能够精确编译、评估和验证分子解空间。该框架支持显式的搜索规则和智能体接口以提出修订，具有自适应性。实验结果验证了方法的正确性与可复用性。

Abstract: An inverse problem comprises a matrix equation together with its unknown space, physical data, equivalence relation, and validation tests. We formulate Bern--Carrasco--Johansson (BCJ) numerator construction as an exact adaptive inverse problem. A fixed scientific specification determines the theory, graph conventions, coefficient field, locality and power counting, cut data, observable equivalence, and independent checks. Each finite working specification compiles to $\mathcal{P}_σ=(A,b;\mathcal{S};\mathcal{T})$, where $Ax=b$ reconstructs numerator coefficients, $\mathcal{S}$ classifies the solution fiber, and $\mathcal{T}$ tests it on held-out information. Left-null obstructions identify candidate numerator-basis directions needed for consistency, while the action of candidate measurements on the right kernel identifies informative new cut equations. We illustrate these steps by hand at four points and apply them to one-loop five-gluon pure Yang--Mills theory. After kinematic and graph-symmetry reduction, the candidate numerator basis contains 1127 independent coordinates. The combined maximal, box, triple, and double cuts have rank 920, giving a 207-dimensional affine solution fiber. Exact reconstruction determines a particular solution and the complete ordered kernel. The specified $R_{12345}$ color-ring readout $\mathcal{S}$ annihilates every kernel direction, so the full fiber represents one observable class. A published forward-limit numerator lies in this fiber, and fresh cuts, independent integral reductions, and helicity-amplitude benchmarks validate the result. Explicit search rules and agent interfaces can propose revisions. Deterministic compilation and exact evaluation assess each proposal.

</details>


### [84] [Kink collisions in a two-dimensional gravity model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13620)
*Zhen-Tao He,Yuan Zhong*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了自引力φ⁴模型中的扭结-反扭结碰撞，该模型耦合了Mann等人提出的二维膨胀引力理论。研究发现引力改变了散射结构：随着引力耦合系数κ增大，共振窗口向更高初始速度移动并变窄，临界逃逸速度轻微上升。碰撞后共形因子减小，表明局部空间尺度收缩，且在所有模拟中里奇标量保持有限，未发现时空奇点形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自引力φ⁴模型中扭结-反扭结碰撞的动力学行为，探究引力效应对散射结构的影响，并检验该二维模型中是否会出现高维厚膜碰撞中常见的时空奇点。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，扫描不同引力耦合系数κ下的初始速度，并结合线性扰动分析（linear perturbation analysis）研究共振激发的性质。模型基于Mann等人提出的二维膨胀引力理论（dilaton gravity theory）。

Result: 引力使共振窗口（resonance windows）向更高初始速度移动并变窄，临界逃逸速度（critical escape velocity）随κ增大而轻微上升。弱引力区域可能存在长寿命共振激发。碰撞后共形因子（conformal factor）减小，表明局部空间尺度收缩；里奇标量（Ricci scalar）出现瞬态峰值但保持有限。

Conclusion: 与高维厚膜碰撞不同，该二维模型在模拟中未发现时空奇点形成的证据。几何响应表现为碰撞后局部空间尺度的收缩，且该效应随引力耦合增强而加剧。

Abstract: We numerically study kink-antikink collisions in the self-gravitating $φ^4$ model coupled to the two-dimensional dilaton gravity theory proposed by Mann et al. The static kink solutions interpolate between an anti-de Sitter (AdS$_2$) region and a Minkowski region, and can be regarded as two-dimensional analogues of certain thick branes. By scanning the initial velocity for several gravitational couplings, we find that gravity modifies the scattering structure: the resonance windows shift toward higher initial velocities and become progressively narrower as the coupling $κ$ increases, while the critical escape velocity increases mildly. A linear perturbation analysis further indicates possible long-lived resonant excitations in the weak-gravity regime, which may be associated with the persistence of bounce windows. The collisions further produce a clear geometrical response: the conformal factor decreases after the collision, corresponding to a contraction of the local proper spatial scale in the conformal gauge, and this effect becomes stronger for larger $κ$. Meanwhile, the Ricci scalar develops transient peaks during kink encounters but remains finite in all simulations considered. Thus, in contrast to higher-dimensional thick-brane collisions, we find no evidence for spacetime singularity formation in this two-dimensional model.

</details>


### [85] [A de Sitter Anti-Scrambling Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13665)
*Wentao Cui,David K. Kolchmeyer*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究半经典观测者在德西特时空（de Sitter space）中的观测代数，发现时间演化超过 scrambling time 后，KMS 条件、迹性质（trace property）与代数结构均发生根本性变化，对观测者中心的静态块全息（observer-centric static patch holography）构成挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨德西特时空中半经典观测者代数结构在长时间演化下的行为，特别是冲击波散射（shockwave scattering）对出时间序关联函数（OTOC）及相关代数性质的影响，并评估其对观测者中心全息框架的挑战。

Method: 通过将观测者时钟分别作为经典变量和量子变量处理，利用冲击波散射修正的出时间序关联函数（OTOC）分析时间推进效应（time advance effect），并结合德西特 JT 引力（de Sitter JT gravity）的经典含冲击解进行说明。

Result: 经典时钟下，时间推进效应导致真空关联函数的 KMS 条件（KMS condition）失效；量子时钟下，Hartle-Hawking 态在叉积代数（crossed-product algebra）上不构成迹（trace）。观测者代数的交换子（commutant）推测为平凡。当算符时间间隔超过 scrambling time 时，OTOC 衰减至零，并出现自由积代数（free product algebra）。

Conclusion: 长时间演化后观测者代数结构发生显著改变，这对观测者中心的静态块全息提出了挑战，可能意味着该全息框架在时间尺度超过 scrambling time 时需要修正或重新解释。

Abstract: We study the algebra of observables of a semiclassical observer in de Sitter space. When operators are time-evolved by a scrambling time, out-of-time-ordered correlation functions (OTOCs) receive corrections due to shockwave scattering near the cosmological horizon. When the observer's clock is treated classically, we show that the time advance effect implies the breakdown of the KMS condition for vacuum correlators of matter operators. When the observer's clock is quantized, this implies that the Hartle-Hawking state is not a trace on the resulting crossed-product algebra. We conjecture that the observer's algebra has a trivial commutant. When the time separation between operators exceeds the scrambling time, the OTOC decays to zero and a free product algebra emerges. We illustrate this using classical solutions of de Sitter JT gravity with shocks. We comment on how our results pose a challenge for observer-centric static patch holography.

</details>

### [87] [An exact algorithm for U(N) matrix models in the gauge-invariant singlet sector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13725)
*Enrico M. Brehm,Jean Cazalis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种精确算法，用于计算玻色型U(N)矩阵模型（bosonic U(N) matrix model）中规范不变单态（gauge-invariant singlet sector）的可观测物理量。该算法基于Schur多项式（Schur polynomials）和限制性Schur多项式（restricted Schur polynomials）的正交基，通过群论约化将哈密顿矩阵元化简为对称群子群的陪集（cosets）与双陪集（double cosets）上的特征标和（character sums），所得矩阵元为关于规范群秩N的闭式多项式（closed-form polynomials），可预计算并重复使用。一矩阵实现通过精确映射到N个无相互作用费米子（non-interacting fermions）进行验证，展示了低能谱随截断的快速收敛。多矩阵扩展的主要瓶颈在于对称群限制性特征标（restricted characters）的计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矩阵模型是M理论（M-theory）和D膜动力学（D-brane dynamics）的基本描述；通过规范/引力对偶（gauge/gravity duality），其规范不变的（gauge-invariant）单态（singlet）部分描述了全息对偶中的纯引力自由度（gravitational degrees of freedom）。现有方法难以精确处理有限N、有限耦合下的规范不变态动力学，特别是在非平面（non-planar）区域。

Method: 采用Schur多项式（单矩阵）和限制性Schur多项式（多矩阵）构成的正交基，该基对角化自由哈密顿量，并通过激发数（excitation number）提供希尔伯特空间的自然截断（truncation）。相互作用哈密顿量或任何规范不变可观测量的矩阵元，通过群论约化（group-theoretic reduction）归约为对称群子群的陪集与双陪集，以及对称群上的特征标和。所得结果为规范群秩N的闭式多项式，由预计算的群论数据组装而成，可对任意N和耦合常数复用。

Result: 一矩阵实现通过与N个无相互作用费米子的精确映射进行验证，低能谱随截断快速收敛。多矩阵扩展已概述，其主要瓶颈在于对称群限制性特征标的计算——目前尚缺乏可与Murnaghan–Nakayama规则（Murnaghan–Nakayama rule）相媲美的算法。

Conclusion: 该框架能直接获取有限N、有限耦合下规范不变态的动力学，为全息矩阵模型（holographic matrix models）的非平面区域（non-planar regime）开辟了新的计算窗口。

Abstract: Matrix models appear as fundamental descriptions of M-theory and D-brane dynamics, and via the gauge/gravity duality their gauge-invariant, or singlet, sector describes the purely gravitational degrees of freedom in the holographic dual. We present a new exact algorithm for computing observables of bosonic U(N) matrix models in the gauge-invariant singlet sector. This sector is spanned by an orthogonal basis of Schur polynomials (for a single matrix) and restricted Schur polynomials (for multiple matrices), which diagonalizes the free Hamiltonian and provides a natural truncation of the Hilbert space by excitation number. Matrix elements of the interaction Hamiltonian, or any gauge-invariant observable, are evaluated through a group-theoretic reduction to cosets and double cosets of suitable subgroups of the symmetric group, together with character sums on the symmetric group. The resulting entries are closed-form polynomials in the gauge-group rank N, assembled from group-theoretic data that are precomputed once and can be reused for any N and any coupling constants. We validate the one-matrix implementation against the exact mapping to N non-interacting fermions, demonstrating rapid convergence of the low-lying spectrum with the cutoff. The multi-matrix extension is outlined; its main bottleneck is the computation of restricted characters of the symmetric group, for which no algorithm comparable to the Murnaghan--Nakayama rule is currently known. The framework gives direct access to finite-N, finite-coupling dynamics of gauge-invariant states and opens a new computational window on the non-planar regime of holographic matrix models.

### [88] [Horizon Microstructure Thermodynamics in AdS Black Holes: Smarr-Consistent Excitation Enthalpy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13824)
*Juan Diego Haro,Ernesto Medina,Bertrand Berche,Pedro Bargueño,Ernesto Contreras*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将四维AdS黑洞的视界分解为微观位点（microscopic sites），利用部分占据位点的组合计数直接导出黑洞熵，包括Bekenstein-Hawking面积律、对数修正及逆面积展开，并从扩展热力学第一定律和Smarr关系为该部分占据图像提供了热力学 justification。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将面积为$A$的视界分解为$\mathcal{N}=A/a_p$个微观位点，其中$N$个位点被占据；通过部分占据位点的组合计数直接得到熵，并在最大熵填充下恢复Bekenstein-Hawking定律（$a_p=4\ln 2\ \ell_{p}^{2}$）。随后构建包含化学势$\mu$的扩展第一定律、Smarr一致的激发焓$\delta M(A,P,N)$以及AdS控制参数$u=PS$来从热力学角度 justify 该部分占据图像。

Result: 在有限填充（finite-filling）区域，熵的主导项正比于视界面积；次领头修正包括一个可减的对数项（subtractive logarithmic term）和一个逆面积展开。扩展热力学框架成功将组合熵识别为视界主导熵，而热力学部分则提供了“外衣”（dressing），用于选择平衡填充并为偏离参考构型赋予有限激发代价。

Conclusion: 提出的视界微观结构方案为黑洞熵的微观推导提供了组合学途径，并且该部分占据区域可通过扩展热力学定律得到自洽的热力学解释，奠定了微观图像与宏观热力学之间的联系。

Abstract: In this work we formulate a horizon-microstructure description of four-dimensional AdS black holes in which a horizon of area $A$ is resolved into $\mathcal{N}=A/a_p$ microscopic sites and $N$ occupied horizon sites. The central result is that the combinatorics of this partially occupied horizon sector yields the entropy directly: in the finite-filling regime the leading term is proportional to the area, and the maximal-entropy filling reproduces the Bekenstein--Hawking law with $a_p=4\ln 2\ \ell_{p}^{2}$. Subleading corrections include a subtractive logarithmic term and an inverse-area expansion. We then show that this partially occupied regime admits a thermodynamic justification from an extended first law with chemical potential $μ$, a Smarr-consistent excitation enthalpy $δM(A,P,N)$, and an AdS control parameter $u=PS$. In this interpretation, the combinatorics provides the dominant horizon entropy, while the thermodynamic sector supplies a dressing that selects the equilibrium filling and assigns a finite excitation cost to departures from a reference partially occupied configuration.

Abstract: We formulate timelike entanglement entropy and its Rényi extension in two-dimensional conformal field theory through the analytic continuation of replica twist correlators to time-ordered, timelike-separated insertions. Within three-dimensional holography, the semiclassical boundary correlator identifies boundary-anchored complex geodesics as the relevant bulk saddles and selects the one with the smallest real part of the length. This provides a direct boundary derivation of the proposed complex extremal surface prescription and extends to Rényi index $n>1$, for which we explicitly construct the corresponding complex cosmic brane geometry in the vacuum. We develop these ideas in several representative settings, including locally and globally excited states and quantum operator quenches, making manifest the precise agreement between boundary twist correlator and bulk complex geodesic calculations. For AdS-Vaidya, our approach predicts a different result from earlier piecewise geodesic constructions, while reproducing the field theory answer. Abstract: Lambert series of the form $\sum_{n>0}a(n)q^n/(1-q^n)$ are ubiquitous in mathematical physics. Resurgence concerns the singular limit as $|q|$ approaches 1. In the Feynman cases we can control this limit, obtaining rapidly convergent expressions, since the Lambert series are iterated integrals of holomorphic Eisenstein series twisted by a character. We generalize this result, to include modular resurgent structures found in topological-string observables.

Motivation: 近期球面路径积分（sphere path integral）的证据支持de Sitter静态斑全息猜想，即包含观测者世界线的欧几里得引力路径积分可计算一个迹。为进一步严格检验该猜想，作者通过在观测者世界线上插入算符，计算两点函数和OTOC来测试其是否满足希尔伯特空间中迹的基本性质。

Method: 采用冲击波形式论（shockwave formalism）扩展了Kolchmeyer和Liu先前的OTOC计算，同时纳入观测者反冲（observer recoil）和引力反作用（gravitational backreaction）效应。

Result: OTOC与希尔伯特空间中迹的循环性（cyclicity）和正定性（positivity）两个基本性质冲突。冲击波几何的信号特征导致扰动eikonal展开的两种不同重求和方法，这两种方法通过循环性相互转换；正定性被违背是因为领头阶扰动贡献导致（正则化后的）OTOC增大。

Conclusion: OTOC与循环性和正定性的冲突表明，将包含观测者世界线的欧几里得引力路径积分解释为迹（trace）的全息对应方案存在根本性问题，需要重新审视de Sitter静态斑全息猜想。

Abstract: We study a version of de Sitter static patch holography in which the Euclidean gravitational path integral, with an observer worldline included, is conjectured to compute a trace. Motivated by recent evidence for this conjecture from the sphere path integral, we test it further by inserting operators along the observer worldline and computing two-point functions and out-of-time-ordered four-point correlators (OTOCs). We extend an earlier OTOC calculation by Kolchmeyer and Liu using the shockwave formalism, incorporating both observer recoil and gravitational backreaction. We find that the OTOC conflicts with two basic properties of a trace in a Hilbert space: cyclicity and positivity. The signaling feature of the shockwave geometry gives rise to two distinct resummations of the perturbative eikonal expansion, which are interchanged by cyclicity. Positivity is violated by the fact that the leading perturbative contribution causes the (regularized) OTOC to increase.

</details>

### [94] [A spinor-adapted geometric approach for nonlinear Dirac systems and its application to a tensorial wave-Dirac system near Minkowski spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13775)
*Seokchang Hong*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文在(1+3)维渐近平坦时空中，研究了一个由Maxwell-Dirac和Einstein-Dirac系统启发的非线性张量波-狄拉克系统（nonlinear tensorial wave-Dirac system），通过建立耦合能量法（coupled energy method）并利用克利福德代数（Clifford algebra）与零分解（null decomposition）的相容性，证明了小数据解的全局存在性（global existence）以及定量加权能量与衰减估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了隔离反对称张量场的零几何（null geometry）与狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）内在一阶几何之间的相互作用，同时避免爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）的导数损失机制（derivative loss mechanism）和麦克斯韦方程（Maxwell equations）的规范结构（gauge structure）。

Method: 保持狄拉克方程在整个非线性论证中的一阶性质；利用狄拉克流（Dirac current）提供基本能量恒等式，通过平方狄拉克算子（squared Dirac operator）产生的波动方程获取定量时空估计；结合积分局部能量衰减估计（integrated local energy decay estimates）与r^p加权能量层级（r^p-weighted energy hierarchies），建立张量和旋量分量的耦合能量法。

Result: 建立了小数据解的全局存在性，并获得了定量加权能量与衰减估计。结合零结构（null structure）与二进论证（dyadic argument），发现如t^{-1/2-δ}的弱衰减（weak decay）足以保证系统的非线性稳定性（nonlinear stability）。

Conclusion: 本文发展的几何思想为更一般的非线性狄拉克系统（包括Maxwell-Dirac和Einstein-Dirac方程）的研究提供了有用的起点。

Abstract: We study a nonlinear tensorial wave-Dirac system on $(1+3)$-dimensional asymptotically flat spacetimes as a semilinear model motivated by the Maxwell-Dirac and Einstein-Dirac systems. The purpose of this model is to isolate the interaction between the null geometry of antisymmetric tensor fields and the intrinsic first-order geometry of the Dirac equation while avoiding the derivative loss mechanism of the Einstein equations and the gauge structure of the Maxwell equations.
  Our analysis preserves the first-order nature of the Dirac equation throughout the nonlinear argument. The Dirac current provides the fundamental energy identity, while quantitative spacetime estimates are obtained from the wave equation arising from the squared Dirac operator. Combining these ingredients with integrated local energy decay estimates and $r^p$-weighted energy hierarchies, we establish a coupled energy method for the tensorial and spinorial components. A key observation is that the Clifford algebra is compatible with the null decomposition of antisymmetric tensor fields and excludes the most singular nonlinear interactions.
  As a consequence, we establish the global existence of small-data solutions together with quantitative weighted energy and decay estimates. Remarkably, combining the null structure with dyadic argument, weak decay such as $t^{-\frac12-δ}$ is sufficient to obtain nonlinear stability of the system, in the spirit of \cite{DHRT}.
  We expect that the geometric ideas developed in this paper provide a useful starting point for the study of more general nonlinear Dirac systems, including the Maxwell-Dirac and Einstein-Dirac equations.

### [95] [On multipoles, their decomposition by time-reversal symmetry, and the electric toroidal monopole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13053)
*Vinzenz A. Müller,Nora Taufertshöfer,Nicola A. Spaldin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入跨壳层算符，构建了局域密度矩阵的完备正交实厄密多极算符基，并将其分类为宇称和时间反演对称性，最后应用于手性三方碲的电环形单极矩分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统“固定壳层（fixed-shell）”的多极分解仅能解析同一轨道角动量$l$内的算符，无法覆盖完整的局域单粒子算符空间。本文旨在通过扩展至跨壳层算符，构建一个完备的正交基，以更完整地描述局域电子自由度。

Method: 首先将轨道和自旋算符空间分别按$\mathrm{SO}(3)$群分解，然后通过耦合得到自旋-1/2局域单粒子算符空间，从而构建实厄密多极算符的完备正交基。随后按宇称（parity）和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）对多极矩进行分类。

Result: 构建了扩展到跨壳层算符的完备多极算符基，该基与现有固定壳层表述一致。通过对称性分类，识别出密度矩阵中对完全对称性分辨可观测量的期望值有贡献的多极矩。在手性三方碲（chiral trigonal tellurium）中，计算了由对称性筛选出的电环形单极矩（electric toroidal monopole moment）。

Conclusion: 所提出的完备多极分解框架能更完整地刻画局域电子结构，并为对称性分辨的物理可观测量提供了明确的分类依据，在手性材料等体系中具有应用价值。

Abstract: The multipole decomposition of the single-site density matrix provides a symmetry-adapted representation of local electronic degrees of freedom. Conventional, so-called fixed-shell, formulations do not span the full local single-particle operator space, as only operators mapping within the same orbital $l$ are resolved. Here we construct a complete orthogonal basis of real Hermitian multipole operators for the local density matrix by extending the existing formulation to inter-shell operators. We revisit the multipole decomposition as a decomposition of the operator space by $\mathrm{SO}(3)$ by first decomposing the orbital and spin operator spaces. Then by coupling them we arrive at the spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ local single-particle operator space, staying consistent with the existing fixed-shell formulations. We then classify the multipoles by parity and time-reversal symmetry, which allows for unique identification of multipole moments of the density matrix that contribute to expectation values of fully symmetry-resolved observables. As an application, we analyze the two enantiomers of chiral trigonal tellurium by computing the electric toroidal monopole moment selected by symmetry.

### [96] [An Information-Theoretic Characterization of Optimal Value-Readout in Response-Register Quantum Oracles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13198)
*Milad Ghadimi,Hesam Soltanpanahi,Vahid Salari*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对有限阿贝尔响应群上的响应寄存器量子预言机（response-register quantum oracles），证明了最优单次查询的值读出概率（value-readout probability）等于响应状态的归一化Rényi-1/2有效傅里叶支撑（normalized Rényi-1/2 effective Fourier support），从而给出了两种操作诠释之间的精确定量关系，并建立了紧致的相位-值互补性定理（phase--value complementarity theorem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 响应寄存器量子预言机存在值读出（value readout）和相位反冲（phase kickback）两种互补的操作性诠释，虽然它们在计算上等价，但二者之间的定量关系此前缺乏精确刻画。

Method: 针对有限阿贝尔响应群（finite Abelian response groups），通过数学推导证明最优单次查询值读出概率等于响应状态的归一化Rényi-1/2有效傅里叶支撑。

Result: 得到了一个精确的信息论刻画，为值读出能力提供了最优表征；赋予Rényi-1/2有效傅里叶支撑以预言机设定下的直接操作性诠释；推导出一个紧致的相位-值互补性定理，并给出了达到该互补性边界的显式响应状态族。

Conclusion: 该结果在预言机设定下建立了量子信息论与傅里叶分析之间的精确联系，并为量子计算中相位与值两类信息的互补性提供了严格的定量描述。

Abstract: Response-register quantum oracles admit two complementary operational interpretations: value readout and phase kickback. Although their computational equivalence is well understood, the quantitative relation between these two operational interpretations has lacked an exact characterization. We prove that, for finite Abelian response groups, the optimal single-query value-readout probability is exactly the normalized Rényi-1/2 effective Fourier support of the response state. This identity provides an exact information-theoretic characterization of optimal value-readout capability, gives the Rényi-1/2 effective Fourier support a direct operational interpretation in the oracle setting, and yields a tight phase--value complementarity theorem together with an explicit family of saturating response states.

### [97] [Ultraviolet structure of entanglement harvesting from energy density and other quadratic couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13131)
*Matheus H. Zambianco,Boris Ragula,Eduardo Martín-Martínez*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究分析了点状探测器（pointlike detectors）在耦合到无质量标量场重整化能量密度（renormalized energy density）时出现的紫外发散（ultraviolet divergences），指出其根源在于相互作用时间重合时的开关函数相关性（switching correlation），并通过非重叠开关或高斯涂抹（Gaussian smearing）消除发散，最终给出任意零均值高斯态（zero-mean Gaussian states）的一般表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前针对二次探测器耦合（quadratic detector couplings）的研究中观察到了持续的紫外发散，但其背后的机制尚不明确。本文旨在揭示这一发散的根本来源，并探讨能量密度耦合是否具有相同的结构特性。

Method: 采用粒子探测器（particle detectors）与无质量标量场（massless scalar field）的重整化能量密度耦合的框架，分析开关函数（switching function）在重合相互作用时间下的分布机制（distributional mechanism），并推导任意零均值高斯态下的一般表达式。

Result: 紫外发散完全由相互作用时间重合时的开关相关性控制；点状探测器在开关不重叠时紫外有限；高斯涂抹探测器在1+1和2+1维中自动有限，更高维中剩余发散可通过非重叠开关消除。

Conclusion: 能量密度耦合与二次探测器耦合共享相同的发散结构，开关函数的非重叠设计是消除点状探测器紫外发散的关键；高斯涂抹在低维中自动截断发散，高维中仍需结合非重叠开关。

Abstract: We study entanglement harvesting with particle detectors coupled to the renormalized energy density of a massless scalar field. Our analysis identifies the distributional mechanism underlying the persistent ultraviolet divergences previously observed for quadratic detector couplings and discusses that the energy density coupling exhibits the same underlying structure. We show that these divergences are entirely controlled by the switching correlation at coincident interaction times. Consequently, pointlike detectors are UV finite whenever the switchings do not overlap. For Gaussian-smeared detectors, the harvesting correlations are automatically finite in 1+1 and 2+1 dimensions, while in higher dimensions the remaining divergences are removed by non-overlapping switchings. Finally, we derive general expressions for arbitrary zero-mean Gaussian states and illustrate the formalism with a thermal field state.

### [98] [Quantum memory advantage for quantum process tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13476)
*Carlos Bravo-Prieto,Weiyuan Gong,Antonio Anna Mele*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了量子记忆（quantum memory）在量子过程断层扫描（quantum process tomography）中能够提供查询复杂度（query-complexity）优势：无记忆的非相干协议的最优查询复杂度为 Θ(d_in³ d_out³/ε²)，而带量子记忆的相干协议仅需 Θ(d_in² d_out²/ε²)，从而建立了二者之间的严格学习分离（learning separation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子过程断层扫描是从黑盒访问中学习未知量子信道（quantum channel）的核心问题。一个基本未解决的问题是：即使无记忆协议可以利用无限经典计算能力进行自适应实验，量子记忆是否能提供查询复杂度上的优势——本文旨在回答这一开放问题。

Method: 本文推导了无量子记忆的非相干协议（incoherent protocol）的最优查询复杂度下界 Ω(d_in³ d_out³/ε²)，并构造了一个非自适应、不含辅助量子比特（ancilla-free）的非相干协议达到匹配的上界 O(d_in³ d_out³/ε²)。该结果将单副本状态断层扫描（single-copy state tomography）的最优样本复杂度界推广为 d_in=1 的特例。

Result: 无量子记忆协议（包括自适应协议）的最优查询复杂度为 Θ(d_in³ d_out³/ε²)，而有量子记忆的相干协议（coherent protocol）查询复杂度为 Θ(d_in² d_out²/ε²)，两者之间存在一个维度因子的严格分离。

Conclusion: 量子记忆在量子过程断层扫描中提供了本质性的查询复杂度优势，即使在无记忆协议可借助无限经典计算进行自适应的条件下依然成立。该结果建立了两类协议之间的严格学习分离，并推广了状态断层扫描的已知结论。

Abstract: Quantum process tomography, the task of learning an unknown quantum channel from black-box access, is a central problem in quantum information. In this setting, protocols with quantum memory can coherently store and jointly process quantum information obtained from multiple channel uses, whereas protocols without quantum memory must measure after each use and retain only a classical transcript of the measurement outcomes. A fundamental open question is whether quantum memory provides a query-complexity advantage even when protocols without quantum memory may adapt their experiments based on all previous outcomes with unbounded classical computational power. In this work, we show that it does. We determine the optimal query complexity of quantum process tomography without quantum memory up to a constant factor to be $Θ(d_{\mathrm{in}}^3 d_{\mathrm{out}}^3/\varepsilon^2)$, where $d_{\mathrm{in}}$ and $d_{\mathrm{out}}$ are the channel input and output dimensions, respectively, and $\varepsilon$ is the target diamond-norm accuracy. More precisely, we prove that any incoherent protocol for this task, including adaptive protocols, requires $Ω(d_{\mathrm{in}}^3 d_{\mathrm{out}}^3/\varepsilon^2)$ queries, even when each channel use may be assisted by arbitrary fresh ancilla, and we present a non-adaptive, ancilla-free incoherent protocol achieving the matching upper bound $O(d_{\mathrm{in}}^3 d_{\mathrm{out}}^3/\varepsilon^2)$. Our results thereby generalize the optimal sample-complexity bounds for single-copy state tomography, recovered as the special case $d_{\mathrm{in}}=1$. By contrast, coherent protocols with quantum memory achieve query complexity $Θ(d_{\mathrm{in}}^2 d_{\mathrm{out}}^2/\varepsilon^2)$. Hence, our results establish a rigorous learning separation between quantum process tomography with and without quantum memory.

</details>


### [99] [Separating Geometry From Interference in Constrained Quantum Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13630)
*Chinonso Onah,Stuart Hadfield,Kristel Michielsen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个框架，将量子优化算法中的几何效应与量子干涉分离，分析了约束保持混合算子的振幅传输行为，并证明了当代价相位被适当设计时，仅需对数增长次数的电路交替即可获得与问题规模无关的保证成功概率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 约束优化问题（如路由、指派、调度）通常被编码为局部变量的乘积空间（product space）与全局可行性惩罚项的组合。这些问题的量子算法中，几何效应与量子干涉通常相互混杂，难以区分各自的作用。本文旨在分离这些效应，以澄清量子采样优势的来源与条件。

Method: 建立一个框架，将通常混杂的三种效应分离：振幅传输（amplitude transport）、传输振幅之间的相干干涉（coherent interference），以及依赖于问题的经典后处理（classical postprocessing）。通过分析混合算子单独作用下的归一化分布向均匀随机配置的距离轮廓演化，揭示其不具备目标搜索能力。进而研究代价相位（cost phases）设计下计算路径的相干叠加条件。

Result: 混合算子单独不具有目标搜索能力；其振幅传输诱导的归一化分布向均匀随机配置的距离轮廓移动。当代价相位被工程化使得抵达目标配置的众多计算路径的相位充分对齐时，电路交替次数仅需随问题规模对数增长，即可将各路径幅值的绝对值之和转化为目标振幅的下界，从而获得与希尔伯特空间维数（Hilbert-space dimension）、搜索空间大小或可行集基数无关的保证成功概率。

Conclusion: 量子采样优势可能仅当多条计算路径的相位对齐从而实现振幅增强时出现。所提框架可应用于问题特定的转译诊断（transpilation diagnostics）、可扩展硬件探针（scalable hardware probes）、约束诱导的量子生成样本经典映射、混合量子-经典工作流中量子分布与经典后处理对解质量的归因，以及经典编码理论中距离分割乘积空间（distance-partitioned product spaces）的关联。

Abstract: We study the separation of geometric effects from quantum interference in quantum optimization algorithms. Constrained optimization problems such as routing, assignment, and scheduling are often encoded as product spaces of local variables, together with global feasibility penalties. The central algorithmic question we address is how a constraint-preserving mixing operator transports quantum amplitude across an exponential search space in the presence of local and global constraints. We develop a framework that separates three effects that are usually intermixed: amplitude transport, coherent interference among transported amplitudes, and problem-dependent classical postprocessing. We show that the mixing operator alone does not have a target-seeking ability. Concretely, the normalized distribution induced by its amplitude transport moves toward the distance profile of a uniformly random configuration. Thus, quantum sampling advantage may only arise when the phases of the many computational paths reaching a target configuration are sufficiently aligned for their amplitudes to reinforce. We show that, when the cost phases are engineered so that these paths add coherently, a number of circuit alternations growing only logarithmically with problem size suffices to convert the sum of their absolute contributions into a lower bound on the target amplitude, yielding a certified success probability independent of the ambient Hilbert-space dimension, the search-space size, or the feasible-set cardinality. We develop applications to problem-specific transpilation diagnostics, scalable hardware probes, constraint-induced classical maps of quantum-generated samples, the attribution of solution quality between the quantum distribution and classical post-processing in hybrid quantum-classical workflows and connections to distance-partitioned product spaces from classical coding theory.

</details>


### [100] [Quantum Boomerang Effect in Time-Crystalline Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07225)
*Qi-wen Peng,Krzysztof Sacha,Chu-hui Fan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从理论上建立并在数量上表征了时间晶体结构中的量子回旋镖效应（quantum boomerang effect, QBE），通过将连续Floquet动力学映射到离散无序紧束缚晶格，证明了波包的平均时间质心在时间域中呈现初始弹道膨胀、显著U形转弯并最终返回初始时间位置的行为，从而确认了时间域中完整QBE的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子回旋镖效应是安德森局域化（Anderson localization）的一个独特动力学标志，但该效应此前尚未在时间晶体（time crystal）结构中得到研究。本工作旨在理论层面建立并定量刻画周期性驱动系统中时间域上的QBE，以拓展该效应的适用范围并探索时间晶体系统中的非平凡动力学行为。

Method: 通过构造最大局域的Floquet-Wannier态（maximally localized Floquet-Wannier states）并引入时间无序（temporal disorder），将一维势阱中周期性驱动的量子粒子的连续Floquet动力学（continuous Floquet dynamics）严格映射到离散无序紧束缚晶格（discrete disordered tight-binding lattice）上。随后在固定空间坐标处设置探测器，监测波包的时间演化，提取时间晶体结构中概率密度的时间域平均质心（mean temporal center of mass）。

Result: 波包的时间域平均质心在演化初期呈现弹道式（ballistic）膨胀，随后出现显著的U形回旋（U-turn），并在长时间演化后最终返回其初始时间位置。这一完整的动力学过程确认了时间域中量子回旋镖效应的存在。

Conclusion: 研究结果证实了时间晶体结构中存在完整的时间域量子回旋镖效应，表明即使时间晶体结构本身具有固有的时间周期性（temporal periodicity），仍然可以在其中探索非平凡的动力学行为。

Abstract: The quantum boomerang effect (QBE) is a unique dynamical signature of Anderson localization, characterized by a launched wavepacket that initially drifts but ultimately returns to its initial position due to fundamental quantum interference. In this work, we theoretically establish and quantitatively characterize the QBE in a time-crystalline structure using a periodically driven quantum particle in a one-dimensional potential well. By constructing maximally localized Floquet-Wannier states and introducing temporal disorder, we rigorously map the continuous Floquet dynamics onto a discrete disordered tight-binding lattice. By positioning a detector at a fixed spatial coordinate, we monitor the temporal evolution of the wavepacket, to extract the mean temporal center of mass of the probability density in a time-crystalline structure. This mean temporal center of mass exhibits an initial ballistic expansion, followed by a pronounced U-turn, and ultimately returns to its initial temporal position after long-time evolution. These results confirm the existence of the complete QBE in the time domain. They also demonstrate that non-trivial dynamics can be explored within time-crystalline systems, even though these structures already possess an inherent temporal periodicity.

</details>


### [101] [Loophole-Robust Certification of Quantum Advantage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13090)
*Prosanta Pal,Gargee Sharma,Ramakrishna Podila*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“基准依赖性（benchmark dependence）”概念，将量子优势声明（quantum advantage claims）中经典策略可获取的边信息（side information）系统形式化，推导出经典得分的最优上界，并在IBM硬件数据和量子核基准（quantum-kernel benchmark）上进行了实证验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子优势声明应能在经典策略获取与评估基准相关的边信息时仍保持稳健，这类似于贝尔认证（Bell certification）必须考虑测量依赖性（measurement dependence）。现有框架尚未系统处理这种任务层面的相关性。

Method: 将边信息形式化为“基准依赖性”，作为测量依赖性的任务级泛化。对有界奖励任务（bounded-reward task）推导出经典得分上界 $S_η\leq\min\{1,S_{\mathrm{cl}}+η\}$，并构造饱和该界的任务族。对重复乘积任务（repeated product tasks）推导出乘性界 $S_η^{(n)}\leq(ω_{\mathrm c}+η)^n$，并扩展至有限样本、互信息约束、多体任务及因果路径分布的相关性。

Result: 在IBM硬件数据上，CHSH和Mermin–GHZ的原始计数循环乘积证书（raw-count cycle-product certificates）分别为0.0812和0.2178，而九上下文幻方构造（nine-context magic-square construction）未获认证。在非贝尔量子核基准中，标签构造变量（label-construction variable）的条件依赖性 $\widehatη_λ^{(Y)}=0.5$ 超过了所需阈值 $η_{\mathrm{req}}=0.375$，经典分类可达到完美准确率。

Conclusion: 该框架将量子–经典得分差转化为一个量化的下界，用于解释该得分差所需的与基准相关的经典信息量，从而为评估量子优势声明提供了一种形式化工具。

Abstract: Claims of quantum advantage should remain robust even when classical strategies have access to side information correlated with the benchmark under evaluation, just as Bell certification must account for measurement dependence. We formalize such correlations as benchmark dependence, a task-level generalization of measurement dependence. For every bounded-reward task, we show that the optimal benchmark-dependent classical score obeys $S_η\leq\min\{1,S_{\mathrm{cl}}+η\}$, and construct a family of tasks that saturates this bound, showing that the linear dependence on $η$ is tight without further assumptions. For repeated product tasks with roundwise dependence, we obtain the stronger multiplicative bound $S_η^{(n)}\leq(ω_{\mathrm c}+η)^n$, and extend the framework to finite-sample data, mutual-information constraints, multipartite tasks, and correlations distributed along a causal path. Applying these results to aggregated IBM hardware data, we obtain positive raw-count cycle-product certificates of 0.0812 for CHSH and 0.2178 for Mermin--GHZ, while the nine-context magic-square construction remains uncertified; readout-mitigated values are reported separately as sensitivity estimates. We also analyze a non-Bell quantum-kernel benchmark, where a label-construction variable has measured conditional dependence $\widehatη_λ^{(Y)}=0.5$, above the threshold $η_{\mathrm{req}}=0.375$, required to close the reported score gap, and yields perfect classical classification. The framework therefore converts a quantum--classical score separation into a quantitative lower bound on the benchmark-correlated classical information required to explain the score separation.

</details>


### [102] [Emulating XX catalysts for quantum annealing via self-consistent transverse fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13150)
*Mohammadhossein Dadgar,Christopher L. Baldwin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过自洽横向场（self-consistent transverse field）来模拟全连接横向相互作用（fully-connected transverse interactions）催化量子退火（quantum annealing）效果的实验可行方案，仅需额外进行横向（$\hatσ^x$）基测量。研究表明，在大系统极限下该协议与原始催化方案动力学一致，并通过$p$-自旋模型（$p$-spin model）数值模拟验证了趋近极限的过程。尽管实际实现需要多种近似，但各近似误差均可控，最终可将协议映射到仅调控单一控制参数的退火平台，在近期量子退火机上展现良好性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全连接横向相互作用被认为可催化量子退火，缓解指数级小能隙（exponentially small gaps）并规避一级相变（first-order phase transitions），但其实验实现极具挑战性。本工作旨在开发一种无需直接实现全连接相互作用、仅依赖现有退火硬件即可模拟其效果的替代方案。

Method: 引入自洽横向场协议，通过在横向（$\hatσ^x$）基下进行测量并反馈，自洽地确定有效横向场，从而模拟全连接横向相互作用的动力学。通过分析证明在大系统极限下二者动力学一致，并在均匀$p$-自旋模型（uniform $p$-spin model）上进行数值模拟以研究有限大小效应。针对实际实现，设计一系列近似变体并量化其误差，最终将协议映射到仅变化单一控制参数的退火平台。

Result: 自洽横向场协议在大系统极限下与原始全连接横向相互作用催化剂产生相同的动力学；数值模拟表明有限尺寸效应可趋于一致；各近似变体的误差均可量化并控制到足够小；即便经过多阶段近似，该协议仍能与原始催化方案动力学良好吻合。

Conclusion: 自洽横向场可作为全连接横向相互作用催化的可行替代方案，适用于近期量子退火机（quantum annealer），为在现有实验条件下实现量子退火催化效应提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Fully-connected transverse interactions have been considered as catalysts for quantum annealing that could mitigate exponentially small gaps and circumvent first-order phase transitions, but their experimental implementation remains challenging. In this work, we introduce a procedure for emulating their effects via a self-consistent transverse field. All that is required beyond conventional transverse-field annealing is the ability to make measurements in the transverse ($\hatσ^x$) basis. We show that this protocol yields identical dynamics in the large-system limit, and study the approach to that limit in numerical simulations of the (uniform) $p$-spin model. However, realizing the protocol in practice requires us to consider a series of approximate variants, each of whose errors we quantify and demonstrate can be made sufficiently small. Lastly, we show how to map the protocol onto annealing platforms that vary only a single control parameter. Even after the multiple stages of approximation, our procedure can generate dynamics that agree well with the original transverse-interaction catalyst, establishing self-consistent transverse fields as a viable alternative on near-term quantum annealers.

B. Ioffe,Kostyantyn Kechedzhi,Xiao Mi,Dmitry Abanin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究利用一款最高达97量子比特（qubits）的模数混合超导处理器，在二维XY自旋-1/2磁体中实现了线性和非线性响应函数的高精度量子模拟。通过将数字门（digital gates）与经哈密顿学习（Hamiltonian learning）精确表征的类比演化（analog evolution）相结合，研究团队选择性地激发具有可调能量密度的磁振子（magnons），测量了温度依赖的线性磁振子谱和寿命，揭示了布里渊区（Brillouin zone）中磁振子衰减率的显著变化，并开展了非线性测量（如自散射机制与泵浦-探测光谱）。研究还发现，矩阵乘积态（matrix-product state）模拟在小系统或低温下表现良好，但在其他区域精度不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子模拟有望通过精确计算复杂物质状态及其微观激发和宏观响应函数来推动材料发现，但核心挑战在于将高保真度演化与操控量子多体态中单个准粒子（quasi-particles）所需的精密控制相结合。

Method: 采用模数混合超导处理器，最高包含97个量子比特，将数字门与经哈密顿学习精确标定的类比演化过程交错进行，以可调能量密度选择性激发磁振子；在此基础上测量线性及非线性响应函数，包括泵浦-探测光谱等。

Result: 成功测量了温度依赖的线性磁振子谱与寿命，发现布里渊区内磁振子衰减率存在显著差异：在范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities）附近增强，在边缘局域模式处受到抑制。非线性测量表征了自散射机制和磁振子相互作用。矩阵乘积态模拟在小系统或低温下有效，但在其他条件下预测不准确。

Conclusion: 本工作实现了量子磁体中相互作用动力学的高精度模拟，为准粒子及其微观散射机制提供了关键见解。

Abstract: Quantum simulation promises to advance materials discovery by accurately simulating complex states of matter, their microscopic excitations, and macroscopic response functions. The central challenge in resolving the underlying interacting dynamics is to combine high-fidelity evolution with the sophisticated control necessary to manipulate individual quasi-particles in quantum many-body states. Here, we report on high-precision simulation of both linear and non-linear response functions in a 2D XY spin-1/2 magnet using an analog-digital superconducting processor of up to 97 qubits. By interleaving digital gates with analog evolution precisely characterized via Hamiltonian learning, we selectively excite magnons at tunable energy densities. Measuring first the linear magnon response -- a central probe in neutron-scattering experiments -- we extract temperature-dependent spectra and lifetimes. Our results reveal stark variations in magnon decay rates across the Brillouin zone, with enhancement near van Hove singularities and suppression for edge-localized modes. Next, we perform a suite of nonlinear measurements, including the study of self-scattering mechanisms, as well as pump-probe spectroscopy to directly characterize the magnon interactions. While matrix-product state simulations capture the dynamics well in either small systems or at low temperatures, their predictions become inaccurate away from these limits. This work demonstrates precise simulation of the interacting dynamics in quantum magnets, and provides key insights into quasi-particles and their microscopic scattering mechanisms.

### [104] [Deterministic single-electron trapping on solid neon using engineered dielectric surface geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13448)
*Kundan Surse,Eric Helgemo,Andrew Palmer,Md Serajum Monir,Lukas Delventhal,Thanh Nguyen,Maja Cassidy,Rajib Rahman*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出在固体氖（solid neon）下方沉积介电层（dielectric layer）作为原子级平滑模板，通过选择性刻蚀构建确定性势阱（deterministic potential minima），以消除表面粗糙度引起的电子非故意束缚（unintentional trapping）和自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）导致的退相干（decoherence），从而提升悬浮电子量子比特（levitating electron qubit）的相干性能。大规模薛定谔-泊松（Schrödinger-Poisson）仿真结果与近期实验吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体氖表面悬浮电子量子比特虽因超洁净惰性环境而天然抑制半导体量子比特中的晶格无序、电荷陷阱和核自旋浴等退相干路径，但表面凹凸、电极间隙等非受控特征可非故意束缚电子，引入电荷噪声（charge noise）并诱发自旋-轨道耦合介导的退相干。因此需设计工程化界面来消除此类表面粗糙度诱导的电子捕获。

Method: 在固体氖下方沉积一层介电层作为原子级平滑模板，再对目标量子比特位置处的介电层进行选择性刻蚀（selective etching），从而构建确定的势阱以可靠捕获电子，同时抑制非期望的表面束缚态（surface bound states）。采用大规模薛定谔-泊松仿真比较现有策略与所提方案的电子捕获效果。

Result: 大规模薛定谔-泊松仿真表明，所提工程化界面策略可有效消除表面粗糙度诱导的电子非故意束缚；仿真结果与近期实验测量取得良好一致。

Conclusion: 所提出的介电层模板与选择性刻蚀方案为固体氖表面悬浮电子量子比特提供了一种抑制表面粗糙度导致退相干的可行工程路径，有望提升该量子信息处理平台的相干性能。

Abstract: Levitating electron qubit on the surface of solid neon has recently emerged as a promising and intrinsically noise-resilient platform for quantum information processing. Their ultra-clean, inert environment suppresses conventional decoherence pathways associated with lattice disorder, charge traps, and nuclear-spin baths that limit coherence in semiconductor qubits. Yet, uncontrolled surface features such as bumps, valleys, and electrode-defined gaps can bind electrons unintentionally, contributing charge noise and inducing spin-orbit coupling mediated decoherence. To address this challenge, we propose an engineered interface in which a dielectric layer is deposited beneath the solid neon to provide an atomically smooth template, eliminating surface-roughness induced trapping. By selectively etching this dielectric layer at desired qubit locations, deterministic potential minima can be engineered to reliably capture electrons while suppressing unwanted surface bound states. We perform large-scale Schrodinger and Poisson simulation to compare the existing and proposed strategies of electron trapping on neon, obtaining good agreement with recent experimental measurements.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本工作为无线互连、低温封装与超导量子硬件的协同设计（co-design）建立了实验框架。

Abstract: Scalable quantum computing is limited by the dense network of electrical interconnects linking cryogenic quantum processors to room-temperature control electronics. To overcome this bottleneck, considerable effort has focused on cryogenic CMOS electronics and microwave-to-optical transduction, aiming to reduce wiring complexity and thermal loading. Wireless interconnects have recently emerged as a promising complementary approach, yet their compatibility with superconducting quantum hardware remains largely unexplored. Here, we demonstrate the wireless excitation of a superconducting microwave resonator of the type routinely employed for qubit readout, operating at millikelvin temperatures inside a dilution refrigerator. By directly comparing wired and wireless operation within the same cryogenic environment, we show that wireless coupling preserves the intrinsic resonator response while revealing parasitic electromagnetic pathways arising from stray radiation within the cryostat enclosure. These results establish a framework for the co-design of wireless interconnects, cryogenic packaging and superconducting quantum hardware.

### [106] [Cluster-configurational study of G-center in Silicon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14083)
*Narayan Pokhrel,Kyungwha Park,Vsevolod Ivanov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用多组态自洽场（MCSCF）方法结合DFT优化几何，系统研究了硅中G中心的自旋与光学性质，并利用簇相关展开（CCE）方法计算了理论自旋退相干时间。计算结果与零声子线（ZPL）和零场分裂（ZFS）张量分量高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺陷（defect）的性质理解对包括量子计算（quantum computing）在内的多种应用至关重要。该研究旨在深入揭示硅（Silicon）中G中心（G center）的自旋与光学性质，为其实践应用奠定理论基础。

Method: 使用多组态自洽场（multiconfigurational self consistent field, MCSCF）方法，并与DFT（density functional theory）优化的几何结构相结合，计算G中心的自旋和光学性质。自旋退相干时间（spin decoherence time）通过簇相关展开（Cluster Correlation Expansion, CCE）方法进行理论计算。

Result: 基于量子化学（quantum chemistry）的计算方法与G中心的零声子线（Zero Phonon Line, ZPL）和零场分裂（Zero Field Splitting, ZFS）张量分量实验值展现出优异的一致性。此外，还给出了G中心的理论自旋退相干时间。

Conclusion: MCSCF结合DFT优化的方法能够准确描述硅中G中心的实验可观测量，表明该方法在缺陷体系的理论研究中具有可靠性。

Abstract: Understanding the properties of defects is imperative for proper use for variety of applications including quantum computing. In this paper, we use the multiconfigurational self consistent field (MCSCF) combined with DFT optimized geometry in order to investigate the spin and optical properties of G centers in Silicon. By utilizing quantum chemistry based methods, we show excellent agreement with the Zero Phonon Line and Zero Field Splitting Tensor components of the G center. We also calculate the theoretical spin decoherence time of the G centers using Cluster Correlation Expansion (CCE) methods.

</details>


### [107] [Sail membranes for optomechanical accelerometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14089)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将贝叶斯优化应用于Si₃N₄薄膜，发现了一类帆状蹦床谐振子结构。将7 kHz器件与纳米带（nanoribbon）垂直集成，实现了单片式腔光力学加速度计。

Conclusion: 帆状薄膜的低温阵列（cryogenic arrays）可能对新物理探寻（new physics searches）和分布式量子传感实验（distributed quantum sensing experiments）具有吸引力。

Abstract: Strained membrane resonators have emerged as a promising platform for optomechanical accelerometry; however, the desired combination of low frequency and high $Q$-mass product requires a rethinking of their dissipation dilution engineering. Applying Bayesian optimization to a Si$_3$N$_4$ membrane, we discover a class of sail-like trampoline resonators in which the frequency is decreased by an order of magnitude while preserving the $Q$-mass product. We demonstrate centimeter-scale sails with kHz frequencies, $Q\sim10^7$ and $Q\times\text{mass}\sim$ 10 g. Vertically integrating a 7 kHz device with a nanoribbon, we realize a monolithic cavity optomechanical accelerometer with a room temperature thermal noise of $40\;\text{n}g_0/\sqrt{\text{Hz}}$, sufficient to resolve $μg_0/\sqrt{\text{Hz}}$ ambient vibration over a bandwidth of 4 kHz with a displacement imprecision of $10^{-14}\;\text{m}/\sqrt{\text{Hz}}$. Cryogenic arrays of sail membranes may be attractive for new physics searches and distributed quantum sensing experiments.

### [108] [Evidence for sequential $Υ$(nS) suppression in light ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13758)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次在氧-氧（oxygen-oxygen）和氖-氖（neon-neon）碰撞中测量了底夸克偶素（bottomonium）的三个最低质量S波矢量共振态——Υ(1S)、Υ(2S)和Υ(3S)的产额，发现Υ(2S)/Υ(1S)和Υ(3S)/Υ(1S)比值显著低于质子-质子（pp）参考值，且Υ(3S)相对于Υ(2S)的压制显著性超过三个标准差，为轻离子碰撞中底夸克偶素的逐级压制（sequential suppression）提供了证据，暗示了夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）介质的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重夸克-反重夸克对束缚态（即夸克偶素，quarkonia）长期被视为夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）的敏感探针。此前在铅-铅和金-金重离子碰撞中观察到了底夸克偶素的逐级压制现象，但尚未在轻离子（如氧和氖）碰撞中对此进行验证。

Method: 在质心系能量每核子对√sNN = 5.36 TeV下，测量氧-氧碰撞中三个最低质量S波矢量底夸克偶素共振态（Υ(1S)、Υ(2S)和Υ(3S)）的产额，并在相同能量下测量氖-氖碰撞中Υ(1S)和Υ(2S)共振态的产额，通过与质子-质子参考值比较来评估相对压制程度。

Result: Υ(2S)/Υ(1S)比值显著低于质子-质子参考值，Υ(3S)/Υ(1S)比值显示出更大幅度的降低；Υ(3S)相对于Υ(2S)的额外压制显著性超过三个标准差。

Conclusion: 这些结果为轻离子碰撞中Υ(nS)态的逐级压制提供了实验证据，其模式与铅-铅和金-金重离子碰撞中的观测结果类似，通常被归因于夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）介质的形成。

Abstract: Bound states of heavy quark-antiquark pairs, known as quarkonia, have long been regarded as particularly sensitive probes of the quark-gluon plasma (QGP). Comparing quarkonium yields in collisions of heavy nuclei, such as gold or lead, with a proton-proton (pp) reference reveals a characteristic pattern of sequential suppression, in which weakly-bound excited states are more strongly suppressed than the ground states. We report the first measurements of the three lowest mass $\mathrm{S}$-wave vector bottomonium resonances, the ground state $Υ$(1S) and the excited states $Υ$(2S) and $Υ$(3S), in oxygen-oxygen collisions at a center-of-mass energy per nucleon pair of $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 5.36 TeV. Measurements of the yields of the $Υ$(1S) and $Υ$(2S) resonances in neon-neon collisions, at the same $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$, are also presented. The $Υ$(2S)/$Υ$(1S) ratio is found to be significantly below the measured pp reference value, and the $Υ$(3S)/$Υ$(1S) ratio shows an even larger reduction. The significance of the relative $Υ$(3S) to $Υ$(2S) suppression exceeds three standard deviations. These results provide evidence for the sequential suppression of $Υ$(nS) states in light ion collisions, similar to observations made in lead-lead and gold-gold collisions, generally attributed to the presence of a QGP medium.

### [109] [Cooper pairing with the onsite exchange interaction: A possible mechanism of high-temperature superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13086)
*Jacques R. Eone*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出由库仑相互作用与 Hund 耦合（Hund's coupling）共同引发的非常规超导机制，在单带 Hubbard 模型（single-band Hubbard model）框架下，利用 Hund 耦合参数 $J$ 产生的吸引分量束缚分数电荷（fractional charges），从而导出超导配对能隙 $\Delta_0$ 和转变温度 $T_c$，并成功复现了超导穹顶（superconducting dome）以及电子-空穴掺杂不对称性（doping asymmetry）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在铜氧化物（cuprates）和铁基超导体（iron pnictides）的多种非常规超导机制中，本文聚焦于库仑相互作用（Coulomb interaction）在 $d$-波和 $s\pm$-波配对对称性中的核心角色，旨在利用 Hund 耦合产生的吸引效应解释分数电荷束缚与超导配对的形成。

Method: 在一个简化的单带 Hubbard 模型（single-band Hubbard model）中，仅考虑掺杂超导平面（doped superconducting plane）上的分数电荷，有效相互作用 $U_\text{eff}=U-J$ 以 Hund 耦合参数 $J$ 引入吸引分量，通过计算该吸引分量带来的束缚能（binding energy）来估计超导配对能隙 $\Delta_0$ 和转变温度 $T_c$。

Result: 推导出一个仅依赖 Hubbard $U$ 和 Hund $J$ 参数的解析表达式，该表达式准确复现了超导穹顶（superconducting dome）的形状，并通过引入 Hund 耦合参数成功解释了铜氧化物中特征性的电子-空穴掺杂不对称性（electron and hole doping asymmetry）。

Conclusion: 该理论能准确描述奇异金属行为（strange metal behavior），但对赝能隙相（pseudogap phase）和欠掺杂同位素效应（underdoped isotope effect）目前仅提供定性解释，表明模型在全面刻画非常规超导现象方面仍有改进空间。

Abstract: Among the various mechanisms proposed for unconventional superconductivity, this paper focuses on the Coulomb interaction responsible for $d$-wave and $s\pm$-wave pairing symmetries in cuprates and iron pnictides. Although the effective interaction $U_\text{eff}=U-J$ is predominantly repulsive, an attractive component arising from the Hund's coupling parameter $J$ is sufficient to bind fractional charges. Evaluating this binding energy within a single-band Hubbard model yields a superconducting pairing gap $Δ_0$ and estimates the transition temperature $T_c$. Given the complex electronic structure and vast compositional space of these materials, the model focuses exclusively on the doped superconducting plane hosting these fractional charges. Through this approach, an analytical expression dependent on the Hubbard $U$ and Hund $J$ parameters that accurately reproduces the superconducting dome is derived. Furthermore, the model successfully addresses the characteristic electron and hole doping asymmetry observed in cuprates by accounting for Hund's coupling parameters. Finally, while the theory accurately describes strange metal behavior, it currently provides only a qualitative explanation for the pseudogap phase and the underdoped isotope effect.

</details>


### [110] [Zero-energy bound state trapped in line-shaped vortex in topological superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13194)
*P. Schlottmann*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本论文研究了二维拓扑超导体中直线涡旋核心内的费米子束缚态。通过椭圆坐标描述超导配对势，求解Bogoliubov-de Gennes方程，发现零能马约拉纳态（Majorana state）与等间距费米子激发序列，并给出了局域态密度的解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨二维拓扑超导体（topological superconductor）中线状涡旋（line-shaped vortex）核心内部的费米子束缚态（fermion bound states）性质，特别是其中可能出现的马约拉纳零能模（Majorana zero mode）。

Method: 采用椭圆坐标（elliptical coordinates）描述沿直线缺陷消逝的超导配对势（superconducting pairing potential）；通过Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）实现自旋-动量垂直锁定；利用Caroli、de Gennes和Matricon发展的方法求解Bogoliubov-de Gennes方程（Bogoliubov-de Gennes equations），计算束缚态的能量、波函数和自旋极化。

Result: 由贝里相位（Berry phase）产生零能马约拉纳态（zero-energy Majorana state），伴随一系列等间距的费米子激发（fermion excitations）；获得了涡旋内局域态密度（local density of states）的解析表达式。

Conclusion: 在拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）通过邻近效应（proximity effect）与第二类s波超导体（type II s-wave superconductor）诱导的超导体系中，直线涡旋核心可支持马约拉纳束缚态及其相关的等间距激发谱。

Abstract: Fermion bound states in the core of a line-shaped vortex of a two-dimensional topological superconductor are investigated. The superconducting pairing potential, described in terms of elliptical coordinates, vanishes along a line defect with the two foci at the endpoints. The superconductivity is induced into a topological insulator via proximity effect with a type II s-wave superconductor. The spin and the momentum are perpendicularly locked by the strong spin-orbit coupling via Rashba interaction. A zero-energy Majorana state arises from the Berry phase together with a sequence of equally spaced fermion exitations. By solving the Bogoliubov-de Gennes equations using the method employed by Caroli, de Gennes and Matricon we calculate the energies, the wave-functions and spin-polarization of the bound states. An analytic expression for the local density of states within the vortex is obtained.
