### [111] [Theoretical prediction of structural stability and superconductivity in T-hexagonal molybdenum dihydrides Monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13297)
*Jakkapat Seeyangnok,Udomsilp Pinsook*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算发现，六方二氢化钼（MoH2）单层的T相（八面体相）比先前报道的H相更稳定，是真正的基态构型。基于该T相结构，利用密度泛函微扰理论（DFPT）和各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg理论，预测其在常压下具有常规超导转变温度Tc ≈ 14.4 K，电子-声子耦合参数λ = 1.04，能隙分布范围为2.07–3.01 meV（5.0 K时），为探索常压低维常规超导电性提供了稳定平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环境压力下的高温超导是凝聚态物理学（condensed-matter physics）的核心追求之一，但体相氢化物需极端压力才能稳定。二维（2D）过渡金属氢化物有望绕过这一压缩约束，因此需要探索常压下稳定的氢基超导材料体系。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）评估MoH2单层的总能量以确定最稳定相；通过密度泛函微扰理论（density functional perturbation theory, DFPT）和各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg形式（anisotropic Migdal-Eliashberg formalism）分析晶格动力学与超导特性。

Result: 确定T-MoH2单层较H相能量低0.198 eV，为基态结构；电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling, EPC）参数λ = 1.04，各向异性Eliashberg方程求解得到常压超导转变温度Tc ≈ 14.4 K，5.0 K时超导能隙Δ分布为2.07–3.01 meV。

Conclusion: T-MoH2单层在结构、力学和热学上均稳定，是探索常压条件下低维常规超导电性（conventional superconductivity）的一个有前景的平台。

Abstract: The realization of ambient-pressure, high-temperature superconductivity in hydrogen-rich materials remains a major pursuit in condensed-matter physics. While bulk hydrides require extreme pressures to stabilize, two-dimensional (2D) transition-metal hydrides offer a promising alternative to bypass these compression constraints. In this work, we investigate the structural stability, electronic properties, and phonon-mediated superconductivity of a hexagonal molybdenum dihydride (MoH2) monolayer using first-principles calculations. Total-energy evaluations reveal that the octahedral T-phase is energetically more favorable than the previously reported trigonal prismatic H-phase by 0.198 eV, establishing the T-phase as the true ground-state configuration. Consequently, we systematically evaluate the lattice dynamics and superconducting properties of this ground-state T-MoH2 monolayer within the frameworks of density functional perturbation theory (DFPT) and the anisotropic Migdal-Eliashberg formalism. The transition metal-hydrogen vibrational networks induce strong electron-phonon coupling (EPC), yielding an integrated coupling parameter of λ= 1.04. Solving the anisotropic Eliashberg equations predicts a conventional superconducting transition temperature (Tc of 14.4K) at ambient pressure, characterized by a moderately gap distribution (Δ= 2.07-3.01meV at 5.0 K). Our findings highlight the T-MoH2 monolayer as a structurally, mechanically, and thermally stable platform for exploring low-dimensional conventional superconductivity under ambient conditions.

### [112] [Direct observation of photon-induced vortices in superconducting films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13664)
*Takeshi Jodoi,Fuminori Hirayama,Tetsuya Tsuruta,Takahiro Kikuchi,Daiji Fukuda*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过直接观测电流承载超导体中光子诱导的涡旋-反涡旋对（vortex-antivortex pair, VAP）动力学，发现了以量化电压信号形式呈现的相滑移（phase-slip）事件，并证明在特定条件下VAP生成数趋于稳定，从而实现了基于相滑移计数的光子数分辨探测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涡旋-反涡旋对（VAP）成核被认为是超导探测器光子探测机制的核心，但此前一直缺乏对其动力学的直接动态观测。

Method: 在电流承载的超导体中吸收光子后，直接观测量化电压信号；通过分析偏置电流、基底温度和输入光子数态下的量化信号特征，研究VAP生成数与条件之间的关系。

Result: 观测到的量化电压信号对应于离散的相滑移事件，每个涡旋穿越引起超导序参量的2π相位变化，时间积分等于磁通量子（magnetic flux quantum）。特定条件下每个吸收光子产生的VAP数量趋于稳定，并实现基于相滑移计数的光子数分辨能力。

Conclusion: 揭示了一种由相位动力学（phase dynamics）而非传统电阻转变主导的探测机制；光子数分辨能力在光子诱导VAP生成的涨落被统计抑制时出现。该发现为基于相滑移计数的光子数分辨探测开辟了新路径，并为量子光学和光子量子技术中的高速超导探测器提供了新机遇。

Abstract: Nucleation of vortex-antivortex pairs (VAPs) is believed to play a central role in the photon detection mechanism of superconducting detectors; however, their direct dynamic observation has remained challenging. Here, we report the direct observation of photon-induced VAP dynamics in a current-carrying superconductor as quantized voltage signals following photon absorption. The observed signals are interpreted as discrete phase-slip events, where each vortex traversal induces a 2-pi phase change of the superconducting order parameter, resulting in a quantized voltage pulse whose time integral is given by the magnetic flux quantum. We analyze the resulting quantized signals as a function of bias current, base temperature, and input photon-number states, and find that the number of VAPs generated per absorbed photon becomes effectively stabilized under specific conditions. Under these conditions, we demonstrate photon-number-resolving capability by directly counting phase-slip-induced voltage quanta. Our results reveal a detection mechanism governed by phase dynamics rather than conventional resistive transitions. We further show that photon-number resolution emerges when the fluctuation of photon-induced vortex-antivortex pair generation becomes statistically suppressed. These findings establish a new route toward photon-number-resolving detection based on phase-slip counting and open opportunities for high-speed superconducting detectors for quantum optics and photonic quantum technologies.

</details>


### [113] [Superconducting proximity effect in a strongly correlated charge-transfer insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13873)
*Mengya Ren,Yaoyao Chen,Fudi Zhou,Can Zhang,Zhaoteng Dong,Lili Zhou,Quanzhen Zhang,Huixia Yang,Xiaolong Xu,Yuanxiao Ma,Yu Zhang,Yeliang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究利用超低温扫描隧道显微镜，在由单层 H-NbSe2（超导体）和单层 T-NbSe2（电荷转移绝缘体）构成的原子级尖锐横向结中，系统地研究了强关联绝缘体中的超导近邻效应，发现了从弱耦合到强耦合可调谐区间内超导能隙的演化以及粒子—空穴对称的束内束缚态（Yu-Shiba-Rusinov 类激发）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联绝缘体中的近邻诱导超导为量子态与人工功能系统设计提供了灵活路径，但超导与关联绝缘态之间的微观相互作用尚不明确，亟需在可控体系中直接探测该效应。

Method: 采用超低温扫描隧道显微镜（STM）并结合 STM 针尖操控技术，构建了由超导单层 H-NbSe2 与电荷转移绝缘单层 T-NbSe2 组成的原子级尖锐横向结，实现可调耦合区间的直接观测。

Result: 在弱耦合区间，T-NbSe2 中观测到鲁棒的近邻诱导超导能隙，但其数值小于 H-NbSe2 的能隙；在强耦合区间，T-NbSe2 能隙接近 H-NbSe2，并出现明显的粒子—空穴对称的束内束缚态（Yu-Shiba-Rusinov 类激发）。

Conclusion: 单层 H/T-NbSe2 横向结可作为阐明强关联电荷转移绝缘体中超导近邻效应的模型平台。

Abstract: Proximity-induced superconductivity in strongly correlated insulators provides a versatile route for engineering quantum states of matter and artificial systems with tailored functionalities. However, microscopic interplay between superconductivity and correlated insulating states remains poorly understood. Here we use ultralow-temperature scanning tunnelling microscopy (STM) to systemically investigate superconducting proximity effects in a charge-transfer insulator. Via STM tip manipulation, atomically sharp lateral junctions composed of superconducting monolayer H-NbSe2 and charge-transfer insulating monolayer T-NbSe2 are constructed, enabling direct access to tunable coupling regimes. In the weak-coupling regime, there is a robust proximity-induced superconducting gap in T-NbSe2, with a reduced gap value relative to that of H-NbSe2. Upon entering the strong-coupling regime, T-NbSe2 exhibits a superconducting gap comparable to that of H-NbSe2, accompanied by pronounced particle-hole-symmetric in-gap bound states, consistent with Yu-Shiba-Rusinov-like excitations. These findings establish monolayer H/T-NbSe2 lateral junctions as a model platform for elucidating superconducting proximity effects in strongly correlated charge-transfer insulators.

### [114] [Reconstruction of f(G) Gravity from an Interacting Viscous Generalized QCD Ghost Dark Energy Model: Cosmology and Thermodynamics: Cosmology and Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13109)
*Zhanar Umurzakhova,Aziza Altaibayeva,Ulbossyn Ualikhanova,Surajit Chattopadhyay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在重建的 $f(G)$ 引力框架下研究了带相互作用的黏性广义 QCD 鬼暗能量模型，采用混合膨胀律进行数值重建，并利用 Barrow 熵检验了热力学一致性，结果表明该模型能够自洽地解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了更真实地描述宇宙演化，需要在修改引力理论中同时考虑暗物质与暗能量之间的相互作用（interaction）以及体黏滞（bulk viscosity），并检验模型的热力学一致性。

Method: 在文献提出的 $f(G)$ 引力框架中引入相互作用项与体黏滞；采用混合膨胀律（hybrid expansion law）重建修正的高斯-博内函数（modified Gauss-Bonnet function），并通过数值方法得到 $f(G)$ 在早期和晚期的形式；进一步提出重建启发的幂律形式（reconstruction-inspired power-law form）用于宇宙学检验；采用 Barrow 熵（Barrow entropy）分析热力学行为。

Result: 重建的 $f(G)$ 函数在整个宇宙历史中平滑演化；有效状态方程（effective equation of state）在晚期逐渐趋近 de Sitter 相；总熵的非负演化表明广义热力学第二定律（generalized second law of thermodynamics）成立。

Conclusion: 带相互作用的黏性广义 QCD 鬼暗能量模型在重建的 $f(G)$ 引力框架下是一个可行且热力学自洽的理论框架，能够解释宇宙晚期的加速膨胀。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate an interacting viscous generalized QCD ghost dark energy model in the framework of reconstructed $f(G)$ gravity proposed in Phys.\ Lett.\ B 631, 1--6 (2005). The interaction between dark matter and dark energy together with bulk viscosity is incorporated to describe a more realistic cosmic evolution. A hybrid expansion law is adopted to reconstruct the modified Gauss-Bonnet function, which naturally connects the early matter-dominated epoch with the present accelerated expansion of the universe. Since an exact analytical reconstruction is difficult, the $f(G)$ function is obtained numerically in both the early- and late-time regimes. Motivated by the numerical reconstruction, a reconstruction-inspired power-law form of $f(G)$ is also considered to examine the cosmological implications of the model. The results show that the reconstructed $f(G)$ function evolves smoothly throughout the cosmic history, while the effective equation of state gradually approaches the de Sitter phase at late times. The thermodynamic behavior of the model is further examined using Barrow entropy following Eur.\ Phys.\ J.\ C 81, 644 (2021). The non-negative evolution of the total entropy shows the validity of the generalized second law of thermodynamics. The study finally concludes that the interacting viscous generalized QCD ghost dark energy model in reconstructed $f(G)$ gravity provides a viable and thermodynamically consistent framework for explaining the late-time accelerated expansion of the universe.

### [115] [Weyl gauge symmetry at LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13146)

Method: 研究者首先分析了Weyl二次引力理论在Weyl几何中的引力波偏振模式，然后将所得结果与最新实验数据进行比较。研究展示了黎曼几何中的测地偏离方程如何转换到Weyl几何，并论证了为何必须在德西特（de Sitter）背景（Weyl二次引力的正确低能极限）下进行分析，以避免改变引力波内容，再计算偏振模式。

Result: 除了爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用预言的两种横向无迹（transverse-traceless）张量模式外，研究还发现了由Weyl规范场横向涨落诱导的两种额外矢量模式（vector modes）。

Abstract: With current advances in gravitational wave (GW) detection made by the worldwide LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) network of detectors, ever-more sensitive tests of gravity in the strong-field regime are now possible. This enables one to test gauge theories beyond Einstein-Hilbert action, such as Weyl gauge theories of gravity. The only anomaly-free (quantum) gauge theory of a space-time symmetry beyond Poincaré is based on Weyl gauge group (of dilatations and Poincaré symmetry) with Weyl conformal geometry as its natural underlying geometry. This gauge theory has spontaneous breaking of Weyl gauge symmetry to Einstein-Hilbert and Proca actions, plus a positive cosmological constant. We investigate the GW polarisation modes of Weyl (quadratic) gauge theory of gravity in Weyl geometry and compare our findings to the most recent experimental data. We show how the geodesic deviation equation from Riemannian geometry translates to Weyl geometry, and explain why it is crucial to perform the analysis around de Sitter background, which is the correct low-energy limit of Weyl quadratic gravity, to not alter the GW content, and then compute the polarisation modes. In addition to the two transverse-traceless tensor modes predicted by Einstein-Hilbert action, we find two additional vector modes induced by the transverse fluctuations of the Weyl gauge field. If detected, these vectors modes would be important evidence for Weyl gauge symmetry.

### [116] [Modeling non-stationary noise: applications in gravitational wave astronomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13168)
*Neil J. Cornish*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对引力波数据中测量噪声的非平稳（non-stationary）和非高斯（non-Gaussian）特性，提出了一种基于动态功率谱 $S(f,t)$ 的通用建模框架。该框架通过 Gram 因子模型（Gram-factor model）构造正半定（positive semi-definite）噪声协方差矩阵，推广了传统的平稳功率谱 $S(f)$，并给出了离散傅里叶表示和小波表示下的闭式解，适用于多种非平稳噪声场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实引力波数据中的测量噪声既不满足平稳性（stationarity）也不满足高斯性（Gaussianity），而现有方法难以对非平稳噪声进行可解释的建模。因此，需要一种通用的、易于解释的框架来刻画噪声的时变统计特性。

Method: 提出一种基于动态功率谱 $S(f,t)$ 的通用建模框架，通过 Gram 因子模型构造噪声协方差矩阵，确保其正半定性。该动态谱可描述噪声协方差在频域、时域及时频小波域（wavelet domain）中的性质，并给出了离散傅里叶表示（discrete Fourier representation）和离散 Wilson-Daubechies 小波表示下的闭式表达，两者均以 Gram 矩阵（Gramian matrix）形式给出。

Result: 给出了非平稳噪声协方差矩阵在离散傅里叶基和小波基下的闭式 Gram 矩阵表达式，并提供了多种非平稳性示例，包括窗函数（window functions）引起的非平稳性、空间探测器对银河双星信号（galactic binary signals）的调制响应，以及其他更一般的非平稳类型。

Conclusion: 该框架为引力波数据处理中非平稳噪声的建模提供了一种通用且可解释的数学形式，能够灵活适用于不同的数据表示基，为后续的噪声抑制与信号检测奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: In an ideal world, the measurement noise in gravitational wave data would be stationary and Gaussian. In reality, neither of these conditions holds. Here a general framework is introduced that can be used to model non-stationary noise in an easily interpretable way, using a dynamic power spectrum $S(f,t)$. The construction is a Gram-factor model for the noise covariance matrix that is positive semi-definite by construction. This construction generalizes the familiar stationary power spectrum $S(f)$. The dynamic spectrum encodes the properties of the noise covariance matrix in any basis, including the frequency domain, time domain, and time-frequency wavelet domain. Closed form expressions are given for discrete Fourier representations of the data, and for discrete Wilson-Daubechies wavelet representations of the data. Both take the form of Gramian matrices. Examples are provided, including the non-stationarity caused by window functions, the modulated response to galactic binary signals for space-based detectors, and other, more general types of non-stationarity.

### [117] [Precision Ringdown Measurements of Binary Black Hole Remnants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13275)
*Achal Kumar,Poulami Dutta Roy,Marek J. Szczepańczyk,Sergey Klimenko*

Method: 采用相干波暴（cWB）方法重构引力波信号，通过降低重构噪声并结合改进的铃宕分析（在更早、更接近并合的时刻探测残骸黑洞性质），提高了对主导模 $(l,m)=(2,2)$ 的频率和阻尼时间的约束精度。

Result: 对第三次引力波瞬变目录（GWTC-3）中所有公开的双黑洞事件进行分析，发现各事件的主导模频率与阻尼时间均与广义相对论预测一致。联合分析给出频率的分数偏差 $δf_{220}=0.003_{-0.028}^{+0.028}$，阻尼时间的分数偏差 $δτ_{220}=0.050_{-0.086}^{+0.081}$，均在不确定性范围内与零一致。

Conclusion: 基于cWB重构的铃宕分析方法相比先前测量获得了更紧的约束，所有分析结果均支持广义相对论的预言，未发现偏离证据。

Abstract: The ringdown gravitational wave from a binary black hole (BBH) merger is a superposition of quasi-normal modes (QNMs) of the remnant black hole. In general relativity (GR), QNMs are damped harmonic oscillations with frequencies and damping times uniquely determined by the remnant's mass and spin. The measurement of the ringdown modes and performing black hole spectroscopy provides a tool to test the validity of GR. We present a ringdown analysis based on reconstruction of GW signals with coherent WaveBurst (cWB). This method yields tighter constraints on the QNM frequency and damping time than previous measurements. The improved precision results from the noise reduction achieved by the cWB reconstruction and the enhanced ringdown analysis, which probes the remnant properties at earlier times, closer to the merger. We have analyzed publicly available binary black hole (BBH) detections from the third Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC-3). For all events considered, the measured frequency and damping time of the dominant $(l,m)=(2,2)$ mode are found to be consistent with the predictions of GR. A combined analysis further strengthens these constraints, yielding fractional deviations in frequency $δf_{220} = 0.003_{-0.028}^{+0.028}$ and damping time $δτ_{220} = 0.050_{-0.086}^{+0.081}$, consistent with zero within the quoted uncertainties.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 聚焦于横向各向同性标量模式，采用零响应通道（NRC）——一种特定的干涉组合设计——来抑制其他极化模式的贡献。构建了分析性动态轨道模型以真实模拟三角形星座，计算了各干涉通道的响应函数和灵敏度曲线，并与标准迈克尔逊（Michelson）通道进行了比较。

Conclusion: NRC将作为未来空间引力波任务中探测引力理论的关键工具，为检验GQFT等非GR理论提供有价值的实验途径。

Abstract: Space-based gravitational-wave (GW) detectors, including LISA and Taiji, offer unprecedented access to regimes where alternative theories of gravity may deviate from General Relativity (GR). Gravitational Quantum Field Theory (GQFT) provides a novel framework in which the Poincaré-type inhomogeneous spin symmetry of Weyl-type fermions in the Standard Model is elevated to a gauge symmetry. Within this construction, the fundamental gravitational field is identified with a gravigauge field which behaves as a Goldstone-type bi-covariant vector field. Unlike GR, GQFT predicts additional polarization states: one transverse scalar (breathing) mode and two vector modes. In this work, we focus on the transverse, isotropic scalar mode and investigate its detectability with Taiji. To isolate this mode, we employ the null-response channel (NRC), a specific interferometric combination designed to suppress contributions from other polarizations. We implement an analytical, dynamic orbital model to realistically simulate a triangular constellation. We compute the response functions and sensitivity curves for various interferometric channels, compare them with the standard Michelson channel, and demonstrate the effectiveness of the NRC approach. Our results show that the NRC provides a reliable, waveform-independent criterion for testing non-GR polarizations, and we anticipate that it will serve as a valuable tool for probing gravitational theories in future space-based GW missions.

### [119] [Solid-state gravitational-wave detectors at GHz frequencies: the search for the primordial stochastic GW background and light primordial black hole binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13741)
*Juan Garcia-Bellido*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于超纯蓝宝石单晶模块化阵列的GHz频段固态探测器，用于探测暴胀后 reheating 产生的随机引力波背景以及轻质量原初黑洞双星并合事件，并对比了两类目标的最优探测策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暴胀后 reheating 产生的随机引力波背景（SGWB）峰值在GHz频段，但现有基于逆Gertsenshtein效应的实验仅达MHz频段；同时，轻质量原初黑洞（PBH）双星并合也在MHz-GHz范围，现有的探测手段无法覆盖这一频率窗口。

Method: 采用模块化阵列设计，包含约10³块超纯蓝宝石（sapphire）单晶（每块(10 cm)³），构成约1立方米的探测器，通过低温单声子传感器（cryogenic single-phonon sensors）读出；阵列分段设计提供热隔离、良好计数统计和符合定时的本底抑制；并对比了蓝宝石与钻石等候选材料。

Result: 钻石单位体积性能更优，但受限于无法获得大尺寸单晶；稳态背景（SGWB）为散粒噪声限制下的计数问题，适合窄带共振增强长积分探测；瞬态啁啾信号（PBH并合）适合快速宽带搜索加符合定时标记。

Conclusion: 模块化固态阵列可利用声子谱连续性，通过交错排列共振单元覆盖探测频段并保留宽带子集进行啁啾跟踪，从而同时服务于两类科学目标。

Abstract: Reheating after inflation is one of the strongest sources of gravitational waves (GW), producing a stochastic background (SGWB) with a non-thermal spectrum peaked at frequencies of order a few GHz. Detecting it is difficult: experiments based on the inverse Gertsenshtein effect in intense magnetic fields reach the MHz but not the GHz band, where the typical strain is around $10^{-30}$. The same window contains the coalescence of light primordial black hole (PBH) binaries, whose merger frequency $f\simeq4.4\ \mathrm{kHz}\,(M_\odot/M)$ falls in the MHz--GHz range for planetary to sub-planetary masses; since such objects are necessarily sub-solar, their detection would be strong evidence for PBHs as a component of the dark matter. We propose a solid-state detector at GHz frequencies that could integrate over months to years the GW continuously arriving from the Big Bang and search for light PBH binary coalescence. As a concrete realization we consider a modular array of $\sim10^3$ ultra-pure sapphire $(10\ \mathrm{cm})^3$ monocrystals forming a cubic-metre detector read out by cryogenic single-phonon sensors, whose segmentation provides thermal isolation, favourable counting statistics and coincidence-based background rejection. We also compare candidate materials, finding diamond superior per unit volume but limited by the unavailability of large single crystals. Finally, we contrast the two targets. The stationary background is a shot-noise-limited counting problem, best served by a narrow, resonance-enhanced, long-integration search; the loud transient chirp of a nearby merger is better caught by a fast, broad-band search with coincidence tagging. Because the phonon spectrum is continuous, a modular solid-state array can serve both, by staggering resonant cells across the band while running a broad-band subset for chirp tracking.

### [120] [DARK-HIDE: Dark matter versus hidden dimensions in black hole images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13992)
*Mohsen Fathi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了黑洞附近暗物质（dark matter）与有效额外维修正（effective extra-dimensional corrections）对相同视界尺度可观测量的影响，发现两者存在简并性（degeneracy）。通过DARK-HIDE框架对比旋转暗物质度规与旋转膜世界度规（braneworld metric），表明仅靠现有EHT阴影尺寸（shadow-size）约束无法区分二者，但局部光子输运（local photon transport）保留了额外的强场信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 如果黑洞图像偏离克尔度规（Kerr metric），无法直接判断其原因是暗物质还是额外维修正，因此需要系统研究这两种物理来源的简并性问题。

Method: 采用DARK-HIDE框架：暗物质分支用带径向质量函数（radial mass function）的旋转度规描述，隐藏维分支用具有非电磁潮汐荷（non-electromagnetic tidal charge）的旋转膜世界度规描述。对比光子区域（photon regions）、临界曲线（critical curves）、图像形态、基于EHT结果的阴影尺寸似然以及局部ZAMO逃逸锥（ZAMO escape cones）。

Result: 强负潮汐荷易于与克尔及两种基准暗物质轮廓区分；但连续调节潮汐荷后可模拟暗物质的临界曲线和图像代理（image proxy），形成简并。在ε/M=0.025时，Einasto和cored cNFW轮廓的最佳P+I模拟分别对应q/M²=-0.01917和-0.01117，标准化分离度分别为0.084和0.051。射线束焦散测试（ray-bundle caustic test）因未通过收敛性和拓扑检查而被排除。当前EHT阴影尺寸约束下，暗物质振幅先验占主导，仅轻微抑制大负潮汐荷，且与q=0完全兼容。局部逃逸锥在匹配分支间保留了小而平滑、可分辨的差异。

Conclusion: 仅凭现有阴影尺寸约束无法打破暗物质与额外维修正之间的简并（DARK-HIDE degeneracy），但局部光子输运包含了额外的强场信息，有望在未来进一步区分二者。

Abstract: Dark matter near a black hole and effective extra-dimensional corrections can change the same horizon-scale observables. This creates a simple but important question: if an image differs from Kerr, what caused the difference? We study this problem with DARK-HIDE. The dark-matter branch is described by rotating metrics with radial mass functions, while the hidden-dimensional branch is a rotating braneworld metric with a non-electromagnetic tidal charge. We compare photon regions, critical curves, controlled image morphology, a shadow-size likelihood calibrated to EHT results, and local ZAMO escape cones. A strong negative tidal charge is easy to separate from Kerr and from the two benchmark dark-matter profiles. The difficult case appears after the tidal charge is continuously adjusted to mimic the dark-matter critical curve and image proxy. At $\varepsilon/M=0.025$, the best $P+I$ mimics occur at $q/M^2=-0.01917$ for Einasto and $-0.01117$ for cored cNFW, with small standardized separations of $0.084$ and $0.051$. A ray-bundle caustic test does not pass the required convergence and topology checks, so it is excluded from inference. After marginalizing over spin and isotropic inclination, current EHT shadow-size constraints leave both dark-matter amplitudes prior dominated. They mildly suppress large negative tidal charge, but remain fully compatible with $q=0$. Local escape cones retain a small, smooth, and well-resolved difference between the matched branches. Thus, present shadow size alone cannot break the DARK-HIDE degeneracy, while local photon transport keeps additional strong-field information.

### [121] [Acoustic Firewalls: Analogue Gravity Perspective on the AMPS Paradox](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14056)
*Nikolay S. Akintsov,Artyom P. Nevecheria,Stepan N. Andreev,Qing-Hua Qin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文将AMPS的黑洞防火墙（firewall）论证转录至模拟声学视界（sonic horizon）中的霍金式声子辐射，利用精确纯态恒等式证明后佩奇时间（post-Page-time）幺正性迫使出射声子与其内部伙伴粒子之间的纠缠消失，从而定义了声学防火墙（acoustic firewall）；其重整化应力张量在近视界区携带负通量，且热大气能量密度呈(δr)^{-2}发散，并在愈合长度处截断。该构造是运动学性的，不解决信息悖论，但给出了一个可证伪的微分声子量热信号预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于将AMSP提出的量子纠缠单配性（monogamy of entanglement）在黑洞视界处导致防火墙的论证，转至可实验模拟的声学黑洞系统，以检验类似效应是否存在于模拟引力体系中的霍金式声子辐射。

Method: 通过将AMPS论证转录至Unruh声学度规（Unruh acoustic metric）中的声子霍金辐射，利用精确纯态恒等式（exact purity identity）分析后佩奇时间幺正性对纠缠结构的约束，并计算重整化应力张量（renormalized stress tensor）与近视界能量密度标度律。

Result: 后佩奇时间幺正性强迫出射声子与其内部伙伴粒子的纠缠消失，导致非哈达玛德（non-Hadamard）的Boulware类声子态，即声学防火墙；其重整化应力张量与光滑态相差一个负的常数近视界通量，静态量热计测得的移除热大气能量密度呈(δr)^{-2}发散（自由下落系中奇异），在愈合长度处截断；得到可证伪预言：微分声子量热信号$\mathcal{R}(δr)=|Δ\mathcal{E}|/\mathcal{E}^{(0)}\to(\ell_κ/δr)^{2}$仅在类比佩奇时间后出现于玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）中。

Conclusion: 该构造是运动学性（kinematic）的，并未解决信息悖论（information paradox），但提供了一个具体且可证伪的实验预言——近视界微分声子量热信号随距离平方反比增长，可在BEC系统中通过模拟佩奇时间前后的比较加以检验。

Abstract: The monogamy of quantum entanglement, applied by Almheiri-Marolf-Polchinski-Sully (AMPS) to black holes, obstructs a smooth horizon vacuum after the Page time. We transcribe this argument to Hawking-like phonon radiation from a sonic horizon in the Unruh acoustic metric. An exact purity identity shows that post-Page-time unitarity forces the entanglement between an outgoing phonon and its interior partner to vanish, selecting a non-Hadamard (Boulware-like) phonon state, which we define as an acoustic firewall. Its renormalized stress tensor differs from the smooth state by a constant, negative near-horizon flux, and the thermal-atmosphere energy density it removes, measured by a static calorimeter, grows as $(δr)^{-2}$ in the radial coordinate toward the horizon (singular in the free-fall frame), cut off at the healing length. The construction is kinematic and does not resolve the information paradox; it yields one concrete, falsifiable prediction: a differential phonon-calorimetry signal $\mathcal{R}(δr)=|Δ\mathcal{E}|/\mathcal{E}^{(0)}\to(\ell_κ/δr)^{2}$, present only after the analogue Page time in a Bose-Einstein condensate.

</details>


### [122] [Entropy release from Minkowski breaking in regular Schwarzschild black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14079)
*Francisco S. N. Lobo,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发现，从正则非奇异构型经典形成Schwarzschild黑洞在广义相对论中是不可能的（Minkowski破缺），该转变必须是离散的量子事件。通过分析带de Sitter核心的正则Schwarzschild黑洞族，揭示了内Killing视界携带形式上的Bekenstein-Hawking熵，该熵在坍缩参数n→0时通过量子过程释放，导致Schwarzschild黑洞作为基态的量子化熵谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近Ovalle等人证明，在广义相对论框架下，从正则非奇异构型经典形成Schwarzschild黑洞是不可能的——几何会在原点处不可避免地产生不连续性，这一现象被称为Minkowski破缺（Minkowski breaking）。这一障碍表明，向Schwarzschild点质量的转变必然是一个离散的量子事件。本文旨在揭示这一转变的热力学印记。

Method: 采用带de Sitter核心（de Sitter core）的正则Schwarzschild黑洞（regular Schwarzschild black hole）显式族作为研究对象。通过分析内Killing视界（inner Killing horizon）的熵性质，并引入坍缩参数n来参数化黑洞族，研究熵随参数变化的行为以及内视界消失时的热力学特征。

Result: 内Killing视界携带形式上的Bekenstein-Hawking熵$S_{\rm inner} = A_{\rm inner}/4$，该熵在奇异Schwarzschild态中不存在。随着坍缩参数n减小，内视界收缩，熵在经典演化过程中逐步释放；当n=0时视界消失，发生Minkowski破缺。n→0⁺时表面引力发散，半经典描述在n~1/ln(h/ℓ_P)处失效。对于n=3的正则黑洞，储存熵约为A/4的59%；在半经典极限n≫1下趋近完整的A/4。n的整数性质意味着量子化的熵谱，Schwarzschild黑洞对应OCK族中的基态。

Conclusion: 假设广义第二定律（generalized second law），内视界消失时储存的熵必须被释放。经典的质量膨胀不稳定性（mass-inflation instability）可能通过柯西视界（Cauchy horizon）的量子消失而避免。该工作厘清了坍缩过程中连续性与离散性的本质，揭示了从正则黑洞到奇异Schwarzschild态的量子跃迁及其热力学特征。

Abstract: The classical formation of a Schwarzschild black hole from a regular, non-singular configuration has recently been shown to be impossible within general relativity: the geometry inevitably develops a discontinuity at the origin, a phenomenon termed Minkowski breaking by Ovalle, Casadio, and Kamenshchik [PRD 113 (2026), 064042]. This obstruction signals that the transition to the Schwarzschild point mass must be a discrete, quantum event. We uncover the thermodynamic footprint of this transition. Using the explicit family of regular Schwarzschild black holes with a de Sitter core, we show that the inner Killing horizon carries a formal Bekenstein-Hawking entropy $S_{\rm inner} = A_{\rm inner}/4$ that is absent in the singular Schwarzschild state. This entropy is hidden from external observers in equilibrium but, assuming the generalized second law, must be released when the inner horizon disappears. As the collapse parameter $n$ decreases, the inner horizon shrinks and its entropy is gradually released during classical evolution, until the horizon finally vanishes at $n=0$ with the Minkowski breaking. The surface gravity diverges as $n\to0^+$, with the semiclassical description breaking down at $n \sim 1/\ln(h/\ell_P)$; the final disappearance is therefore a deep quantum process. For the $n=3$ regular black hole, the stored entropy is approximately $59\%$ of $A/4$; in the semiclassical limit $n\gg1$, it approaches the full $A/4$. The integer nature of $n$ implies a quantized entropy spectrum, with the Schwarzschild black hole as the ground state within the OCK family. We discuss how the classical mass-inflation instability may be circumvented by the quantum disappearance of the Cauchy horizon, and clarify the continuous vs. discrete nature of the collapse.

</details>

### [123] [Mono-Z Dark Matter Search with Neural Spline Flows Using CMS Run 2015D Open Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13771)
*Hitesh Rasineni,Bhavishya Chebrolu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 利用CMS Run 2015D公开数据（积分亮度2.32 fb⁻¹）和简化模型蒙特卡罗模拟，首次将神经样条流（Neural Spline Flow）似然比评分方法应用于mono-Z暗物质搜索。通过37维运动学特征向量和双通道（μμ与ee）联合剖面似然拟合，在95%置信水平上给出了标量、矢量、轴矢量中介子的信号强度上限。观测上限弱于预期，归因于高MET区域的背景建模残差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质（dark matter, DM）与普通物质间的弱相互作用使得直接探测困难，需要利用高能对撞机（collider）通过暗物质伴随标准模型辐射产生的单喷注/单Z等末态进行间接搜索。本文旨在利用CMS公开数据和基于神经样条流的似然比方法来提高mono-Z末态暗物质搜索的灵敏度。

Method: 采用CMS Run 2015D公开数据（2.32 fb⁻¹）和简化模型蒙特卡罗模拟，选取mono-Z→ℓ⁺ℓ⁻末态（μμ和ee通道）。从MINIAOD和MINIAODSIM中提取40个运动学观测量（kinematic observables），经物理解理清洗后降为37维特征向量。训练五个神经样条流（Neural Spline Flow）分别建模标准模型（Standard Model）背景和不同中介子（mediator）的暗物质信号密度。基于信号与背景密度估计的对数似然比（log-likelihood ratio）构建逐事件检验统计量，避免硬MET阈值。采用双通道联合剖面似然拟合（profile-likelihood fit）提取上限。

Result: 在95%置信水平上，标量中介子的信号强度参数（signal-strength parameter）观测（预期）上限为μ<0.0177（0.0018）；矢量中介子为μ<0.0362（0.0039）；轴矢量中介子为μ<0.0498（0.0069）。观测上限弱于预期，原因是高MET区域的背景建模残差，而非暗物质信号证据。

Conclusion: 本研究是首次将神经样条流似然比评分方法应用于CMS Run 2015D公开数据mono-Z暗物质搜索，并同时联合μμ和ee两个通道。结果表明该方法能够利用全运动学相空间（full kinematic phase space）信息而无需硬MET截断，但高MET区域的背景建模仍需改进。未发现暗物质存在的证据。

Abstract: We report a search for dark matter (DM) produced in association with a leptonically decaying \(Z\) boson at \(\sqrt{s}=13\) TeV using CMS Run 2015D open data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of \(2.32\,\mathrm{fb}^{-1}\) together with simplified-model Monte Carlo simulation. Events are selected in the mono-\(Z\rightarrow\ell^+\ell^-\) final state in both the \(μμ\) and \(ee\) channels. Forty kinematic observables are extracted from MINIAOD and MINIAODSIM, cleaned with physics-motivated selections, and reduced to a 37-dimensional feature vector. Five Neural Spline Flows are trained independently to model Standard Model background and mediator-specific DM signal densities. The per-event test statistic is constructed from the log-likelihood ratio between the signal and background density estimates, providing sensitivity across the full kinematic phase space without requiring a hard upper \(\mathrm{MET}\) threshold. A simultaneous profile-likelihood fit combining the two channels yields observed (expected) 95\% confidence level upper limits on the signal-strength parameter of \(μ<0.0177\) (\(0.0018\)) for the scalar mediator, \(μ<0.0362\) (\(0.0039\)) for the vector mediator, and \(μ<0.0498\) (\(0.0069\)) for the axial-vector mediator. The observed limits are weaker than expected because of a residual high-\(\mathrm{MET}\) background-modeling discrepancy rather than evidence for a DM signal. To our knowledge, this is the first application of Neural Spline Flow likelihood-ratio scoring to a mono-\(Z\) dark matter search using CMS Run 2015D open data simultaneously in the \(μμ\) and \(ee\) channels.

### [124] [Microstructure-Conditioned Surrogate Models for Graded Multiscale Optimization of Mycelium Composites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13688)
*J. Storm,I. B. C. M. Rocha,S. Schyck,K. Masania,F. P. van der Meer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于超网络（hypernetwork）的条件替代模型（conditioned surrogate model），通过将混合物理-数据替代模型（hybrid physics-data surrogate）条件化于微观结构变量，在少量训练数据下实现了对菌丝-木屑复合材料（mycelium-woodchip composite material）多尺度力学行为（multiscale mechanical behavior）的准确预测，并进一步将网络条件化于制造变量（manufacturing variables），为可持续材料的多尺度优化（multiscale optimization）提供了实用路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 新兴可持续材料依赖于工程化的层级结构（engineered hierarchy）与微观结构（microstructure）来控制其性质与力学行为。高效的多尺度模拟需要对微观尺度的数据驱动替代模型（data-driven surrogate models）进行训练，但固定微观结构已需要大量数据；当考虑多种微观结构（如多尺度优化场景）时，数据需求进一步激增，成为关键瓶颈。

Method: 采用超网络（hypernetwork）将混合物理-数据替代模型（hybrid physics-data surrogate）条件化于微观结构变量（microstructural variables）。该方法允许替代模型在不同微观结构间泛化，无需为每种微观结构单独生成大量训练数据。进一步，该方法被扩展为将网络直接条件化于制造变量（manufacturing variables）。

Result: 在小数据集训练下，该条件替代模型可准确预测菌丝-木屑复合材料的多尺度力学行为，使功能梯度结构（functionally graded structures）的多尺度模拟变得可行，并与完整的FE²模拟进行了验证。优化后的梯度多尺度圆盘（graded multiscale disk）相较于随机微观结构圆盘，峰值应力降低了42%。

Conclusion: 条件替代模型（conditioned surrogate models）能够有效实现微观结构工程化材料的可追溯多尺度优化，并可通过直接条件化制造变量来调控微观结构以获得期望的宏观行为（macroscale behavior）。该工作加速了未来可持续材料与结构的设计与开发。

Abstract: Emerging sustainable materials increasingly rely on engineered hierarchy and microstructure to achieve control of their properties and mechanical behavior. Optimizing these materials with controllable microstructures requires efficient multiscale simulations. Data-driven surrogate models for the microscale can accelerate multiscale simulations, but require large amounts of data even for a fixed microstructure. When a range of microstructures is considered, as is the case in multiscale optimization, even more data is needed to train a surrogate. To overcome this challenge, we condition a hybrid physics-data surrogate on microstructural variables using a hypernetwork. This approach enables accurate predictions of multiscale mechanical behavior for a mycelium-woodchip composite material, even when trained on small datasets. The conditioned surrogate makes multiscale simulations of functionally graded structures tractable, and we validate it against a full FE^2 simulation. We optimize a graded multiscale disk, and reduce the peak stress by 42% compared to one with a random microstructure. Then, we go one step further, conditioning the network directly on manufacturing variables that can have a complex influence on the microstructure. This is a practical route to engineer the microscale for desired macroscale behavior. This contribution highlights the benefits of microarchitectured structures and demonstrates how conditioned surrogate models enable their multiscale optimization, which will accelerate the development and design of future sustainable materials and structures.

</details>

### [125] [Condition for $1/f$ noise to occur along with an example for a diffusion equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13856)
*H. Mouri*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过解析扩散方程发现了一个1/f噪声的新实例，并结合流体湍流中标度行为的已有知识，提出了任意稳态1/f噪声出现的一个充要条件：该噪声须由两个恒定频率flow≪fhigh刻画，且在flow到fhigh的频率范围内，除噪声的平均振幅外无其他恒定参数，从而在flow≪f≪fhigh区间渐近表现为1/f标度。该条件具有统计性和简单性，适用于任意系统，因此解释了1/f噪声的普遍性；对于1/f^α（α≠1.0）的噪声，也可通过类似湍流的间歇性机制加以推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 1/f噪声（1/f noise）虽在多种系统中普遍存在，但其背后的物理机制仍不明确。本文旨在从扩散方程的解析研究中寻找新的1/f噪声实例，并提炼出该噪声出现的普适条件。

Method: 对普通扩散方程（ordinary diffusion equation）进行解析研究，得到一个1/f噪声的新实例；然后将该实例的解析表达式与流体湍流（fluid turbulence）中已知的标度行为（scaling）相结合，推导出稳态1/f噪声出现的充要条件。

Result: 发现稳态1/f噪声出现的充要条件是：噪声需由两个恒定频率flow≪fhigh刻画，且在flow至fhigh的频率范围内，除噪声的平均振幅外不存在其他恒定参数。在此条件下，当flow≪f≪fhigh时，噪声渐近地遵循1/f标度。该条件具有统计性（statistical）和简单性（simple），适用于任意系统。此外，该条件还可通过类似湍流间歇性（intermittency）的机制推广到1/f^α（α≠1.0）的噪声。

Conclusion: 所提出的充要条件因其统计性和简单性而适用于任何系统，从而解释了1/f噪声的广泛存在性（ubiquity）。同时，该框架也为理解α≠1.0的1/f^α噪声提供了推广路径。

Abstract: While $1/f$ noise is ubiquitous and has been found in various systems, its physics remains uncertain. From an analytical study of an ordinary diffusion equation, we find an additional example of the $1/f$ noise. The formula for this example, together with existing knowledge about scaling in fluid turbulence, implies a necessary and sufficient condition for the occurrence of any stationary $1/f$ noise. That is, the noise needs to be characterized by two constant frequencies of $f_{\rm low} \ll f_{\rm high}$. For a frequency range from $f = f_{\rm low}$ to $f_{\rm high}$, it is further needed that, except for the mean amplitude of the noise, there is no other constant parameter. Then, at $f_{\rm low} \ll f \ll f_{\rm high}$, the noise scales asymptotically as $1/f$. Being statistical and simple, our condition applies to any system and hence explains the ubiquity of the $1/f$ noise. It is also applicable to some systems with noise of $α\ne 1.0$ for $1/f^α$, via intermittency analogous to that of the turbulence.

</details>


### [126] [Dynamics of a microroller under confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14053)
*Han Gao,Nan Xie,Zaiyi Shen,Xiaoping Hu,Shiyuan Hu,Ye Xu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过实验、数值模拟和标度分析，研究了受限微通道中微滚轮（microroller）的动力学行为，发现其平移速度在收缩通道中下降并在窄通道中发生速度反转，揭示了远场旋子流（rotlet flow）产生的粘性应力主导速度变化，而近场剪切流（shear flow）的平移阻力抑制运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旋转粒子在表面附近会发生平动，形成具有广泛生物医学和微流控应用潜力的微滚轮。然而，在受限微通道中微滚轮的动力学行为尚不清晰，需要系统研究其在不同几何形状通道中的运动规律和物理机制。

Method: 采用实验、数值模拟和标度分析（scaling analysis）相结合的方法，研究了微滚轮在不同几何形状（矩形、圆柱形及收缩形）受限微通道中的动力学行为。基于自由平移的无净力条件（force-free condition），建立了一个可推广至不同通道几何形状的系统性标度框架。

Result: 在收缩通道中，微滚轮的平移速度随其接近收缩区域而下降。在矩形和圆柱形通道中，随特征通道宽度减小，均出现速度反转（velocity reversal）现象。所建立的标度分析给出了平移速度对受限程度（degree of confinement）的函数依赖关系，与实验和数值模拟结果吻合良好。远场旋子流产生的粘性应力（viscous stress）决定了速度的降低和反转，而近场剪切流导致的平移阻力（translational resistance）在强受限条件下抑制了平动。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了远场旋子流和近场剪切流在微滚轮受限动力学中的不同作用，为在受限流体环境中控制微滚轮动力学提供了实用指导。

Abstract: Rotating particles can translate when placed near a surface, forming microrollers with a wide range of biomedical and microfluidic applications. In this work, we investigate the dynamics of microrollers in confined microchannels with different geometries by combining experiments, numerical simulations, and scaling analysis. In constricted channels, we find that the translational velocity of a microroller decreases as it approaches the constricted region. In both rectangular and cylindrical channels, velocity reversal occurs as the characteristic channel width decreases. Using the force-free condition for free translation, we develop a systematic scaling framework that can be generalized to different channel geometries. The scaling analysis yields functional dependences of the translational velocity on the degree of confinement, which agree well with both experiments and simulations. Importantly, we demonstrate that the viscous stress generated by the far-field rotlet flow governs the observed velocity reduction and reversal, while the translational resistance resulting from the near-field shear flow suppresses translation under tight confinement. The distinct roles of these flow components revealed by our analysis may provide practical guidance for controlling microroller dynamics in confined fluid environments.

</details>

### [127] [Three-Dimensional Non-Foliated Fractional Quantum Hall Phases with Irrational Anyons in Twisted van der Waals Multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13127)
*Seyoung Jin,Hyeonseo Lim,Youngwook Kim,Gil Young Cho*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过大角度扭曲范德华多层结构在三维体系中实现了非叶状分数量子霍尔效应，获得了具有非理性编织统计和指数级拓扑简并度的拓扑序，为三维分数量子霍尔物质提供了可行的材料平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维分数量子霍尔相能够展现非叶状（non-foliated）的强拓扑序、指数级拓扑简并度和具有非理性编织统计（braiding statistics）的准粒子，但其微观实现因三维朗道量子化（Landau quantization）通常产生一维色散带而困难重重。

Method: 采用大角度扭曲的范德华多层结构（twisted van der Waals multilayers），利用大扭转角通过动量失配抑制相干层间隧穿，同时保持原子级层间距下强的层间库仑相互作用；并通过蒙特卡洛计算比较862个竞争试波函数的能量。

Result: 广义Halperin态在多个连续层间实现量子相干，在实验可达的磁场区间取代传统非扭曲类石墨多层中的金属性自发层间相干相；这些液体实现了与分形子拓扑序（fractonic topological order）密切相关的非叶状分数量子霍尔序，具有理性电荷但非理性编织统计的准粒子。

Conclusion: 大角度扭曲范德华多层结构为超越传统二维量子霍尔体系的三维分数量子霍尔物质提供了现实可行的材料平台，其大拓扑简并度和非理性统计相位可能为量子信息存储与处理提供非传统资源。

Abstract: Three-dimensional fractional quantum Hall phases offer a route to intrinsically higher-dimensional topological order beyond simple stacks of two-dimensional quantum Hall liquids. Such phases can exhibit non-foliated, intrinsically three-dimensional entanglement structures, exponentially large topological degeneracies and quasiparticles with irrational braiding statistics. Their microscopic realization has remained elusive because Landau quantization in three dimensions generally leaves dispersive one-dimensional bands, favoring metallic and density-wave states over incompressible fractional liquids. Here we show that large-angle twisted van der Waals multilayers provide a practical route around this obstruction. Large twist angles suppress coherent interlayer tunneling through momentum mismatch, while the atomic-scale layer separation preserves strong interlayer Coulomb interactions. Using Monte Carlo calculations to compare the energies of an extensive set of 862 competing trial wavefunctions, we find that generalized Halperin states with quantum coherence extending across multiple consecutive layers are stabilized. In experimentally accessible magnetic-field regimes, these states replace the metallic spontaneous-interlayer-coherent phases that dominate conventional untwisted graphite-like multilayers. The resulting liquids realize non-foliated fractional quantum Hall order closely related to fractonic topological order, hosting quasiparticles with rational electric charges but irrational braiding statistics. Their large topological degeneracy and non-rational statistical phases may offer unconventional resources for quantum information storage and processing. Our results establish twisted van der Waals multilayers as a realistic materials platform for three-dimensional fractional Hall matter beyond conventional two-dimensional quantum Hall systems.

</details>

Abstract: We combine first-principles density-functional theory, Berry-curvature analysis, semiclassical Boltzmann transport, and atomistic spin dynamics to establish hexagonal NiS as a compensated 3d altermagnetic semimetal in which topology, magnetism, and lattice dynamics are intrinsically intertwined. ### [131] [Hubbard-assisted stability of Hatsugai-Kohmoto correlations in a one-dimensional open chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13434)
*Yan-Xiao Wang,Yin Zhong*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过在一维自旋费米子链中同时引入Hatsugai-Kohmoto（HK）相互作用和局域哈伯德（Hubbard）排斥作用，利用精确对角化方法研究了有限局域排斥势如何修正HK物理的实空间可观测量和局域谱。结果表明，哈伯德项不会破坏HK主导的物理，反而在中等HK耦合强度下促进了更强HK行为的出现，而最近邻密度相互作用则与HK显示出竞争趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HK模型被证明是描述Mottness的不动点（fixed-point），在弱微扰下稳定。一个自然的问题是超出弱微扰区域后，有限局域排斥作用（如哈伯德相互作用）如何修正HK物理的实空间可观测量和局域谱。

Method: 作者采用严格对角化（exact diagonalization）方法，在一维开链（open chain）的半满自旋费米子链中，计算基态关联函数（correlation functions）和位点分辨的局域谱（site-resolved local spectra）。

Result: 哈伯德项不会将系统驱离HK主导的区域；在中等$U_{\rm HK}$下，有限$U_{\rm Hub}$促进了纯HK链在更大$U_{\rm HK}$下才表现出的行为特征，包括正自旋关联的发展、单粒子相干性（single-particle coherence）的抑制、杂质引起的局域谱权重重分布以及配对关联（pairing correlations）的演化。相比之下，最近邻（NN）密度相互作用与HK相互作用表现出竞争趋势，无法复现相同的强HK行为。

Conclusion: 上述结果为HK物理的不动点稳定性提供了非微扰的实空间补充，表明附加排斥相互作用的效果对其空间结构（spatial structure）高度敏感。

Abstract: The Hatsugai-Kohmoto (HK) model has recently been identified as a fixed-point description of Mottness that is stable against perturbing local interactions. This raises a natural question beyond the weak-perturbation regime: how does a finite local repulsion modify HK physics in real-space observables and local spectra? We address this question in a half-filled one-dimensional spinful fermion chain, where the HK interaction is supplemented by an onsite Hubbard repulsion. Using exact diagonalization in an open chain, we compute ground-state correlation functions and site-resolved local spectra. We find that the Hubbard term does not drive the system away from the HK-dominated regime. Instead, at moderate $U_{\rm HK}$, a finite $U_{\rm Hub}$ promotes the emergence of behavior characteristic of the pure HK chain at larger $U_{\rm HK}$. This Hubbard-assisted strong-HK response is reflected consistently in the development of positive spin correlations, the suppression of single-particle coherence, the impurity-induced redistribution of local spectral weight, and the evolution of pairing correlations. As a control perturbation, we replace the onsite Hubbard interaction by a nearest-neighbor (NN) density interaction. In contrast to the Hubbard case, the HK and NN interactions display competing tendencies and do not reproduce the same strong-HK behavior. These results provide a nonperturbative real-space complement to the fixed-point stability of HK physics and show that the effect of an additional repulsive interaction depends sensitively on its spatial structure.

The supersolid order develops through successive BKT transitions: the longitudinal order appears at higher temperature, while the transverse component associated with the Bose-Einstein condensate emerges only below a lower-temperature transition accompanied by a change in the interlayer correlations. At the lowest measured temperature, the transverse ordered moment reaches only 11% of the longitudinal component. Moreover, the low-energy spin fluctuations are found to be predominantly longitudinal in character. These results provide direct evidence that the supersolid ground state survives even in the near-Ising regime and exhibits longitudinal low-energy dynamics, imposing stringent constraints on microscopic theories of triangular-lattice XXZ antiferromagnets.

### [133] [Stoner transitions beyond mean-field in two-dimensional electronic systems: a diagrammatic Monte Carlo study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13675)
*Yueh-Chen Lee,Nikolay P. Prokof'ev,Andrey V. Chubukov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用图解蒙特卡洛（diagrammatic Monte Carlo）方法研究二维电子系统中超越梯形近似的斯通纳不稳定性（Stoner instability），发现单谷系统只有引入动量截断时才能在低密度下发生铁磁相变，双谷系统则存在直接或分步的斯通纳相变路径，具体由费米子色散的各向异性调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平均场（梯形）近似已充分描述了排斥相互作用费米子的斯通纳不稳定性，但该近似在低密度极限下存在对数发散的修正，因此需要超越梯形近似来更准确地理解二维电子系统中的磁性相变。

Method: 采用图解蒙特卡洛（diagrammatic Monte Carlo）算法，将梯形（ladder）与非梯形重整化（non-ladder renormalizations）置于同等地位进行处理；同时分析了粒子-粒子通道（particle-particle channel）中粒子-空穴顶角（particle-hole vertex）的重整化贡献。

Result: 单谷系统中，仅当相互作用传递的动量转移（momentum transfer）存在截断时，低密度下才会发生斯通纳铁磁相变；双谷系统中限制较弱，可能发生直接进入自旋-谷极化态（spin- and valley-polarized state）的斯通纳相变，或经由中间谷极化态（valley-polarized state）的两步斯通纳相变。

Conclusion: 超越梯形近似后，二维电子系统的斯通纳相变行为显著依赖于谷自由度数目和色散各向异性；双谷系统为调控磁性相变路径提供了更丰富的可能性。

Abstract: Stoner instabilities for fermions with repulsive interaction have been well studied within the mean-field (ladder) approximation. In this study, we consider two-dimensional electronic systems with one or two valleys and discuss a Stoner transition beyond the ladder approximation. At weak coupling, the corrections to the ladder approximation come predominantly from the renormalization of the particle-hole vertex in the particle-particle channel, and the lowest-order corrections are logarithmically singular in the low-density limit. To investigate the problem beyond the lowest order, we apply the diagrammatic Monte Carlo algorithm and treat ladder and non-ladder renormalizations on equal footing. We find that in a one-valley system, a Stoner transition to a ferromagnetism occurs at low density only if there is a cutoff on the momentum transfer carried by the interaction. In a two-valley system, the restriction is less severe. Here we find either a direct Stoner transition into a spin- and valley-polarized state, or a set of two Stoner transitions via an intermediate valley-polarized state. The pathway is controlled by the anisotropy of the fermionic dispersion.

### [134] [Magnetic quadrupole current generation and accumulation in noncentrosymmetric systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13680)
*Yuuga Takasu,Satoru Hayami*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文论证了在非中心对称反铁磁体中，磁四极矩（MQ）电流可作为实现磁化控制的有效途径，通过构建磁四极矩电导率张量的多极表示，建立了MQ电流产生的对称性条件，并在线性响应区域以点群对称性降低为例展示了MQ电流的产生，同时揭示了类似自旋霍尔效应的MQ边缘积累现象。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建磁四极矩电导率张量的多极表示（multipole representation），以此建立MQ电流产生的对称性条件；以从中心对称点群$mmm$降至其非中心对称子群$mm2$的对称性降低（symmetry lowering）为例，在线性响应（linear-response）区域内展示MQ电流的产生。

Result: 证明了MQ电流在非中心对称晶体学点群（noncentrosymmetric crystallographic point groups）中具有普适性；揭示了MQ在样品边缘的积累（edge accumulation）现象，该现象类似于自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）引起的自旋积累。

Conclusion: MQ边缘积累为MQ电流的产生提供了直接证据，并构成了在非中心对称反铁磁体中实现MQ注入及基于MQ的磁化控制的关键前提条件。

Abstract: Magnetization control via magnetic octupole injection has recently been proposed for a new class of centrosymmetric antiferromagnets, namely $d$-wave altermagnets, where the magnetic octupole is the lowest-rank magnetic multipole allowed by symmetry and serves as an alternative carrier to spin injection. In contrast, in noncentrosymmetric antiferromagnets, the magnetic quadrupole (MQ) constitutes the lowest-rank symmetry-allowed magnetic multipole, suggesting that MQ currents can provide an efficient route toward magnetization control through MQ injection. Here, we establish the symmetry conditions for MQ-current generation by constructing the multipole representation of the MQ conductivity tensor and show that MQ currents are generically allowed in noncentrosymmetric crystallographic point groups. As a representative example, we demonstrate MQ-current generation in the linear-response regime associated with symmetry lowering from the centrosymmetric point group ($mmm$) to its noncentrosymmetric subgroup ($mm2$). Furthermore, we reveal MQ accumulation near sample edges, analogous to spin accumulation induced by the spin Hall effect. This edge accumulation provides direct evidence of MQ-current generation and constitutes a key prerequisite for realizing MQ injection and MQ-based magnetization control in noncentrosymmetric antiferromagnets.

### [135] [Fractional Chern insulators in alternating twisted multilayer MoTe$_{2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13807)
*Xi-Hang Feng,Shi-Ping Ding,Xiang-Jian Hou,Ying-Hai Wu,Jin-Hua Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过滑动交替扭转三层和四层 MoTe₂ 的顶层并结合垂直电场，调控能带结构与量子几何性质。精确对角化表明，分数陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulators）的稳定性主要取决于能带的量子几何性质（由迹条件量化），而非仅由拓扑性（Chern 数）决定。滑动可作为探测莫尔（moiré）体系中多体态的有效调控手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索交替扭转三层和四层 MoTe₂ 中的强关联多体态，研究是否可以通过滑动顶层并施加垂直电场来调控能带结构和量子几何性质，从而稳定分数陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulators）。

Method: 通过在交替扭转的三层和四层 MoTe₂ 体系中滑动顶层并施加垂直电场实现多种能带结构；采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法研究不同参数区域中分数陈绝缘体的稳定性。

Result: 在某些参数区域内分数陈绝缘体得以稳定存在，而在另一些区域即使能带具有拓扑性（unity Chern number）也无法稳定。这一差异主要由能带的量子几何性质（由迹条件量化）决定。

Conclusion: 滑动可作为探测莫尔（moiré）体系中多体态的有效调控手段，量子几何性质对分数陈绝缘体的稳定性起关键作用。

Abstract: We study strongly correlated many-body states in alternating twisted trilayer and tetralayer MoTe$_{2}$. By sliding the top layer with respect to others and applying a perpendicular electric field, a variety of band structures can be realized. In many cases, the topmost hole band has unity Chern number and its quantum geometric properties can be tuned to some extent. Exact diagonalizations suggest that fractional Chern insulators are stabilized in certain parameter regimes but not in some regimes even when the band is topological. This contrast is attributed primarily to different quantum geometries as quantified by the trace condition. Our results demonstrate that sliding can serve as a useful knob for probing many-body states in moiré systems.

</details>


### [136] [Angular momentum splitter effect of $d$-wave axial phonons in orbital altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13923)
*Dimos Chatzichrysafis,Alexander Mook*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明，在不存在自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的情况下，轨道交变磁体（orbital altermagnets）中的轴向声子（axial phonons）可以承载 d 波角动量织构（d-wave angular momentum texture）。通过紧束缚模型和玻恩-奥本海默近似（Born-Oppenheimer approximation）下的分子贝里曲率（molecular Berry curvature），电子态的 d 波轨道磁矩织构被转移至声子，并预言了角动量塞贝克效应（angular-momentum Seebeck effect）和分离效应（splitter effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在无需相对论性自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的条件下，能否在轨道交变磁体（orbital altermagnets）中实现携带有限角动量的轴向声子（axial phonons），并揭示其 d 波角动量织构（d-wave angular momentum texture）的物理起源。

Method: 构建了一个最小化的电子紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），引入破坏时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）的 d 波环流序（d-wave loop-current order）；在玻恩-奥本海默近似（Born-Oppenheimer approximation）框架下，通过分子贝里曲率（molecular Berry curvature）纳入电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling），从而将电子态的 d 波轨道磁矩织构传递给声子。

Result: 证明了轴向声子可以承载 d 波角动量织构，且该转移过程不依赖相对论性自旋-轨道耦合；进一步指出该机制可实现纵向和横向角动量流，分别对应角动量塞贝克效应（angular-momentum Seebeck effect）和分离效应（splitter effect）。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了可用于工程化轴向声子的平台范围，并揭示了 d 波织构特有的功能，例如由温度梯度驱动角动量流的塞贝克与分离效应，为声子角动量输运提供了新的实验方向。

Abstract: We theoretically demonstrate that axial phonons, lattice vibration quanta carrying finite angular momentum, can host a $d$-wave angular momentum texture in orbital altermagnets in the absence of spin-orbit coupling. We consider a minimal electronic tight-binding model with $d$-wave loop-current order that breaks time-reversal symmetry. Within the Born-Oppenheimer approximation, we incorporate electron-phonon coupling via the molecular Berry curvature and show that the underlying $d$-wave orbital magnetic moment texture of the electronic state is transferred to the phonons without requiring the relativistic spin-orbit coupling. Our results expand the range of platforms available for engineering axial phonons and point to functionality unique to $d$-wave textures, including angular-momentum Seebeck and splitter effects, corresponding to longitudinal and transverse angular-momentum currents driven by a temperature gradient.

Abstract: Structural, thermodynamic and electrical transport properties of TbAuPb were investigated on single crystals. The compound was found to crystallize with the cubic MgAgAs-type structure characteristic of half-Heusler materials. It orders antiferromagnetically at TN = 5 K and undergoes a transition into a different antiferromagnetic phase emerging in high magnetic fields. Electrical transport in TbAuPb exhibits a multiband character, with a predominance of hole-like carriers. Angular magnetoresistance evolves systematically with applied magnetic field and changes its symmetry near the spin-reorientation transition, highlighting strong coupling between the charge transport and the magnetic order. The results of first-principles calculations indicate that TbAuPb is a band inverted semimetal in the non-magnetic state, which becomes topologically trivial in the field-induced ferromagnetic state.

For three-quark operators we summarize two-loop RI/SMOM matching for N=0 baryonic operators and three-loop anomalous dimensions together with two-loop matching for the N=1 Mellin moment, enabling improved lattice studies of baryon distribution amplitudes. ### [142] [Activity Regeneration from Silent States in Neuronal Networks with Transient Synaptic Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14000)
*Mozhgan Khanjanianpak,Alireza Valiadeh*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出一个具有有限寿命突触（finite-lifetime synapse）的最小神经元网络模型，揭示了在神经元完全静默后的自发活动再生机制。研究表明，首个静默状态下的残余突触构型（residual synaptic configuration）已能决定网络是否自发再生额外活动周期，并通过“潜在兴奋性招募容量”（LER）指标近乎完美地预测多周期动力学，证明瞬时突触记忆（transient synaptic memory）本身足以产生多样化的未来网络动态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管瞬时突触记忆被认为可能在无持续性神经元活动（persistent neuronal activity）的情况下维持短期信息，但隐藏的突触状态（hidden synaptic state）本身是否足以预测神经元网络在活动停止后的未来演化，仍不清楚。

Method: 构建了一个具有有限寿命突触的最小神经元网络模型，系统研究了神经元完全静默后自发活动再生的机制。通过分析首个静默状态下的残余突触构型，引入“潜在兴奋性招募容量”（Latent Excitatory Recruitment, LER）这一量化指标，定义为新鲜兴奋性神经元的累积数量。

Result: 残余突触构型已能决定网络活动是在单次活动周期后终止，还是自发再生额外周期。LER指标可作为近乎完美的预测因子，无需继续后续网络模拟即可判断多周期动力学。在原本同质的神经元网络中，仅凭瞬时突触记忆即可产生截然不同的动力学结果。

Conclusion: 研究提供了从残余突触状态解释活动再生的机制，表明短期记忆不仅编码于持续的神经元活动中，也存在于潜伏的突触构型（latent synaptic configuration）中，后者保留了网络招募新神经元装配（neuronal assembly）的能力。该快照（snapshot）框架为预测乃至控制神经元网络的未来演化提供了新视角。

Abstract: Transient synaptic memory has emerged as a potential mechanism for maintaining short-term information even in the absence of persistent neuronal activity. However, it remains unclear whether the hidden synaptic state alone contains sufficient information to predict the future evolution of neuronal networks after activity has ceased. Here, we introduce a minimal neuronal network model with finite-lifetime synapses and investigate the mechanism underlying spontaneous activity regeneration following complete neuronal silence. We show that the residual synaptic configuration at the first silent state already determines whether network activity terminates after a single activation cycle or spontaneously regenerates an additional cycle. By analyzing this synaptic-memory snapshot, we identify the Latent Excitatory Recruitment (LER) capacity, quantified by the cumulative number of fresh excitatory neurons, as a near-perfect predictor of multi-cycle dynamics without continuing the subsequent network simulation. Remarkably, these distinct dynamical outcomes emerge in an otherwise homogeneous neuronal network, demonstrating that transient synaptic memory alone is sufficient to generate diverse future dynamics. Our findings provide a mechanistic explanation for activity regeneration from a residual synaptic state and suggest that short-term memory is encoded not only in ongoing neuronal activity but also in the latent synaptic configuration that preserves the network's capacity to recruit new neuronal assemblies. More broadly, the proposed snapshot-based framework offers a new perspective for predicting and potentially controlling the future evolution of neuronal networks.

### [143] [The Origin of Multi-TeV Gamma-rays in LHAASO J0341+5258 via Cosmic Ray Illumination of Molecular Clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13991)
*Abhijit Roy,Alan Sunny,Martina Cardillo,Jagdish C. Joshi,Ritabrata Sarkar*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究利用时间依赖的强子模型（GAMERA数值包）和解析模型两种独立框架，对LHAASO探测到的超高能伽马射线源J0341+5258的起源进行建模。结果表明，TeV波段发射可被解释为从超新星遗迹逃逸的高能粒子照亮邻近分子云所致，而GeV波段发射可能源于超新星遗迹本身，从而自洽地解释了从GeV到TeV的整个伽马射线谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHAASO探测到的超高能伽马射线源LHAASO J0341+5258尚未与任何已知天体关联，其辐射起源未知。本研究旨在通过建模解释该源的超高能伽马射线发射机制。

Method: 采用两种独立框架建模：一是基于GAMERA数值包的时间依赖、源无关的强子（hadronic）模型，描述粒子在星际介质中传播并与分子气体相互作用；二是解析描述从超新星遗迹（SNR）加速的宇宙线群体与其周围分子气体的相互作用。利用已观测到的TeV伽马射线探索假想SNR的参数空间。

Result: GAMERA模型在物理合理的源-云分离距离和传播时标下，对粒子输运导致的能谱修正提供了一阶近似，并与超高能伽马射线数据拟合良好。解析框架表明，GeV发射可能源于SNR本身，而TeV发射源于从SNR逃逸的粒子照亮邻近分子云。

Conclusion: 通过时空演化的SNR-分子云相互作用场景，可自洽地解释从GeV到TeV能段的整个伽马射线谱。尽管加速源的性质仍存在不确定性，但LHAASO探测到的TeV发射可以在“照亮场景”（illumination scenario）框架下得到一致解释。

Abstract: We investigate the origin of the ultra-high-energy $γ$-ray emission detected by the Large High Altitude Air Shower Observatory (LHAASO) from the source LHAASO J0341+5258, which has not yet been associated with any known astrophysical object within the detector's field of view. The observed UHE emission is modelled within two independent frameworks: initially with a time-dependent, source-independent hadronic scenario implemented with the numerical package GAMERA, where particles propagate through the interstellar medium and subsequently interact with the molecular gas observed in the region and finally with an analytical description of the interaction between the accelerated cosmic-ray population from a supernova remnant (SNR) and the molecular gas around it. The relevant parameter space for the hypothetical past SNR is explored using the observed TeV $γ$-rays. We show that, for physically plausible source-cloud separations and propagation timescales, GAMERA provides a first-order approximation to the spectral modifications induced by particle transport and yields an adequate fit to the ultra-high-energy $γ$-ray data. Within the framework of our analytical approach, we demonstrated that the observed GeV emission can plausibly originate from the SNR itself, while the TeV emission detected by LHAASO can be consistently interpreted as arising from particles that have escaped from the SNR and are illuminating nearby molecular clouds. We invoke a spatio-temporally evolved SNR-molecular cloud interaction scenario to account self-consistently for the entire $γ$-ray spectrum from GeV to TeV energies. Despite the remaining uncertainty regarding the nature of the acceleration source, we conclude that the TeV emission detected by LHAASO can be consistently interpreted within the framework of an illumination scenario.
